### 2026-06-18 — Nano tuning pass: muted-seed recipe (fixes the cross-city artifacts) — *drop nano-styleref-sweep (cont.)*
Follow-up to the $9 sweep. The cross-city generic candidates' worst artifact was the tight-seed's **near-white road centerlines + bright-gold landmark markers** rendering as glowing schematic streaks / token icons. NEW `overnight_runner.py` **`tune`** mode + `regenerate_muted_seed()`: regenerates each city's seed with **muted streets/casing/markers** (`MUTED_STREET/CASING/LM_DIST/LM_GEN`, hue-PRESERVING) + a `_warm_neutral` **de-blue** that neutralises cool district fills Gemini paints as water (skipped for ocean Kamino via `OCEAN_CITIES`), then runs the style-ref batch — worst-first, on its own `_tune` ledger + budget, lock-serialised. Live-validated on kuat_city: the glowing white road-asterisk is gone, roads read as ground-paths (before/after at `static/tools/batches/_review/kuat_before_after.png`). Seed backup/restore is fully non-destructive — a freshly-rendered keymap (most cities ship none) is deleted on restore. Also built per-city contact sheets + a curated `_review/best/` folder (mos_eisley uses the tuned smoke plate; open/desert cities good generic; structured cities use the tuned pass). +4 tests in `tests/test_mapgen_overnight_runner.py` (`_warm_neutral`, muted constants, non-destructive keymap delete, muted seed has no near-white roads). Key ENV-only.

The one untried high-value map-automation lever (HANDOFF §3d) is now PROVEN: feeding the existing hand-made plate as a **style-reference** (2nd image in the Gemini call) pulls output to painterly + away from the tactical-grid/VTT look that sank earlier iterations. (a) NEW `tools/mapgen/style_ref_experiment.py` — reproducible harness (fixes the handoff's "the prior temp script wasn't persisted" gap): backs up → regenerates the warm-desert seed (`WARM_DESERT_HUES`, no slate-blue index-0 that Gemini paints as water; muted markers) → swaps in the nameless dual-image brief → runs the batch with the style anchor → restores in a `finally` (non-destructive). (b) NEW `tools/mapgen/overnight_runner.py` — unattended, **pure-Gemini** (zero Anthropic — survives a Claude compute-limit gap that throttles the Opus/Sonnet loops) cross-city sweep, hard-capped at a configurable Gemini budget (**$9**; Brian raised $5→$9, $10 funded), lock-serialised + ledger-resumable, wrapping each city's brief with a terrain-agnostic style preamble + its own hand-made plate as the anchor; `AREA_PLATE` maps each seed slug to its (non-uniform) plate filename. ### 2026-06-18 — Concurrency/tick verification fix 4: WS-routing group (area-map memo, combat parallelism, null-room broadcast, dead dispatch) — *drop verify-fix-ws-routing*
Four WS-path findings. (a) **HIGH — area-map blank-until-re-enter:** `send_hud_update`'s `_last_sent_area_key` memo is advanced when the geometry is STAGED into the hud (server/session.py:1420), but the actual send (`:2114`) can fail and `return` — leaving the memo saying "already sent" so the map stays blank until the player leaves + re-enters the area. Fix: on send-failure, if the hud carried `area_geometry`, reset the memo so it re-sends next hud. (b) **HIGH — combat head-of-line blocking:** `_send_combat_state` (parser/combat_commands.py) awaited per-viewer sends in a sequential loop, so one slow/backpressured WS client stalled the whole combat round + the tick loop; now sent via `asyncio.gather(..., return_exceptions=True)`. (c) **MEDIUM — null-room broadcast crash:** `broadcast_chat`'s global branch did `for s in self._sessions` (dict → KEYS/ints) then `s.send_json` → AttributeError; → `.values()` + character guard. (d) **LOW:** removed a dead duplicate `case 'pose_event'` arm in the client WS dispatch (static/client.html). New `tests/test_ws_broadcast_routing.py` (2: global-broadcast iterates values + no duplicate dispatch case); existing combat-state suite green (12).

### 2026-06-18 — Concurrency/tick verification fix 3: tutorial hint-timer leak — *drop verify-fix-hint-timer*
Verification HIGH: `start_hint_timer` (engine/tutorial_v2.py) spawns a detached per-session `_hint_loop` asyncio task but it was only ever cancelled on the player's NEXT command (`on_player_input`) — never at disconnect. A player who enters the tutorial and drops without typing leaves the task looping forever, calling `session.send_line()` on a dead transport every `HINT_REPEAT` (the send error is swallowed, so it never dies); under launch churn these orphan coroutines + `_hint_tasks` entries accumulate. It was also keyed on `id(session)` (a memory address reused after GC → cross-session collision). Fix: rekey `_hint_tasks` on the monotonic `session.id`, and cancel from `SessionManager.remove` (server/session.py) — the single funnel every disconnect path (WS/telnet/web/idle/kick) already routes through (local import avoids a `session`↔`tutorial_v2` cycle). New `tests/test_hint_timer_teardown.py` (2): `remove()` cancels + de-registers the timer; keyed on `session.id` not the address.

### 2026-06-18 — Concurrency/tick verification fix 2: read-pool poisoning — *drop verify-fix-readpool*
Verification HIGH (the B1-read-pool blast-radius risk, reproduced): a `query_only`-rejected write on a pooled read conn left it stuck `in_transaction` (Python's legacy `isolation_level=''` auto-BEGINs before the DML, and SQLite raises *after* the BEGIN with nothing to roll it back). The `_reader` finally returned that conn to the pool as-is, so the held WAL read-transaction **pinned a stale snapshot** (subsequent pool reads served stale data) **and blocked WAL checkpointing** (-wal grew unbounded). Fix (`db/database.py`): open the pool conns with `isolation_level=None` (autocommit → SELECTs never auto-BEGIN, so a rejected write can't open a transaction), plus a self-healing `await conn.rollback()` on release (defense in depth). Corrected the docstrings that overstated "consistent-snapshot." New `tests/test_t321_read_pool.py::test_rejected_write_does_not_poison_pool_conn` (size-1 pool: rejected write → a later committed writer change must be visible, not stale). Suite 10 green.

### 2026-06-18 — Concurrency/tick verification fix 1: the `sm.sessions` blocker — *drop verify-fix-sessions*
The concurrency/tick verification campaign (a Workflow adversarial probe of the never-load-tested runtime surfaces) found a **blocker**: four sites iterate a **nonexistent `<mgr>.sessions`** attribute — the real `SessionManager` exposes `all` / `_sessions` / `count`, never `.sessions`. Effects: `server/tick_handlers_death.py:77` (`getattr(sm,"sessions",[])` → `[]` every tick) made **free time-based wound recovery a permanent no-op** — a player who doesn't pay for bacta stays wounded forever; `engine/debt.py:65` raised AttributeError (swallowed per-debtor) so **Hutt-debt collection collected nothing**; `engine/achievements.py:271` (under a now-false `hasattr(...,"sessions")` guard) and `engine/director.py:1138` were silently degraded. All four → `.all`. The bug hid because the suite's only coverage was `assertTrue(hasattr(tick_handlers_death,"wound_recovery_tick"))` (existence, not behavior) and several test STUBS define a `.sessions` the real manager lacks. New `tests/test_session_manager_accessor_contract.py` (4): a behavioral test proving `wound_recovery_tick` now reaches an enrolled wounded session via `.all` and clears it, + a static guard that no runtime module reintroduces `<mgr>.sessions`. Existing death/recovery suites green (127).

### 2026-06-17 — MSSP telnet option support — *drop marketing-mssp*
Added **MSSP (Mud Server Status Protocol, option 70)** to `server/telnet_handler.py` — the highest-leverage discoverability lever for MUD listing sites (MudVerse, MUDStats, Grapevine auto-index without manual registration). MSSP is sent **proactively on every new telnet connection** via `writer._transport.write()` (raw bytes, bypasses telnetlib3's text encoding which is required for the IAC/SB/SE framing). The payload is `IAC WILL MSSP + IAC SB MSSP <body> IAC SE` where the body is a sequence of `MSSP_VAR <key> MSSP_VAL <value>` byte pairs (UTF-8). Fields: `NAME` (from `config.game_name`), `PLAYERS` (live count via `session_mgr.count`), `UPTIME` (Unix timestamp of handler init), `PORT`, `STATUS=Beta`, `CODEBASE=SW_MUSH`, `LANGUAGE=English`, `CRAWL DELAY=300`. Sent **before** the session is added to `session_mgr` so crawler connections do not inflate the live player count. **Fail-open**: any `Exception` from the transport write is caught+logged at DEBUG, never propagated — MSSP failure cannot abort a real player session. `tests/test_marketing_mssp.py` (15 tests): payload structure guards (IAC WILL header, SB/SE framing), key-value encoding for all 8 required fields, no-IAC-in-body assertion, transport-injection integration (shell writes MSSP bytes on connect), and session-continues-on-transport-failure. No schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean. Marks `PRELAUNCH.marketing_launch` task 3 (MSSP) DONE.

### 2026-06-17 — T3.19 telemetry breadth: the objective funnel (catalog C) (Opus loop) — *drop t319-objective-telemetry*
**Telemetry BREADTH continuation** of `t319-telemetry-sink` (Brian decision #5: "SINK + BROAD EMITTERS"). The sink + the economy/CP/skill-check chokepoints shipped; this adds the **objective-completion funnel (catalog C)** so post-launch Claude can see whether missions get started-but-abandoned, which tier's pay is too low to bother finishing, etc.
- **NEW `engine.telemetry.emit_objective(kind, phase, char_id, *, oid, reward, **extra)`** — a single `objective` event type carrying `kind` (`mission`/`bounty`/`smuggling`) + `phase` (`start`/`complete`/`abandon`), so the offline funnel is a trivial pivot: `count(start)` vs `count(complete)` vs `count(abandon)` per kind, plus reward distribution per outcome. `char_id` is coerced to `int` when it parses (a str-id and an int-id system join on the same player); `None` extras are dropped; fail-open (wraps the already-fail-open `emit()` + guards field assembly).
- **9 emit sites at the lifecycle chokepoints** of the three board systems (all emitted only AFTER the DB mutation lands, so a record is a real transition): `MissionBoard.accept|complete|abandon` (+`mission_type`,`faction`; abandon captures `accepted_by` **before** it's cleared), `BountyBoard.claim|collect` (+`target`,`alive`; `collect` is the sole completion chokepoint — the auto-collect on kill via `notify_target_killed` routes through it, so one emit covers both paths), `SmugglingBoard.accept|complete|fail|dump_cargo` (+`tier`,`cargo`; `fail` carries `reason`+`fine`, `dump_cargo` `reason="dumped"`). Spacer/communal/chain quests have no single chokepoint (auto-trigger dispatchers) → deferred to a later breadth fire.
- Every call site is double-guarded fail-open: a broken telemetry layer can NEVER break a mission accept / bounty collect / smuggling run. No schema, no faucet/sink (telemetry OBSERVES objective transitions, never creates credits), era-clean. None of the chokepoints live in an avoid-lane file. `tests/test_t319_objective_telemetry.py` (18: helper schema/coercion/None-drop/fail-open + all 9 sites + reject-no-emit + auto-collect-routes-through + a raising-emitter-doesn't-break-accept proof).

### 2026-06-17 — Claude Design UI/UX review handoff package — screenshots + capture tool — *drop claude-design-handoff*

### 2026-06-17 — T3.19 telemetry: append-only JSON-line sink + 3 chokepoint emitters (Opus loop) — *drop t319-telemetry-sink*
**Second half of T3.19 (the telemetry instrumentation) — the SINK + broad emitters** Brian asked for (decision #5: "SINK + BROAD EMITTERS, not minimal"). Phase 0/1 (the `tunables.yaml` config half) shipped earlier; this lands the data-collection half so post-launch Claude can read real player behaviour and recommend knob changes (`telemetry_purpose_clarified`).
- **NEW `engine/telemetry.py`** — bounded-buffer, append-only JSON-line sink honouring the "never slow the game loop" contract: `emit()` ONLY appends to a bounded `deque` (non-blocking, fail-open, never raises, safe from sync or async code); ALL disk writes happen on a periodic flush (`flush_async` offloads the write to a thread executor). A stalled/disabled flush can't leak memory (bounded buffer drops oldest + counts it); a missing/unwritable sink degrades to dropping events, never to disturbing gameplay. Each record is `{"ts","seq","ev", **fields}`; envelope keys are collision-protected; non-serializable fields degrade via `default=str`. Default sink `logs/telemetry/events.jsonl` (gitignored); `SWMUSH_TELEMETRY_FILE` / `SWMUSH_TELEMETRY_ENABLED` overrides. Sampling support for high-frequency events. `configure()`/`reset()`/`stats()` for boot + test isolation.
- **NEW `server/tick_handlers_telemetry.flush_telemetry_tick`** — registered in `game_server.py` (`telemetry_flush`, interval=30, offset=11): drains the buffer to disk off the per-command hot path.
- **3 principled chokepoint emitters** (one site each captures an entire metric category, the elegant alternative to scattering emit calls):
  - `db.log_credit` → **`credit_flow`** `{char_id, delta, tag, balance}` — the single funnel EVERY credit movement (system / faucet-throttled / normal) passes through ⇒ the whole economy by tag (catalog B: per-faucet inflow + per-sink outflow).
  - `db.cp_add_character_points` → **`cp_award`** `{char_id, amount}` — every CP balance move (positive = earn, negative = spend; catalog B CP earn-vs-spend).
  - `engine.skill_checks.perform_skill_check` → **`skill_check`** `{char_id, skill, difficulty, roll, success, margin, crit, fumble}` — the single funnel for ALL out-of-combat dice ⇒ success rates by skill + difficulty band (catalog D: are DCs calibrated). Highest-frequency chokepoint, so its keep-rate is the new tunable `telemetry.skill_check_sample` (1.0 at launch; read at use-site per the T3.19 contract).
- All three emit calls are double-guarded (`emit()` is itself fail-open; the call site wraps it in `try/except` too) — a broken telemetry layer can never break a credit move, a CP grant, or a dice roll (explicit fail-open tests prove it).
- `data/tunables.yaml`: + `telemetry.skill_check_sample`. No schema change, no faucet/sink (telemetry observes credit movement, never creates it), era-clean.
- `tests/test_t319_telemetry.py` (31): sink semantics (buffer/drain/flush/append/sampling/bounded-overflow-drops-oldest/disabled/bad-field/write-error fail-open/stats), `flush_async`, module-singleton API, all 3 emitters against a real in-memory `Database` + a real `perform_skill_check`, the sample tunable, the fail-open invariant (gameplay survives a throwing emit), the flush tick, and structural drift pins on the wiring. Gate green single-process.

### 2026-06-17 — Guide_09 CP-progression timeline accuracy (QA M7 + L5) (Opus loop) — *drop guide09-cp-timeline-accuracy*
**Authoritative Opus quality pass on a guide** (guides are Opus-owned). The v23 CP retune (`200` ticks/CP, `400`-tick weekly cap = 2 CP/week, `10` ticks/day passive) had its *headline* numbers updated in the served guide, but the **derived advancement timeline was never recomputed** — it still quoted the pre-v23 (300/300/5, 1-CP-week) rate. - **Arithmetic fix:** the §8 table listed **3D→7D as 57 CP** — the engine's flat `advance_skill` rule (`cost = current whole-dice value`, QA L3 confirmed no doubling) yields 9+12+15+18 = **54 CP**. Corrected in both copies.

Synced to v23 — core loop 300→200, cap 300→400/1→2 CP/wk, passive 5→10 ticks/day, the Developer-Internals constants block (`TICKS_PER_CP`/`WEEKLY_CAP_TICKS`/`PASSIVE_TICKS_PER_DAY`) → 200/400/10, kudos "over a third of the 300-tick" → "over a quarter of the 400-tick", same timeline + 54-CP fixes. Also corrected a stale **kudos rule**: "Both players must be in the same room" → "Players do not need to be in the same room" (v23 removed the same-room requirement, `cp_commands.py:250`).
- Minor accuracy polish in both: "A 30-pose scene earns the **maximum** 54 ticks" → "earns 54 ticks (the 60-tick cap is reached around 33 poses)" — 54 is what 30 poses yield, not the cap.
- `tests/test_guide_09_timeline_accuracy.py` (new): guards **both** copies against the pre-v23 markers (300-tick / 10–12-days / 7-months / 57-CP / same-room) and asserts the corrected v23 timeline + same-room phrasing; cross-checks every quoted CP total (21/36/54/23) against an in-test reimplementation of the engine `advance_skill` cost rule and the 2-CP/week ceiling against `WEEKLY_CAP_TICKS // TICKS_PER_CP`, so a future retune that moves the engine but not the guide trips the test. ### 2026-06-17 — command-syntax rework DROP 7: type-3 genuine-conflict resolution → baseline ZERO (Opus loop) — *drop command-syntax-drop7-type3-conflicts*
**Terminal canonicalization drop.** Resolves the **last 9 baseline collisions** — the IC "type-3" conflicts DROP 6 deferred (`command_syntax_rework_design_v2.md` §"Phased build plan"). These are names two *genuinely-different* commands both wanted; the prior drops' comments at `combat_commands.py`, `mission_commands.py`, `crew_commands.py`, and `espionage_commands.py` explicitly parked each one for "a separate type-3 decision." Each is resolved CLEAN (delete the loser's claim, no back-compat alias) so the convention-invariant baseline reaches **0** (the ratchet's terminal state). **Three resolutions also fix live mis-resolutions** where last-wins had bound a contested verb to the *wrong* command.
- **`key:accept` + `alias:accept`** — bare `accept` stays with `mission_commands.AcceptMissionCommand` (it already smart-dispatches a PC challenge to combat's `AcceptCommand` when the arg names a challenger in-room). Combat's `AcceptCommand` is **no longer registered standalone** (its key:accept collision is gone); it lives on as the `+combat/accept` switch handler (`_SWITCH_IMPL["accept"]`) + the mission smart-dispatch delegate (both call it by class). Dead `accept` umbrella aliases removed from `+combat` and `+mission` (both dispatch `accept` via their switch maps + `valid_switches`).
- **`key:investigate`** — bare `investigate <id>` stays with `anomaly_commands.InvestigateCommand` (resolve a wilderness anomaly). The espionage room-search (`espionage_commands.InvestigateCommand`) is **re-canonicalized to `search`** (alias `inspect`) — it had aliased `search`/`inspect` but those routed to the anomaly key while it was shadowed, so the room search was reachable ONLY via `+spy investigate`. Now `search`/`inspect` cleanly reach it (a previously-unreachable bare form **restored**, per best/most-complete) and `+spy investigate` still dispatches it by class.
- **`key:order` + `alias:order`** — bare `order` stays with `crew_commands.OrderCommand` (order NPC crew). The space commander `OrderCommand` is **no longer registered standalone**; reachable via `+bridge/order` (`_BRIDGE_SWITCH_IMPL["order"]`). Dead `order` umbrella alias removed from `+crew` (dispatches via `+crew/order` switch).
- **`alias:listen` (mis-resolution fix)** — was binding to the trial-only `village_trial_commands.ExamineCommand` (last-wins). Now `listen` → `espionage_commands.EavesdropCommand` (listen to an adjacent room) — the universal meaning. Removed the `listen` alias from `+spy` and from the trial examine (trial players use the documented `examine fragment_<N>`).
- **`alias:p` (mis-resolution fix)** — was binding to `+party`. Now `p` → `mux_commands.PageCommand` (page), the universal MU* convention. Removed the `p` alias from the `+party` umbrella (`party` long-form survives).
- **`alias:retreat` (mis-resolution fix)** — was binding to wow_counsel's OOC leave-of-absence command. Now `retreat` → `combat_commands.FleeCommand` (combat disengage; it already aliased `run`/`retreat`) — the in-combat expectation. Removed the dup `retreat` alias from `+combat` and the bare `retreat` alias from `wow_counsel_retreat.RetreatCommand` (which keeps its A1-correct OOC `+retreat` key).
- **`alias:train`** — bare `train` stays with `cp_commands.TrainCommand` (spend CP to advance a skill). Removed the dead `train` alias from `tutorial_commands.TrainingCommand` (Training Grounds, reached via `training`/`+training`).
- Baseline ratchet **collisions 9→0, run_on_keys 0** (regen `tools/gen_command_convention_baseline.py`; **zero added** — baseline only shrinks; this is its terminal value). The command-syntax rework collision surface is now fully canonicalized (133→0 across Drops 0-7).
- `tests/test_command_syntax_drop7.py` (new): asserts the baseline + live registry are collision-free, parametrizes every contested name → its canonical owner (incl. the `search`/`inspect`/`eavesdrop` espionage re-home), pins each loser's alias is gone (and the survivor's long-form kept), and verifies the two de-registered commands stay reachable via their umbrellas (`+combat/accept`, `+bridge/order`) + are no longer standalone. Gate green single-process (drop7 + convention-invariant + drop2 + admin-access-invariant + S54 combat / S56 crew / S57b space umbrellas + drop6 @-namespace + wow2c/wow3b retreat+duels + guide22/syn5 espionage + f7c1 trials + pm3 training + h2/session49 missions + hygiene + smoke foundation; 470+ passed). Parser-layer only — no `engine/combat.py`/`director.py`/`harvest.py` (avoid-lane); no schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean.

### 2026-06-17 — command-syntax rework DROP 6: @-namespace collision resolution (Opus loop) — *drop command-syntax-drop6-at-namespace*
Resolves **6 of the 9 remaining baseline collisions** — every collision in the `@` staff namespace (`command_syntax_rework_design_v2.md`). The other 3 + their alias twins are IC type-3 conflicts (`accept`/`order`/`investigate`/`listen`/`p`/`retreat`/`train`) deferred to a later drop. Diagnostic recipe (monkeypatch `CommandRegistry.register` to trace declarer+module, then `reg.get(name)` for the winner) classified each collision as a dead/mis-bound alias vs a shadowed-duplicate key.
- **Dead / mis-bound building aliases** (each registered after its true owner, so it was a dead duplicate; removing it leaves the correct winner): `@set` no longer aliases `@succ` (stray copy-paste; `@succ`→`@success`); `@dig` no longer aliases `@tel` (`@tel`→`@teleport`); `@open` no longer aliases `@tun` — **behaviour-correcting**: `@tun` abbreviates `@tunnel`, but `@open` had wrongly captured it by registering later, so `@tun` was silently doing `@open`. Removing it **restores `@tun`→`@tunnel`**.
- **`@ai` duplicate deleted, capability folded in:** `parser/npc_commands.py` had a second `AIStatusCommand` (status/enable/disable) permanently shadowed by the richer `parser/director_commands.py` dashboard (Ollama/idle-queue/barks/flush, `@ollama`/`@idle` aliases) — Guide_27 documents the dashboard. Deleted the dead npc duplicate; **folded its unique `enable`/`disable` toggle into the surviving dashboard** (`@ai enable | @ai disable` flip `ai_manager.config.enabled`) so no capability is lost (best/most-complete). Parser-layer only — does **not** touch `engine/director.py` (avoid-lane); the command operates on the AI manager, not the Director economy engine.
- **`@getattr`/`@setattr` two-tool conflict disambiguated:** two genuinely different tools shared these keys. The **universal object-attribute system** (`parser/attr_commands.py`: TinyMUX attrs on rooms/exits/objects via `object_attributes`, `&` shorthand + room-hook engine, BUILDER) always won and **keeps `@getattr`/`@setattr`**. The **character-JSON-blob debug tool** (`parser/building_tier2.py`: dumps/sets the executing char's raw `attributes` blob, e.g. `@setcharattr starter_quest = 10`, ADMIN) was permanently shadowed/**dead** yet documented in Guide_27 — **renamed to `@getcharattr`/`@setcharattr` (`@gca`/`@sca`)** so it is reachable again (a documented-but-broken admin tool restored, not deleted). `data/guides/Guide_27_Administration.md` §6 updated to the new keys + a note distinguishing the two systems.
- Baseline ratchet **collisions 15→9** (regen `tools/gen_command_convention_baseline.py`; removed `alias:@succ`/`@tel`/`@tun` + `key:@ai`/`@getattr`/`@setattr`, **zero added** — baseline only shrinks). No `@`-namespace collision remains; the 9 leftovers are all IC type-3 (`key:accept`/`order`/`investigate` + `alias:accept`/`order`/`listen`/`p`/`retreat`/`train`).
- `tests/test_command_syntax_drop6_at_namespace.py` (new): pins the 6 winners, asserts the npc `AIStatusCommand` class is gone (not merely unregistered), the char-attr tool is reachable under the new keys at ADMIN, `@getattr`/`@setattr` stay the BUILDER universal system, a behavioural check that the folded-in `@ai enable`/`disable` flips `config.enabled` (incl. graceful no-AI-manager), and the baseline shrank. Gate green single-process (drop6 + convention-invariant + admin-access-invariant + chain-corpus-reachability + npc-dialogue-cleanup + syn9-player-buildings + S57b space umbrellas + hygiene + smoke foundation; 206 passed). No schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean.

The switch form is the only way in.

### 2026-06-17 — command-syntax rework DROP 5a: space station-umbrella dead-alias cleanup (Opus loop) — *drop command-syntax-drop5-stations*
Third module batch of the command-syntax rework long tail (`command_syntax_rework_design_v2.md` §"Phased build plan"; follows DROP 3 service-family + DROP 4 combat/crew/mission/espionage). Trimmed the four **space station umbrellas** (`+pilot`/`+gunner`/`+sensors`/`+bridge`, registered FIRST per `register_space_commands`) of the per-verb DUPLICATE aliases each re-declared but a STANDALONE maneuver/action command in the same module already OWNED — the standalone registers later so it WON the binding → every such umbrella alias was DEAD (never resolved to the umbrella). Deleting them is **pure zero-behaviour-change cleanup**: all 26 removed aliases still resolve through the full registry to the EXACT same handler (verified via `reg.get` in the per-drop test).
- **`+pilot`** (10 removed): `evasive`→EvadeCommand, `broll`→BarrelRollCommand, `immelmann`→LoopCommand, `sideslip`→SlipCommand, `getbehind`→TailCommand, `shake`→OutmaneuverCommand, `approach`→CloseRangeCommand, `breakaway`→FleeShipCommand, `navigate`/`setcourse`→CourseCommand.
- **`+gunner`** (3 removed): `gunnery`→GunnerCommand, `lock`/`targetlock`→LockOnCommand.
- **`+sensors`** (1 removed): `sensor`→SensorsCommand.
- **`+bridge`** (12 removed): `command`/`captain`→CommanderCommand, `comm`/`radio`→CommsCommand, `pwr`→PowerCommand, `transp`→TransponderCommand, `breakfree`→ResistTractorCommand, `damagecontrol`/`repair`→DamConCommand, `unstation`→VacateCommand, `coord`→CoordinateCommand, `order`/`orders`→the crew `OrderCommand` (unchanged). (`alias:order` STAYS in the baseline — it's still produced by the crew vs space `key:order` type-3 conflict; only `alias:orders` cleared.)
- **The bare verbs matching a standalone's KEY are KEPT** (`+pilot`: evade/jink/barrelroll/loop/slip/tail/outmaneuver/close/fleeship/course; `+gunner`: gunner/fire/lockon; `+sensors`: sensors/scan/deepscan; `+bridge`: commander/hail/comms/shields/power/transponder/resist/damcon/vacate/assist/coordinate) — they are not tracked collisions (a primary-key registered after an alias is not flagged) and removing them wouldn't shrink the baseline. This matches the `+combat` umbrella's kept verbs (DROP 4).
- **ONLY the `.aliases` lists were edited; the `_*_ALIAS_TO_SWITCH` / `_*_SWITCH_IMPL` dispatch maps LEFT intact** (they drive the canonical `+pilot/<switch>` etc. forms — verified the switch tables still reach EvadeCommand/CourseCommand/LockOnCommand/ScanCommand/DamConCommand/OrderCommand).
- **DEFERRED (type-3 / ship-family, next Opus fire):** the **ship-family** consolidation (`+ships`/`+myships`/`+shipinfo`/`+shiprepair`/`+shipname` + bare `ships`/`si`/`myships`/… → the `+ship/<switch>` umbrella; needs the bare-vs-`+` A1 decision + ref updates) and the genuine cross-command key conflicts (`key:accept`, `key:order` space-vs-crew, `key:investigate`, `alias:retreat`, `alias:listen`, `alias:train`, `key:@ai`/`@getattr`/`@setattr`, `@succ`/`@tel`/`@tun`, `alias:p`).
- Baseline ratchet **collisions 54→28** (regen `tools/gen_command_convention_baseline.py`; zero added — baseline only shrinks). `tests/test_command_syntax_drop5_stations.py` (10) + reframed the four `test_aliases_cover_bare_verbs` assertions in `tests/test_session57b_space_umbrellas.py` from "umbrella must alias every bare verb" → "kept aliases are the canonical verbs; removed ones still resolve via their standalone"; updated the module docstring alias counts. Gate green single-process (192). No schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean.

### 2026-06-17 — command-syntax rework DROP 4: combat/crew/mission/espionage umbrella dead-alias cleanup (Opus loop) — *drop command-syntax-drop4*
Second module batch of the command-syntax rework long tail (`command_syntax_rework_design_v2.md` §"Phased build plan"; follows DROP 3's service-family cleanup). Trimmed the `+combat` / `+crew` / `+mission` / `+spy` umbrellas of the per-verb aliases they re-declared but a STANDALONE command in the same module already OWNED — the standalone registers later so it WON the binding → every such umbrella alias was DEAD (never resolved to the umbrella). Deleting them is **pure zero-behaviour-change cleanup**: all 36 removed aliases still resolve through the full registry to the EXACT same standalone handler (verified via `reg.get` in the per-drop test), so NO runtime / onboarding / help / SPA string changed.
- **`+combat`** (15 removed): `cs`→CombatStatusCommand, `att`/`kill`/`shoot`/`hit`→AttackCommand, `fdodge`→FullDodgeCommand, `fparry`→FullParryCommand, `soak`→SoakCommand, `run`→FleeCommand, `distance`→RangeCommand, `hide`→CoverCommand, `fp`→ForcePointCommand, `combatpose`→CombatPoseCommand, `duel`→ChallengeCommand, `refuse`→DeclineCommand.
- **`+crew`** (5 removed): `recruiting`/`hireboard`→HireCommand, `roster`→RosterCommand, `firecrew`→DismissCrewCommand, `ord`→OrderCommand. (`crew`/`mycrew` — the umbrella's own view shorthands — kept.)
- **`+mission`** (10 removed): `missions`/`mb`/`jobs`→MissionsCommand, `myjob`/`activemission`→ActiveMissionCommand, `takejob`→AcceptMissionCommand, `finishjob`/`turnin`→CompleteMissionCommand, `dropmission`/`quitjob`→AbandonMissionCommand.
- **`+spy`** (6 removed): `size`→ScanCommand, `search`/`inspect`→InvestigateCommand, `intel`→IntelCommand, `wiretap`/`comtap`→InterceptCommand.
- **ONLY the `.aliases` lists were edited; the `_*_ALIAS_TO_SWITCH` / `_*_SWITCH_IMPL` dispatch maps LEFT intact** (they drive `+cmd/<switch>` + the arg-keyed `+spy <verb>` form, and are exercised by the S54/S55/S56/S58 dispatch tests — touching them would break those).
- **Genuine cross-command CONFLICTS NOT touched** (deferred to a later type-3 drop): `key:accept` (combat AcceptCommand vs mission AcceptMissionCommand), `key:order` (space vs crew), `key:investigate` (anomaly vs espionage), `alias:retreat` (combat flee vs wow_counsel RetreatCommand), `alias:listen` (espionage vs village_trial). The entire **space** module (ship-family + station umbrellas, ~40 collisions) is its own follow-up batch.
- Baseline ratchet **collisions 90→54** (regen `tools/gen_command_convention_baseline.py`; zero added — baseline only shrinks). `tests/test_command_syntax_drop4.py` (7) + reframed the four umbrella-alias assertions S54/S55/S56/S58 from "umbrella must alias every bare verb" → "bare verbs still resolve via their standalone command". Gate green single-process. No schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean.

### 2026-06-17 — command-syntax rework DROP 3: service-family umbrella dead-alias cleanup (Opus loop) — *drop command-syntax-drop3*
Third canonicalization phase of the ratified rework (`docs/design/command_syntax_rework_design_v2.md` §"Phased build plan" Drops 3-4 — the long tail, "in module-grouped batches"). First module-grouped batch: the six **service-family umbrellas** whose `aliases` lists re-declared verb/query names that a **standalone command in the same module already owned**. Because the standalone registers *after* the umbrella it WINS the binding, so every such umbrella alias was already **dead** (it never resolved to the umbrella). Deleting it is a **pure zero-behaviour-change cleanup** that drops the registry collision and removes the redundant form rule C calls for.
- **Umbrellas trimmed (dead aliases deleted — each name is owned by the standalone command shown):**
  - `+bounty` ← `bounties`/`bboard`/`bountyboard` (→ `+bounties`), `mybounty`/`activebounty`/`myhunt` (→ `+mybounty`)
  - `+smuggle` ← `smugjobs`/`smugboard`/`underworld` (→ `+smugjobs`), `smugaccept`/`takerun` (→ `smugaccept`), `smugjob`/`myrun`/`cargo` (→ `+smugjob`), `smugdump`/`dumpcargo`/`jettison` (→ `smugdump`)
  - `+craft` ← `craft`/`survey`/`resources`/`res`/`schematics`/`schem`/`experiment`/`exp`/`teach` (→ the standalone bare IC verbs / query commands)
  - `+medical` ← `heal`/`healaccept`/`haccept`/`healrate`/`hrate` (→ `heal`/`healaccept`/`+healrate`)
  - `+place` ← `places`/`place`/`join`/`sit`/`depart`/`stand` (→ `places`/`join`/`depart`)
  - `+quest` ← `quests`/`personalquests` (→ `+quests`)
- **Surgical scope — ONLY the `aliases` lists changed.** The genuine umbrella shorthands that *do* route through the umbrella to a switch are KEPT (`+bounty`: claimbounty/acceptbounty/tracktarget/hunttrack/collectbounty/claimreward; `+smuggle`: deliver/dropoff; `+craft`: buyres; `+quest`: acceptquest/pqaccept/finishquest/pqcomplete/completequest/abandonquest/pqdrop). The internal `_*_ALIAS_TO_SWITCH` dispatch maps are **left intact** — they still drive the arg-keyed `+medical <verb>` / `+place <verb>` forms and are exercised by direct-instantiation tests; their (now-inert) entries for removed bare words harmlessly document the historical dispatch.
- **Verified zero behaviour change:** all 41 removed aliases still resolve through the full live registry to the *exact same* standalone command as before (the standalone always won). No runtime/onboarding/help/SPA string needed updating — every form types and resolves identically.
- **Baseline ratchet shrunk:** regenerated `tests/data/command_convention_baseline.json` — **collisions 116 → 90** (26 recorded collisions de-collided; the alias-shadowed-by-key dead forms removed too as bonus cleanup); **zero new entries** (baseline only shrinks). `run_on_keys` stays 0.
- **`tests/test_command_syntax_drop3.py` (7 tests):** the umbrellas no longer declare the dead aliases; every removed alias resolves unchanged to its standalone owner; the recorded collisions are gone; the regenerated baseline excludes them and the live registry introduces nothing beyond it; the umbrella keys + live switch-routing aliases still reach the umbrella; the arg-keyed dispatch maps are intact. Updated the expected-churn assertions in the umbrella suites (`tests/test_session55_jobs_umbrellas.py` ×3, `tests/test_session56_craft_crew_umbrellas.py` ×1, `tests/test_session58_cleanup_umbrellas.py` ×2) from the old "umbrella must alias every bare verb" invariant to "bare verbs still resolve via their standalone command".
- **NEXT (Opus loop) = command-syntax Drop 4** (the remaining collision worklist: combat/space/crew/mission/espionage umbrella dead-alias cleanup + the genuine cross-command key conflicts `accept`/`order`/`investigate`/`retreat`/`listen`), then **Drop 5** (the 6 `@`-exceptions). No schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean.

### 2026-06-17 — QA L2: 0D force-attribute lockout fixed — *drop qa-l2-force-0d-lockout* (Sonnet loop)
A character whose `attributes` JSON contained `control`/`sense`/`alter` = `'0D'` was incorrectly reconstructed as `force_sensitive=True` (key presence triggered the flag) but then **rejected by every Force command** (`list_powers_for_char` checks `pool.dice > 0 or pool.pips > 0` → False for 0D). The player was trapped: shown as Force-sensitive, locked out of all powers.
- **`engine/character.py` `from_db_dict`:** refactored the force-attribute loop to capture the parsed `DicePool` first; `force_sensitive = True` is now only set if `not pool.is_zero()`. A `village_chosen_path`-committed Jedi with 0D attrs still gets the safety-net `force_sensitive=True` from the existing failsafe (intact). No behavior change for chars with 1D+ attrs.
- **`tests/test_qa_l2_force_0d_lockout.py`** (8): all-zero attrs → not-force-sensitive; pip-only pool → force-sensitive; mixed 0D+non-zero → force-sensitive; committed path + 0D → failsafe preserves True.

### 2026-06-17 — QA H2: faction-mission reconciliation — live DB path made canonical + complete — *drop qa-h2-faction-missions*
Resolves design call `H2.faction_mission_system_reconciliation` → **Option A** (Brian: best/most-complete). Two faction-mission systems coexisted and neither yielded an acceptable+completable mission. **Decision: make the LIVE leader/Director DB path canonical** (the unwired procedural `generate_faction_mission` would have *deleted* player-leadership + Director-authored faction missions — both author angles preserved instead).
- **`db/database.py` `post_faction_mission`:** was writing `data='{}'` (board discarded it). Now writes a full slug-keyed `Mission.to_dict()` blob — slug id `fm-<faction>-<uuid4 hex>` (full hex so the accept-path `data LIKE` can't collide), `faction_code`, `faction_rep_required`, `objective`, reward, and a real **`destination_room_id` (the completion model)**.
- **Completion model:** leader-posted → turn in at the faction **HQ room** (`org.hq_room_id`); Director-posted → a room in the Director's **target zone**. The existing accept→travel→`complete`→`adjust_credits`→rep→territory funnel then works unchanged (reward stays on the existing funnel — no new faucet).
- **Rep gate enforced at accept** (`parser/mission_commands.py`): the public board had no rep filter; a non-member / under-rep player now cannot accept a faction mission. Faction missions are excluded from the public board (private `faction missions` only). Slug shown in the display; footer verb fixed (`accept <id>`).
- **`engine/missions.inject_faction_mission_into_board`:** posts hit the live board immediately (no 30-min refresh wait). Relocated to the board's own engine module (was in the parser layer) so the Director can call it without an engine→parser import inversion.
- **director.py touch** (avoid-lane, sanctioned for completeness): one localized guarded branch in `_apply_faction_order` resolves the target-zone room via the public `db.fetchall` (was reaching the private `db._db` — fixed per review).
- **Verified:** `tests/test_h2_faction_missions.py` (14 — leader + Director full accept→complete→reward loops, rep-gate rejection, blob round-trip, public-board exclusion, slug display) + `test_session49_faction_missions` 20/20. Verify fan-out (invariant + code-review + smoke) → fix-then-ship, all findings folded.

### 2026-06-17 — QA H1: phantom item registry — author the 14 dead items into weapons.yaml — *drop qa-h1-item-registry*
Resolves QA finding H1 (Brian: best/most-complete). ~14 combat-class item keys granted by faction rank-up / commissary / tutorial chains were defined NOWHERE → they couldn't be equipped ("You aren't carrying a weapon matching…") → **broken starter kits at every tutorial graduation**. The QA premise was half-wrong: armor already has a home (`weapons.yaml` holds `type:armor`); the real defect was a *disconnect* between the grant paths' stub catalogs and the registry. **Decision: EXTEND the existing registry** (the new-unified-ItemRegistry is the parallel-system the invariants forbid → deferred post-launch as `ITEM.unified_item_registry`).
- **`data/weapons.yaml`:** 14 new rows — 5 weapons (dc17_pistol, dc15_blaster_rifle, officers_sidearm, e5_blaster_rifle, concealed_blaster) + 9 armor (republic_uniform/republic_light_armor/improved_armor/smuggler_vest/padawan_robes/jedi_robes/cis_field_armor/flight_suit_republic/officers_uniform_republic), re-statted to WEG R&E D6 (CW-era; DC-15/17/E-5 canon), all `vendor_stocked: false` so faction/tutorial gear never leaks into the open `buy` vendor. (`improved_armor` re-balanced per review to +2D/+1D, -1D Dex — full-body composite carries the standard penalty.)
- **Grant paths rewired** (`engine/organizations.py`, `engine/commissary.py`, `engine/chain_rewards.py`): resolve display name+slot from `get_weapon_registry()` when the key resolves; the ~24 legitimately registry-less narrative props fall back to the stub dict.
- **Verified:** `tests/test_h1_item_registry_consistency.py` (16 — the cross-registry test that was missing, which is why H1 hid: every grant-path weapon/armor key must resolve in the registry; + a granted item actually equips). 128 passed in the build.

### 2026-06-16 — QA blocker B1: the sqlite3.Row.get() bug class (root-cause row_factory fix) — *drop qa-blockers-row-get*
Fixes the **hardest** of the three verified launch BLOCKERS from `docs/design/QA_FINDINGS_2026-06-16.md` — B1, the one the loop-safe `qa-blockers-b2-b3` drop deliberately left for an attended session. **B2 + B3 were fixed in parallel by the Opus loop** (`drop qa-blockers-b2-b3`, below), so this drop reconciled to **B1-only**; its test still validates B2/B3 behaviorally. The green ~7,700-test suite was blind to B1 because its DB stubs return dicts; found by the live-harness QA campaign + **verified with an empirical `sqlite3.Row.get()` AttributeError repro**.
- **B1 — `sqlite3.Row.get()` AttributeError, a whole bug CLASS (root-cause fix).** Production `row_factory = aiosqlite.Row` (== `sqlite3.Row`, **no `.get()`**); the `fetchall`/`fetchone` wrappers return raw rows and **127 DB methods call the raw `execute_fetchall` directly** — so the correct single-point fix is the **row_factory**, not the wrapper (Brian's call: dict-convert reads). New `db.database._dict_row_factory` (`{col: val}` from `cursor.description`) set on BOTH the main connection and every read-pool connection. All ~163 `row.get(...)` sites now work; the confirmed-broken death/recovery arc — bacta tank/pack, loot-own-corpse, corpse-decay (was *silently destroying gear*), and the 1-hr wound auto-recovery (the `-1D` penalty was *permanent*) — is restored transitively. **Positional-indexing audit done first** (dict rows key by name, not position): only 2 real DB sites converted — `engine/smuggling.py` `row[0]`→`row["data"]`, `db/integrity.py` PRAGMA reads→`list(row.values())`; the other `row[N]` hits were Python constants or already `isinstance`-guarded.
- **Test (closes the blind spot):** `tests/test_qa_blockers_row_get.py` (11) runs against a **REAL `Database`**, not a dict stub — asserts `.get()`/named access on real `fetchone`/`fetchall`/read-pool rows, drives `get_wound_state` through a real character (+ behavioral B2/B3 coverage that validates the loop's fixes). **Verified:** broad DB-read cross-section **1754 passed** single-process (only the known `smuggler` chain-walkthrough suite-order flake failed — passes solo). ⚠ **Core-DB blast radius (every read) → the full `run_all_tests.bat` suite is the merge gate.**

### 2026-06-17 — command-syntax rework DROP 2: run-on smashes → verb/switch families (Opus loop) — *drop command-syntax-drop2*
Second canonicalization phase of the ratified rework (`docs/design/command_syntax_rework_design_v2.md` §"Phased build plan" Drop 2). The ~9 run-on "smash" command keys are **DELETED** in favour of the canonical `+verb/<switch>` umbrella form (CLEAN — no back-compat aliases, since nobody is playing yet). The umbrellas (`+bounty`/`+quest`/`+smuggle`/`+craft`) already existed and dispatched via switches; the run-on standalone commands were legacy duplicates registered alongside them.
- **Deleted run-on key → canonical replacement:**
  - `bountyclaim` → `+bounty/claim` · `bountytrack` → `+bounty/track` · `bountycollect` → `+bounty/collect`
  - `questaccept` → `+quest/accept` · `questcomplete` → `+quest/complete` · `questabandon` → `+quest/abandon`
  - `smugdeliver` → `+smuggle/deliver`
  - `buyresources` → `+craft/buyresources`
  - `spacerquest` → `+spacerquest` (the FDtS chain's run-on key promoted to the `+` form — A1: OOC/query takes the `+` prefix; not a switch family, it's a single command with arg subcommands `log`/`abandon`)
- **Mechanism:** the per-verb command classes (`BountyClaimCommand`, `QuestAcceptCommand`, `SmugDeliverCommand`, `BuyResourcesCommand`, …) survive as **switch implementations only** — they are removed from their `register_*` functions and from the umbrella `aliases` lists + `_*_ALIAS_TO_SWITCH` dispatch maps, so the run-on keys no longer resolve as a key, alias, or prefix match (typing `bountyclaim` is now a clean "command not found"). The umbrella `_*_SWITCH_IMPL` tables still wire them, so `+bounty/claim` etc. dispatch unchanged.
- **CLEAN, de-collided:** the surviving **non-run-on** aliases (`claimbounty`, `acceptbounty`, `tracktarget`, `hunttrack`, `collectbounty`, `claimreward`, `acceptquest`, `finishquest`, `abandonquest`, `completequest`, `deliver`, `dropoff`, `buyres`) keep routing through the umbrella and — because the duplicate standalone registration is gone — are no longer collisions. The legacy bare forms are the Drops 3-4 long-tail; only the run-on smashes are removed here.
- **Runtime/onboarding strings updated to canonical** (don't tell players to type a deleted command): `parser/{bounty,narrative,smuggling,crafting,spacer_quest}_commands.py` usage + help strings; `parser/builtin_commands.py` `+commands` CATEGORIES listing; `engine/{bounty_board,smuggling,spacer_quest,tutorial_v2,chain_missions,crafting}.py` hints/comments; `build_tutorial.py` tutorial-room descriptions + NPC briefings (baked into the DB at boot via `auto_build_if_needed`).
- **Web SPA staging** (real command-sends): `static/spa/m3_board.js` stages `+bounty/claim <id>` / `+bounty/track`; `static/spa/m3_craft.js` stages `+craft/buyresources <type> `; `static/client.html` doc comments. The `+verb/switch` form parses identically (the parser splits `/switch` into `ctx.switches` before lookup).
- **Baseline ratchet shrunk:** regenerated `tests/data/command_convention_baseline.json` via `tools/gen_command_convention_baseline.py` — **run_on_keys 9→0** and **collisions 132→116** (16 run-on-family aliases de-collided); **zero new entries** (the baseline only shrinks). `tests/test_command_convention_invariant.py` stays green.
- **`tests/test_command_syntax_drop2.py` (8 tests):** every run-on smash is gone (no key/alias/prefix); the run-on baseline ratchet is empty; the `+verb/switch` canonical forms resolve to their umbrella + the switch is a declared `valid_switch`; the umbrella switch-impl dispatch tables still wire each verb's class; the surviving non-run-on aliases still route to the umbrella; `+spacerquest` promotion; de-collision. Updated the umbrella tests (`tests/test_session55_jobs_umbrellas.py`, `tests/test_session56_craft_crew_umbrellas.py`) and SPA render tests (`tests/spa/test_m3_board.py`, `tests/spa/test_m3_craft.py`) and smoke scenarios (`chain_bounty_track`, `chain_walkthrough`, `smuggling_loop`, `spacer_quest`, `portal`) to the canonical forms.
- **Deferred (by design):** the help/guide corpus (`data/help/**`, `data/guides/**`) documents the canonical forms in the coordinated doc rework that runs *after* all canonicalization drops land — left untouched here. No schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean.

### 2026-06-17 — TD.DUAL_PYTEST_INI + TD.TEXTURE_ENCOUNTER_TICK_SEEDLESS_FLAKE: pytest consolidation + flaky test fix (Sonnet loop) — *drop tech-debt-pytest-ini-flake-fix*
Closes two open tech-debt items.

**TD.DUAL_PYTEST_INI** — Two `[pytest]` configs had to be kept in sync manually; targeted `pytest tests/<module>` runs resolved `tests/pytest.ini` (nearest ancestor) while no-arg runs used root `pytest.ini`. Added `-m "... and not slow"` to BOTH addopts in the test-suite-prune drop (2026-06-14) and logged the smell. Now resolved: `tests/pytest.ini` deleted; root `pytest.ini` comment updated to note it governs both no-arg and targeted runs (pytest resolves nearest ancestor — with the inner file gone, all runs fall back to root). `tests/test_slow_marker_contract.py`: `test_tests_pytest_ini_excludes_slow_by_default` replaced by `test_single_pytest_ini_no_duplicate` (tombstone guard — asserts `tests/pytest.ini` does NOT exist so it cannot be reintroduced silently). `.claude/agents/smoke-verifier.md` reference updated.

**TD.TEXTURE_ENCOUNTER_TICK_SEEDLESS_FLAKE** — `tests/test_session38.py::TestTextureEncounterTick::test_security_scaling` ran 5000 iterations of `texture_encounter_tick` with unseeded random. The zone probability gap (`coruscant_orbit` neutral→0.005 vs `nar_shaddaa_orbit` lawless→0.010) is only 2×, giving a ~1/550 failure probability per run — enough to occasionally flip the board RED. Fix: save RNG state at entry, `random.seed(0)`, run the loop, restore in a `finally` block. With seed=0 the test produces ~24 secured vs ~58 lawless — deterministic and correct. No behavior change to the production code.

- **Files:** `pytest.ini` (comment update), `tests/pytest.ini` (deleted), `tests/test_slow_marker_contract.py`, `tests/test_session38.py`, `.claude/agents/smoke-verifier.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-17 — TD.WILDERNESS_AMBIENT_LINES_DEAD_WRITE: per-room landmark ambient lines now fire in-game (Sonnet loop) — *drop wilderness-ambient-reader*
Closes tech debt item `TD.WILDERNESS_AMBIENT_LINES_DEAD_WRITE`. `engine/wilderness_writer.py` wrote authored `ambient_lines` blocks (from `force_resonant_landmarks.yaml` + `coruscant_underworld_landmarks.yaml`) into the `wilderness_ambient_lines` room property, but no runtime path ever read that property — the authored atmospheric flavor text (Force-resonant stone circles, Tusken burial grounds, Coruscant underworld tunnels) has never surfaced in-game.
- **Fix (additive, no deletions):** `engine/ambient_events.py` — (1) new `_get_room_ambient_lines(room_id, db)` async method reads `properties.wilderness_ambient_lines` from a room, builds `AmbientLine` objects, and caches permanently (wilderness rooms never change their authored lines at runtime). (2) `_pick_line(zone_key, room_lines=None)` — new optional param; when non-empty, `room_lines` are merged into the static pool path (room-authored lines stand alongside the zone static pool; both draw at the 70% static rate). (3) `tick()` now calls `_get_room_ambient_lines` and passes the result to `_pick_line` — non-landmark rooms return an empty list with one cached DB call overhead, net zero ongoing cost.
- **`tests/test_wilderness_ambient_lines_reader.py` (12 tests):** `_get_room_ambient_lines` returns AmbientLine objects from props; empty for rooms with no lines or missing rooms; caches after first call (second call skips DB); empty strings skipped; `_pick_line` merges room lines into static draw; room-only pool with no static zone still returns a line; existing no-room-lines callers unaffected; returns None when both pool and room_lines are empty. No schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean.

### 2026-06-17 — QA L6: P2P velocity alert now pages online staff (Sonnet loop) — *drop qa-l6-p2p-staff-page*
Closes QA finding **L6** from `docs/design/QA_FINDINGS_2026-06-16.md`.
- **Root cause:** the P2P trade-velocity alert (ECON.p2p_cap_review=a — the old 1,500 cr/24h cap threshold repurposed as telemetry) recorded breaches to the ring buffer (`record_alert`) and wrote to the server log, but unlike the server-wide `credit_velocity_alert_tick` it did NOT page online admin/builder sessions in real-time. Staff had to poll `@economy alerts` manually.
- **Fix:** made `_page_economy_alert_staff` a public function (`page_economy_alert_staff`) in `server/tick_handlers_economy.py`; the P2P alert block in `parser/builtin_commands.py` now imports and calls it after `record_alert`/`log.info`. Wrapped in the existing fail-open `except Exception` guard so a page failure never disturbs a completed trade. `ctx.session_mgr` is already available at that call site (other code in the same handler uses it).
- **`tests/test_qa_l6_p2p_velocity_staff_page.py` (9 tests):** alert below caution returns None; at caution returns correct dict; bad input is safe; `format_alert_line` renders correctly; ring buffer records and retrieves; `None` session_mgr is a no-op; pages admin+builder but not player or spectator; tolerates a broken session; public symbol importable. No schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean.

### 2026-06-17 — command-syntax rework DROP 1: prefix canonicalization (high-traffic OOC/HUD) (Opus loop) — *drop command-syntax-drop1*
First canonicalization phase of the ratified rework (`docs/design/command_syntax_rework_design_v2.md` §"Phased build plan" Drop 1). Drop 0 (the convention enforcement guard, `ecfd070`/`90156af`) made collisions observable but renamed nothing; this is the first phase that **deletes** redundant forms. A1 prefix policy: OOC/meta/query/HUD commands take a single canonical `+`-prefixed form; the bare forms and `+`-synonyms are DELETED (CLEAN — no back-compat aliases, since nobody is playing yet).
- **Canonicalized (canonical ← deleted forms):**
  - `+who` ← `who`, `online`, `+online`, `players`
  - `+inv` ← `inventory`, `inv`, `i`, `+inventory`
  - `+sheet` ← `sheet`, `score`, `stats`, `+score`, `+stats`, `sc`
  - `+finger` ← `finger`
  - `+roll` ← `roll`
  - `+check` ← `check`
  - Movement is already A1-compliant (bare direction words route via `_MOVEMENT_DIRECTIONS`/`DIRECTION_ALIASES`) — no change.
- **`who` dual-impl fork RESOLVED (feature-preserving merge):** there were two live "who's online" commands — `parser/builtin_commands.WhoCommand` (`+who`: name/species/`[PROTOCOL]`/title) and `parser/channel_commands.WhoCommand` (bare `who`: name/location/combat-status). The bare `who` shadowed the builtin `who` alias (channel registers after builtin; a primary key beats an alias). Merged: `+who` is now the single canonical who-listing and gained the channel version's richer per-player **location + combat status** (helper ported as `_who_player_status`). The channel `WhoCommand` and its now-orphaned `_get_player_status` are DELETED (no dead code). The low-value `[PROTOCOL]` column was dropped in the merge.
- **`inv` prefix-match consequence (documented):** with the bare `inv` inventory alias deleted, typing `inv` now prefix-matches `investigate` (the only registered key starting with `inv`) rather than inventory — an intentional consequence of the CLEAN deletion; players use `+inv`.
- **Onboarding updated to canonical:** `engine/tutorial_v2.py` (Rocky Pass hint + the tutorial-step list) now say `+inv` (were `inventory`).
- **Baseline ratchet shrunk:** regenerated `tests/data/command_convention_baseline.json` via `tools/gen_command_convention_baseline.py` — **133→132 collisions** (`alias:online` is resolved by deleting the `online` synonym from both who-commands); the 9 run-on stems are unchanged; `tests/test_command_convention_invariant.py` stays green.
- **`tests/test_command_syntax_drop1.py` (8 tests):** canonical `+`-forms resolve to their own key; every deleted form is gone (`registry.has_exact` — no prefix matching); bare `inv` no longer reaches the inventory command; `who` is a single canonical command (no stray `who` key); the merge preserves location+status (`_who_player_status` exists, help advertises location); the channel helper is removed; `alias:online` is no longer a live collision. Updated the 3 smoke scenarios that drove bare `who` → `+who` (`tests/smoke/scenarios/foundation.py`, `tests/smoke/scenarios/movement.py`). No schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean.

### 2026-06-17 — QA L1: Insight trial requires Saro dialogue first (Sonnet loop) — *drop qa-l1-insight-saro-required*
Closes QA finding **L1** from `docs/design/QA_FINDINGS_2026-06-16.md`.
- **Root cause:** `engine/village_trials.py::accuse_insight_fragment` fell back to `correct = 2` (hardcoded) when `village_trial_insight_correct_fragment` was 0, meaning a player who skipped the Elder Saro Veck dialogue and guessed `accuse fragment_2` would instantly pass the Trial of Insight — no roleplay required.
- **Fix:** when `correct == 0` (Saro not yet consulted), the function now blocks with "Before making your accusation you must speak with Elder Saro Veck at the Council Hut." The Saro check is moved **before** the attempt counter so blocked attempts do not count against the player.
- **`tests/test_qa_l1_insight_saro_required.py` (7 tests):** block without Saro (all three fragment choices); correct fragment not passing without Saro; attempt counter stays 0 when blocked; correct/wrong behavior unchanged after Saro consulted; drift guard asserting `correct = 2` fallback no longer exists in source. No schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean, single-file change.

### 2026-06-17 — QA M4 + L3: on_planet_visited wired + advance_skill dead branch removed (Sonnet loop) — *drop qa-m4-l3-planet-achievement*
Closes QA findings **M4** and **L3** from `docs/design/QA_FINDINGS_2026-06-16.md`.
- **M4 (`on_planet_visited` never called):** The "Galaxy Traveler" achievement (visit 4 unique non-Tatooine planets, `data/achievements.yaml`) was permanently stuck at 0% — `engine/achievements.py::on_planet_visited` existed but was never called from anywhere. Additionally the hook used the additive `check_achievement` path with `count=planets_count` (the TOTAL), which would have accumulated counts multiplicatively on every landing, overshooting the trigger threshold. Fix (two parts): (1) `on_planet_visited` now uses the high-water-mark pattern (same as `on_room_visited`) — iterates `_BY_EVENT["planets_visited"]` directly, SETs progress to the total count, and awards/upserts correctly. (2) `parser/space_commands.py LandCommand.execute` now calls `on_planet_visited` (via a guarded block after the `on_planet_land` call) for all non-Tatooine landings, reading `planets_visited` count from `char["attributes"]` (already updated by `on_planet_land`). No schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean.
- **L3 (dead if-branch in `advance_skill`):** `engine/character.py::advance_skill` had a misleading docstring claiming "If skill is above attribute, cost is doubled" and a dead no-op if-branch (`if current_bonus.dice > 0: cost = total_pool.dice`) that assigned the same value already set on the line above — WEG R&E never doubles CP cost above attribute; cost is simply total-dice-count. Removed the dead branch and corrected the docstring.
- **`tests/test_qa_m4_l3_planet_achievement.py` (14 tests):** Source guards (on_planet_visited uses `_BY_EVENT` not `check_achievement`; uses `_upsert_progress`; LandCommand references `on_planet_visited` and `planets_visited`; advance_skill has no doubled-claim or dead branch); plus functional tests (advance_skill cost at base/bonus/high-bonus; on_planet_visited awards at count≥4, no award below 4, idempotent on repeat calls). No schema change, era-clean.

### 2026-06-17 — QA M3: shop stock works on bare-list inventory + canonical `coerce_inventory` (Opus loop) — *drop qa-m3-shop-bare-list*
Closes QA finding **M3** from `docs/design/QA_FINDINGS_2026-06-16.md` end-to-end, plus a discovered baseline-red test fix.
- **Root cause:** the `characters.inventory` column has two valid on-disk shapes — dict-form `{"items":[...],"resources":[...]}` (written by the crafting helpers + `db.add_to_inventory`) and a **bare list** `[item, ...]` (the column's schema default is `'[]'`, so every fresh char and any char that only ever held general items carries a bare list). The player-shop stock path assumed dict-form everywhere and called `.get()` on the parsed inventory; on a bare list that raises `AttributeError`, which the surrounding `except` swallowed → `shop stock <item>` reported **"not found"** for an item the character was visibly carrying. Even when found, the removal step crashed the same way. Fresh characters (the common case) were the worst hit.
- **Fix:** new canonical pure helper `engine.items.coerce_inventory(raw)` normalizes any inventory value (JSON str / dict / bare list / None / garbage) into the dict shape with two guaranteed list fields — mirrors `db._get_inventory_raw` but operates on the in-hand char dict (no DB round-trip). Rewired the three shop/vendor sites that had the bug: `parser/shop_commands.py::_find_in_inventory` (the QA-flagged "not found" site), `engine/vendor_droids.py::stock_droid` (both the resource-decrement and general-item removal branches — the downstream crash), and `engine/vendor_droids.py::_is_faction_issued` (same latent class; previously fail-safe). A bare-list inventory is normalized to dict-form on write-back, the same shape crafting/`add_to_inventory` already persist — no new on-disk shape, all readers already tolerate dict-form.
- **Drive-by:** fixed a pre-existing baseline-red in `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_f.py::test_force_detector_stays_out` — the new "Rein**force**d Salvage Arm" Wildspace-mod schematic name tripped a naive `"force" in name` substring ban (intended to bar a Force *detector*); added a "reinforced" exemption mirroring the existing "force_pike" one. Test-only, zero production change.
- **`tests/test_qa_m3_shop_bare_list_inventory.py` (19 tests):** `coerce_inventory` shape matrix (str/dict/bare-list/None/garbage/non-list field values); `_find_in_inventory` finds a general item in a bare-list inventory + resource in dict-form + skips faction-issued; `stock_droid` removes a general item end-to-end from a bare-list inventory + decrements a resource stack (dict-form path still works). No schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean.

### 2026-06-17 — QA M1 + L4: LandCommand safety — emergency landing + hyperspace guard (Sonnet loop) — *drop qa-m1-l4-land-safety*
Closes QA findings **M1** and **L4** from `docs/design/QA_FINDINGS_2026-06-16.md`. Both are loop-safe `parser/space_commands.py` LandCommand fixes.
- **M1 (pilot stranded in space):** LandCommand hard-refused landing when `credits < docking_fee` (25cr base), permanently stranding any pilot who spent credits while in orbit. Fixed with an emergency-landing path: `actual_fee = min(credits, docking_fee)`; if `actual_fee < docking_fee`, pilot gets a warning message and lands for free (or charges whatever is available); the success broadcast uses `actual_fee` so the fee is accurate. No pilot can ever be stranded in space by a lack of docking credits.
- **L4 (hyperspace guard):** LandCommand had no `in_hyperspace` check; landing mid-jump would set `docked_at` while `in_hyperspace=True` simultaneously — an impossible ship state that would mis-teleport on the next tick. Fixed: `_get_systems(ship)` is called immediately after the pilot check, and `in_hyperspace=True` returns an error before any bay lookup or credit deduction.
- **`tests/test_qa_m1_l4_land_safety.py` (9 tests):** Source-inspection drift guards (L4 guard present; M1 emergency-landing path present, no hard refusal; `actual_fee` variable present; success message uses `actual_fee`); plus a harness regression confirming the normal launch+land arc with sufficient credits still works. No schema change, no faucet/sink imbalance, era-clean.

### 2026-06-17 — QA H4: planet-trade pricing/supply restored — `land` keeps `current_zone` (Opus loop) — *drop qa-h4-land-current-zone*
Closes QA finding **H4** (loop-safe per `docs/design/QA_FINDINGS_2026-06-16.md`). The planet-trade economy was silently dead in production: `parser/space_commands.py` `LandCommand` popped `systems["current_zone"]` on every land, but the docked trade surface (`market` / cargo `buy` / cargo `sell`) resolves *which planet you're docked at* via `current_zone → ZONES[zone].planet`. With the zone gone, the next docked trade read an **empty** planet →
- `get_planet_price(good, "")` collapsed to a flat base price (the source-discount + demand-premium that make trade routes profitable never applied — every market quoted a flat 100%); and
- `SUPPLY_POOL.available("", key)` was gated behind `if planet:` → the per-planet supply cap (the anti-infinite-cargo-farming sink) was **bypassed**.
- **Fix:** stop clearing `current_zone` on land. A docked ship is already excluded from all space traffic / targeting by the `docked_at IS NOT NULL` filter (`db.get_ships_in_space` feeds `engine/npc_space_traffic`), so the zone never needed clearing — and keeping it (= the orbit zone we dropped from, == the planet whose bay we docked at) lets docked trade resolve the planet. `launch` overwrites `current_zone` fresh on the next departure. No extra DB write on land, no redundant `docked_planet` state, no schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean.
- **`tests/test_qa_h4_land_preserves_current_zone.py` (5 tests):** live boarding→pilot→launch→land harness arc asserts the landed ship still carries a non-empty, planet-resolvable `current_zone`; plus a source drift-guard pinning that `LandCommand` never re-introduces a `current_zone` pop. This is the end-to-end land→trade coverage whose absence let the bug hide behind the green suite.

### 2026-06-17 — PRELAUNCH.web_landing_retention: portal landing accuracy fixes (Sonnet loop) — *drop web-landing-planet-accuracy*
Closes `PRELAUNCH.web_landing_retention`. The portal landing page had two factual accuracy bugs.
- **`static/portal.html` landing desc:** "Tatooine, Nar Shaddaa, Kessel, and Corellia" → "Tatooine, Coruscant, Nar Shaddaa, Geonosis, Kamino, and Kuat" (Kessel and Corellia have no world YAML in `data/worlds/clone_wars/planets/`; the six actual launch planets are now named).
- **`server/web_portal.py` `handle_stats`:** Hardcoded `"planets": 4` corrected to `6` (the actual planet YAML count).
- **`tests/test_web_landing_accuracy.py` (4 tests):** Guards phantom-world absence (Kessel/Corellia not in landing copy), actual-planet presence, YAML count == stat constant, and expected 6-planet count. No engine change, no schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean.

Allowlists: `<!-- lint-era-ok -->` markers (deliberate CW-vantage foreshadowing in Guide_04) + the WEG D6 scale-18 `Death Star scale` mechanics table row in Guide_01 (clearly labelled "no such weapon exists in the Clone Wars era"). ### 2026-06-16 — QA launch-blocker fixes B2 + B3 (loop-safe pair) — *drop qa-blockers-b2-b3* (Opus loop)
Fixes two VERIFIED launch blockers from `docs/design/QA_FINDINGS_2026-06-16.md`, both flagged loop-safe.
**B2 — all weapon vendors dead (buy-gear credit SINK inert):** `engine/npc_loader.py::_build_ai_config` built `ai_config_json` from a fixed whitelist with NO `vendor` pass-through, so an NPC's `vendor: true` (declared under `ai_config:` in YAML — verified in mos_eisley, southern-underground, craft-armorer, def-civilians, nar-shaddaa, planets/*) was silently dropped at the DB-write seam. The buy consumer (`parser/space_commands.py:4172` `ai_cfg.get("vendor")`) was always falsy → "No merchant here sells weapons." in *every* room incl. Kayson's shop. Added the conditional `vendor` pass-through (same idiom as `trainer`/`is_intel_handler`/`chain_enemy_template`). **B3 — faction comms reach 0 recipients:** `server/channels.py::get_faction` read `char["faction"]` / `attrs["faction"]`, but membership lives in the `faction_id` column (DEFAULT 'independent'); a DB-row-shaped char dict has no `faction` key → every real member collapsed to `independent` → `fcomm` / `faction channel` / leader `faction announce` delivered to nobody. Now reads `char.get("faction_id")` first (the CW org codes republic/cis/jedi_order are in `FACTIONS`, so members resolve); legacy top-level `faction` key + attributes-blob fallback preserved. Both were test-invisible (the systemic stub blind spot the campaign called out): the vendor producer test only checked the YAML source not the DB write; `get_faction` was only ever exercised with hand-built `{"faction": ...}` dicts. `tests/test_qa_blockers_b2_b3.py` (13) exercises the real `_build_ai_config` build→json-roundtrip→consumer-gate path + `faction_id`-shaped rows. No schema change, no faucet/sink imbalance (re-enables an existing sink), era-clean. Lane: both loop-safe (npc_loader + channels; NOT death.py/db core — B1 stays ATTENDED-Opus).

### 2026-06-16 — Command-syntax rework Drop 0: convention enforcement guard — *drop command-convention-guard*
The FOUNDATION drop of the ratified command-syntax rework (`command_syntax_rework_design_v2.md` §"Enforcement guard"). Pure safety net — **no command renames** — so every later canonicalization phase (Drops 1-5) is guarded against silent collisions. This is the guardrail Brian asked for ("make future commands follow our updates").
- **Registry collision instrumentation (`parser/commands.py`):** `CommandRegistry.register()` now records every key/alias collision (a name already bound to a *different* command) in `self._collisions` — the last-wins binding is unchanged (zero behaviour change), but the silent overwrite that bites during canonicalization is now observable. New `collision_signatures` property (sorted unique `"kind:name"`) and `has_exact()` helper (exact key/alias lookup, no prefix matching).
- **One-line boot summary (`server/game_server.py`):** after the registry is built, emits a SINGLE `log.warning` with the collision count (`133` at HEAD) — never per-collision (135 lines would be boot spam / could trip clean-log smoke). Points at the tracked baseline.
- **Convention-invariant ratchet (`tests/test_command_convention_invariant.py`, 13 tests):** builds the full live registry (reusing the single authoritative `_build_full_registry` shared with the `9ca0692` @-access guard — no third copy of the registration list) and asserts the live registry introduces **nothing** beyond the frozen baseline. Two ratchets: (1) no NEW key/alias collision beyond `tests/data/command_convention_baseline.json` (133 collisions); (2) no NEW or reintroduced run-on "smash" stem (the 9 `bountyclaim`/`questaccept`/… stems Drop 2 converts to verb/switch). Plus a synthetic collision-detection-mechanism unit test (so the ratchet can't go vacuous once the baseline reaches zero) and a tripwire that composes — does not duplicate — the @-key↔access invariant.
- **Generated baseline + regenerator (`tests/data/command_convention_baseline.json`, `tools/gen_command_convention_baseline.py`):** the baseline **only shrinks** — regenerate it after each canonicalization drop deletes redundant forms; never add entries to silence a new collision.
- No schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean. Gate: 38 green single-process (convention + admin-access + hygiene + smoke foundation).

### 2026-06-16 — DIFF.5: threat band tinting on area map (Sonnet loop) — *drop diff5-area-map-band*
Closes the last deferred difficulty-tiers item (DIFF.5). The web area map now color-codes room name labels by threat band so players can tell at a glance whether a neighboring zone is safe or dangerous.
- **Server (`engine/area_map.py`):** `build_area_map` now resolves and emits a `band` field on every room node, following the same room→zone inheritance chain as `sec` and `env`. Room-level `threat_band` overrides zone; falls back to zone `threat_band`; defaults to `"settled"` when neither carries the field. Additive, no behavior change to any existing field.
- **Client (`static/client.html`, CSS):** Four new CSS rules add `rm-band-{band}` label coloring: frontier → teal-green (#5ec498); settled → default amber (no class emitted); contested-marches → orange (#ff9048); wilds → red (--warn). CSS cascade order: band rules follow `.rm-adj`, so adjacent rooms show zone difficulty; `.rm-current .rm-label` follows band rules, so the current room always stays accent-bright regardless of band. Far rooms show the band color at the existing 0.3 opacity from G3 dimming.
- **Client (JS `renderAreaMap`):** Adds `rm-band-{band}` class to the room `<g>` (converts `contested_marches` underscores to hyphens for CSS; omits the class for `settled` to keep the default amber).
- **Tests:** `tests/test_diff5_area_map_band.py` (9 tests): room-level frontier/settled/contested_marches/wilds, zone-fallback, room-beats-zone, no-band-defaults-to-settled, all rooms in neighborhood carry the field.
- **No schema change, no faucet/sink, era-clean.**
- **Files:** `engine/area_map.py`, `static/client.html`, `tests/test_diff5_area_map_band.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-16 — Defect-sweep: achievement hooks + intercept fix + destination_slug — *drop defect-sweep-achievements*
Fixes 3 categories of defects found in the June-14 adversarial defect-hunt (findings A1/A2/B1).
- **A1 — 5 dead achievement hooks wired:** `on_item_crafted` (with `quality` arg for masterwork threshold) in `parser/crafting_commands.py` craft-success path; `on_experiment_success` in `ExperimentCommand._handle_success`; `on_trade_goods_sold` in `_handle_sell_cargo` after `adjust_credits`; `on_ship_launch` in `LaunchCommand.execute` after launch broadcast; `on_anomaly_salvaged` in `SalvageCommand.execute` after `remove_anomaly`. All wrapped in canonical try/except that log.debug-swallows. `on_dark_side_atoned` DEFERRED — no DSP-decrement seam exists in the codebase (see design_calls_pending_brian).
- **A2 — intercept achievement call fixed:** `parser/espionage_commands.py:715` — args were mis-ordered (`char` dict as db, `"intercept"` as char_id, `ctx.db` as event). Fixed to `check_achievement(ctx.db, char["id"], "intercept", session=ctx.session)`. Added `signal_hunter` achievement to `data/achievements.yaml` (trigger event `intercept`, count 1, category social, cp_reward 2) so the consumer now has a real producer.
- **B1 — destination_slug now consumed:** `parser/mission_commands.py::_check_ground_destination` — when `active.mission_data` carries a non-empty `destination_slug`, resolves it via `await ctx.db.get_room_by_slug(slug)` and does a precise room-id comparison. Preserves the existing fuzzy-name fallback for missions with no slug (back-compat). `destination_room_id` check still takes priority.
- **Files:** `parser/crafting_commands.py`, `parser/builtin_commands.py`, `parser/space_commands.py`, `parser/espionage_commands.py`, `parser/mission_commands.py`, `data/achievements.yaml`, `tests/test_defect_sweep_achievements.py` (new, 21 tests), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
