### 2026-06-14 — T3.20 live-DB integrity / orphan validator (scope_notes e) — *drop db-integrity-validator*
Fourth T3.20 state-preservation slice (`scope_notes` e — "a DB-integrity validator that can scan a live DB for corruption/orphans before & after a migration"). New `db/integrity.py::scan_integrity(db)` is a READ-ONLY scanner wrapping SQLite's own `PRAGMA integrity_check` (structural corruption) and `PRAGMA foreign_key_check` (every row orphaned by a missing parent, across all 80+ declared `REFERENCES` constraints — no hand-written per-table SQL to drift), returning a structured `IntegrityReport` (corruption list + `OrphanFinding`s, with `.ok` / `.summary()`). Consumer: `tools/check_db_integrity.py <db>` — an operator CLI that prints the report and exits 0 clean / 1 on findings / 2 on a usage error, meant to run BEFORE & AFTER a migration and on any restored backup.
- **Why it's needed even though `foreign_keys=ON` at connect:** enforcement is per-connection and governs only writes made AFTER it is enabled. The orphan/corruption-introducing paths T3.20 cares about bypass it — a table-rebuild migration (the canonical 12-step ALTER recipe toggles `foreign_keys=OFF`), a backup/restore, an offline/manual edit. This is the belt-and-suspenders scan for exactly those.
- **Confirmed clean:** a freshly initialized + seeded DB scans referentially intact (no orphans, no corruption) — a positive launch property now pinned. An orphan introduced the way a migration can (parent dropped with enforcement OFF) is detected and named (`characters -> accounts`).
- **Read-only:** issues only PRAGMA reads, never a write; safe against a live DB.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_db_integrity.py` (6 — pure report helpers + real temp-DB clean-then-orphan detection + fresh-DB corruption-free) + CLI smoke (clean DB -> OK / exit 0) + full-suite gate.
- **Files:** `db/integrity.py` (new), `tools/check_db_integrity.py` (new), `tests/test_db_integrity.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
### 2026-06-14 — T3.20 reload-round-trip invariant for the persisted board/inventory/buff entities — *drop persisted-entity-roundtrip*
Third T3.20 state-preservation slice (`scope_notes` c — "a reload-round-trip invariant test per persisted entity"), extending the Character contract (drop character-reload-roundtrip) to the rest of the durable-state surface: the five board/inventory/buff entities that persist through a `to_dict`/`from_dict` pair. `tests/test_persisted_entity_roundtrip.py` round-trips a fully-populated `ItemInstance` (engine/items.py), `Mission` (engine/missions.py), `BountyContract` (engine/bounty_board.py), `SmugglingJob` (engine/smuggling.py), and `Buff` (engine/buffs.py) two ways — the pure dict contract `from_dict(x.to_dict())` AND the REAL production persist path `from_dict(json.loads(json.dumps(x.to_dict())))` — and, because each is a plain `@dataclass`, asserts via value-based `__eq__` that the WHOLE entity survives, plus the strongest guard: `to_dict` is stable under the round trip. Catches the silent save-data-loss class (a field added to one serializer but not the other, a renamed key, an enum that stops round-tripping, a precision change) that no per-feature test would notice. Test-only; collision-free; 25 tests.
- **Audit outcome — all five contracts CLEAN** (no save-data-loss bug found): every `to_dict` key is restored by `from_dict` under the same name; enum fields (`MissionType`/`MissionStatus`, `BountyTier`/`BountyStatus`, `CargoTier` int-enum / `JobStatus` str-enum) round-trip via `.value` and rebuild to the correct enum TYPE (asserted with `isinstance`, not merely scalar equality). The seeds set non-default values in every field so `to_dict`'s default-omissions and producer quirks are exercised.
- **Two intentional contract details PINNED:** (1) `ItemInstance.to_dict` OMITS the crafter + experiment block when unmodified; `from_dict`'s defaults must reproduce an unmodified instance identically (asserted). (2) `Buff.to_dict` substitutes a title-cased `buff_type` for an EMPTY `display_name`, so a buff saved with `display_name=""` reloads with the derived label — documented producer behavior, now pinned so any change is conscious.
- **Coverage gap closed:** the existing `test_bounty_board_unit` round-trip omits `chain_bounty_id` from its field loop; the new test asserts it survives (the chain_events dispatcher reads it on board.claim to advance the BHG tutorial chain).
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_persisted_entity_roundtrip.py` (25) + full-suite gate.
- **Files:** `tests/test_persisted_entity_roundtrip.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
### 2026-06-14 — T3.20 Character reload-round-trip invariant (the (de)serialization contract) — *drop character-reload-roundtrip*
Second T3.20 state-preservation slice (`scope_notes` c), for the most important persisted entity — a player Character. `tests/test_character_reload_roundtrip.py` builds a Character from a realistic DB row and asserts every CORE field survives a `to_db_dict` → `from_db_dict` round-trip: name/species/template/room/description/CP/FP/DSP/credits/wound_level, every attribute (via the live `ATTRIBUTE_NAMES`), `force_sensitive` + control/sense/alter, skills, and the equipped-weapon/worn-armor keys — plus the strongest guard, that re-serializing the reloaded character reproduces the EXACT same core dict. Catches the silent save-data-loss class where a field is added to one serializer but not the other (or a column key renamed) — drift no per-feature test would notice. Test-only; collision-free.
- **Scope boundary pinned (documented design, not a gap):** `to_db_dict` is the CORE-column serializer; the typed-column extras (`wound_state`, `wound_clear_at`, `village_chosen_path`) and per-slot equipment INSTANCES are written by `save_character` / specific setters, NOT by `to_db_dict` (see engine/character.py). The test asserts the core round-trip; that boundary IS the contract.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_character_reload_roundtrip.py` (7) + full-suite gate.
- **Files:** `tests/test_character_reload_roundtrip.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
### 2026-06-14 — Achievements: wire `on_scene_completed` so `storyteller` can fire — *drop scene-achievement-hook*
Second engine-side fix of the defect-hunt's "achievement hooks defined but never called" findings (A1). `engine/achievements.py::on_scene_completed` was never emitted, so `storyteller` (social, +3 CP, complete 5 RP scenes) was unwinnable. The defect-hunt mapped this hook to `parser/scene_commands.py`, but the completion is actually ENGINE-side — `engine/scenes.py::stop_scene` is what sets `status='completed'` (the parser `+scene/stop` just calls it) — so the emit is parallel-safe.
- **Fix (`engine/scenes.py::stop_scene`):** after the scene is marked complete and IC pose counts tallied, emit `on_scene_completed(db, pid)` for **every IC participant** (the `pose_counts` keys), not just whoever ran `+scene/stop` — they all completed the scene. `check_achievement` count-increments (+1) and is idempotent (`if completed: continue`), so each completed scene advances `storyteller` once per participant toward 5. `try/except` graceful-drop so a hook failure can't break the scene stop; `stop_scene` has no session, so it records silently.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_scene_achievement_hook.py` (2 — stop_scene awards every IC poser; a hook exception does NOT break the stop and the result is intact) + scene subsystem regression green (33). Confirmed `storyteller`/`scene_completed` is a real consumer in `data/achievements.yaml`.
- **Files:** `engine/scenes.py`, `tests/test_scene_achievement_hook.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-14 — Achievements: wire `on_org_rank_reached` so `faction_loyalist` can fire — *drop org-rank-achievement-hook*
Fixes one of the overnight defect-hunt's "achievement hooks defined but never called" findings (`HANDOFF_defect_hunt_findings_2026-06-14.md` A1) — the one with an **engine-side** emit seam (the rest seam into `parser/`, the command-syntax session's lane). `engine/achievements.py::on_org_rank_reached` existed but **nothing ever called it**, so `faction_loyalist` (social, +5 CP, trigger `org_rank_reached` count 3) was **unwinnable**.
- **Fix (`engine/organizations.py::promote`):** emit `await on_org_rank_reached(db, char["id"], next_level)` right after the promotion is persisted + logged. Both manual `promote` and `check_auto_promote` (which calls `promote`) flow through this one point, so a single emit covers both paths. The hook is a high-water-mark + idempotent (its own `if completed: continue` guard), so firing on every promotion is safe. Lazy import + `try/except` graceful-drop so an achievement-subsystem hiccup can never block a promotion. `promote()` carries no session, so the achievement records silently (the player sees it in their list) — no signature change, no parser-seam edit, parallel-safe.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_org_rank_achievement_hook.py` (3 — promote emits the hook with the new rank level; a hook exception does NOT block the promotion (rank still persisted); a no-op promotion at max rank does NOT fire the hook) + organizations/achievements regression green (64 — rewicker boundary, profession achievements, achievements unit). Confirmed `faction_loyalist`/`org_rank_reached` is a real consumer in `data/achievements.yaml` (not a phantom emit).
- **Files:** `engine/organizations.py`, `tests/test_org_rank_achievement_hook.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-14 — Ollama ambient-flavor feeder: the idle GPU enriches rooms — *drop ambient-flavor-feeder*
First **enrichment** drop on the era-guard substrate (after the 4 era-guard drops): puts the idle local GPU to work generating atmospheric room ambient lines, the free local analogue of the Director's *paid* `ambient_pool` — and valuable precisely because the Director path is gated on API credits/billing on Brian's box.
- **New `engine/idle_queue.py::AmbientFlavorTask`** — during GPU idle, Ollama pre-generates 5 short ambient room lines per zone (era-framed with `ERA_PROMPT_HINT`, JSON array, fence-tolerant parse). Seeded by piggybacking the existing `seed_barks_for_populated_rooms` (run ~4h via `bark_seed_tick`): one task per occupied **zone** (deduped via a `seeded_zones` set + an `idle_pool_needs_refresh` gate), resolving the zone key through the ambient manager's own `_get_zone_key`. No new tick, no server-file edit.
- **`engine/ambient_events.py::set_idle_pool`** — ingest boundary: validates + **era-guards** (shared `engine.era_validator` via a new `_validate_lines` helper that `set_dynamic_pool` now also uses — no duplicated filter) + length- and count-caps (`MAX_IDLE_LINES_PER_ZONE`) the generated lines into a **new `_idle_pool`, SEPARATE from the Director's `_dynamic_pool`** so the two LLM writers never clobber (the Director `.clear()`s its pool every Faction Turn). Always stamps the refresh timestamp (even when every line is dropped) so a garbage-producing zone isn't re-hammered.
- **`_pick_line`** now draws its 30% "live" line from the Director dynamic + Ollama idle pools **combined** (a fresh concatenated list — no pool mutation); the 70% static path and `None`-fallback are unchanged.
- **Fail-safe throughout:** generation runs in the already-exception-guarded idle task; the seeding block is in its own try/except inside the bark loop; bad/empty/non-list JSON safely no-ops; off-era lines are dropped at ingest (static pool still covers the zone). No credit/dice/influence/YAML surface.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_ambient_flavor_feeder.py` (11 — era-guard on ingest, separate-pool no-clobber, count cap, all-off-era→no-pool-but-ts-stamped, refresh logic, `_pick_line` draws from idle / combines both pools, task feeds era-guarded pool, bad-JSON-safe, enqueue dedup) + ambient/idle/era regression green (93 passed) + boot import (no cycle) + code-reviewer & invariant-auditor fan-out clean (chain confirmed non-phantom).
- **Files:** `engine/idle_queue.py`, `engine/ambient_events.py`, `tests/test_ambient_flavor_feeder.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-14 — Space encounters: fix skill-check funnel bypass (checks ignored character skill) — *drop encounter-skillcheck-funnel*
Fixes an always-on funnel-bypass bug found by the overnight defect-hunt sweep. `engine/encounter_{anomaly,hunter,patrol,pirate,texture}.py::_skill_check` invoked the funnel as `await perform_skill_check(char_id=char_id, skill_name=…, difficulty=…, db=db)` — but `engine.skill_checks.perform_skill_check` is **synchronous** and takes the char **dict** positionally with **no `char_id`/`db` params**. So the call **always raised**, and every space-encounter skill check silently fell back to **raw 3D, ignoring the character's actual skill** (and reported `roll` 0 via the wrong result-field names `roll_total`/`critical`). A skilled pilot and a green recruit had identical odds on every transponder bluff, sensor sweep, contraband-hide, and pursuit check.
- **Not a balance change:** the encounter difficulty values are standard WEG D6 (15 = Moderate, 20 = Difficult) — designed for *real* skill checks, not raw 3D. The raw-3D behavior was purely the accidental result of the broken call; fixing it makes the checks resolve as those difficulties always intended.
- **Fix (all 5 helpers):** load the char via `await db.get_character(char_id)`, call `perform_skill_check(char, skill_name, difficulty)` correctly (sync, positional), and map the real result fields (`.success`, `.critical_success`, `.roll`; patrol also `.fumble`). The genuine-exception fallback to raw 3D is **retained but now LOUD** (`log.warning(..., exc_info=True)`) instead of silently swallowing.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_encounter_skillcheck_funnel.py` (4 — across all 5 modules: a 12D skill beats difficulty 22 with a real roll **>18** which raw-3D could never produce; 1D fails difficulty 28; missing-char falls back to raw-3D without raising; patrol keeps its `fumble` key) + encounter-module regression green (133 passed / 5 xfailed). Parallel-safe: `engine/encounter_*.py` are in neither live session's avoid-set.
- **Files:** `engine/encounter_anomaly.py`, `engine/encounter_hunter.py`, `engine/encounter_patrol.py`, `engine/encounter_pirate.py`, `engine/encounter_texture.py`, `tests/test_encounter_skillcheck_funnel.py` (new), `docs/design/HANDOFF_defect_hunt_findings_2026-06-14.md` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`.

### 2026-06-14 — Breaching: report honest failure when obstacle removal fails (no false breach success) — *drop breaching-delete-failsafe*
Fixes a silent-swallow defect found by the overnight defect-hunt sweep. `engine/breaching.py::attempt_breach`, on a *successful* Demolitions check, called `await db.delete_object(obstacle["id"])` inside a `try/except` that only logged a warning and then fell through to the **"The charge blows %s open!"** success return — so if the delete raised (DB error), the obstacle stayed in the room while the player was told the breach succeeded (the way "clear" but still blocked).
- **Fix:** the delete-exception branch now returns an honest `breached: False` result ("the charge detonates… but the way is still blocked; the rubble couldn't be cleared; try again") instead of falling through to the success return — mirroring the skill-check-failure branch directly above it. Engine-only; the parser caller already renders `result["msg"]`/`breached`.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_breaching.py::TestAttemptBreach::test_delete_failure_reports_honest_failure_not_false_success` (passing demolitions + a `delete_object` that raises → `breached` is False, no "blows open" line, obstacle still present) + full breaching suite green (10).
- **Files:** `engine/breaching.py`, `tests/test_breaching.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-14 — Era-cleanness blocker: gate off-era GCW profession chains in tutorial_v2 — *drop tutorial-v2-era-remediation*
Closes a **live, uncaught B3 era-cleanness violation** found by the overnight defect-hunt sweep. `engine/tutorial_v2.py` predates this deployment settling on the Clone Wars era and carried two wholesale Galactic-Civil-War profession chains — **`REBEL_CELL`** (Rebel Alliance recruitment via "Fulcrum") and **`IMPERIAL_SERVICE`** (Imperial Service under "Sergeant Kreel") — plus scattered off-era barks in the live chains. The dispatch (`check_profession_chains`) is **wired into production** (`parser/mission_commands.py`, `npc_commands.py` `talk_rebel_contact`, `smuggling_commands.py`, `space_commands.py`), and the chains gated only on `missions_complete >= 2` with **no era check**, so a Clone Wars player who finished 2 missions was offered Rebel/Imperial onboarding. An AST scan found **53 banned-era-token strings** in the file.
- **Why it was missed:** the existing era-cleanness test (`tests/test_laneb_era_cleanness.py`) is deliberately *surgical* — a curated `(file, string)` list — and never scanned `tutorial_v2.py`. Same partial-coverage blind spot the wilderness/chain reachability drops hit.
- **Mitigation (reversible, content-preserving):** new module flag `_GCW_PROFESSION_CHAINS_ENABLED = False` gates `_can_start_rebel_cell` / `_can_start_imperial_service` to `False` **and** hides both rows from `get_chain_status_lines` — the two chains are now **unstartable + invisible** in CW. Their definitions/dispatch remain in source (unreachable) so the permanent disposition is non-destructive (logged as design call `ERA.tutorial_v2_gcw_profession_chains`: delete vs keep-dormant vs CW-rewrite).
- **Live barks reworded to CW-clean flavor:** Nar Shaddaa "No Imperials" → "No patrols"; Kessel "The Empire controls the spice mines" → "The Hutt cartels…"; Corellia "officially Imperial territory / Rebel sympathizers" → "officially Republic territory / independents keep their heads down"; Smuggler's Run "evading an Imperial patrol" → "…a Republic customs patrol"; Kessa's "Imperial liaison work" teaser → "courier security contracts".
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_tutorial_v2_era_cleanness.py` (5 — walks every LIVE chain object with NO allow-list and asserts era-clean; pins both GCW chains unstartable for a maxed char; asserts `get_chain_status_lines` is era-clean and omits the two chains while still rendering Smuggler's Run). A no-allow-list object walk so future off-era additions to a reachable chain fail. No existing test referenced these chains (they were untested). Targeted regression green (9).
- **Files:** `engine/tutorial_v2.py`, `tests/test_tutorial_v2_era_cleanness.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-14 — Director economy prompt-tuning: teach the LLM the economy block + the spend advisory — *drop director-economy-prompt*
Closes the two `director_scope_and_adaptive_spend_v1.md` prompt follow-ups noted by the economy-eyes + adaptive-spend-slice-2 drops. The Director already COMPILED the `digest['economy']` faucet/sink rollup and PARSED an optional `recommend_fidelity` advisory — but the LLM was never told either exists, so it couldn't use them. This wires the prompt side (pure `data/worlds/clone_wars/director_config.yaml` edit, additive; no engine change; collision-free).
- **ECONOMY section:** describes the `economy` digest block (total_faucet/total_sink/net_flow/transactions/top_faucets/top_sinks) and instructs the LLM to seed OPPORTUNITIES from it (smuggling/trade boom → caravans + rare buyers; a wealth-heavy window → fences/bounties/faction courtship; a quiet market → a caravan) — explicitly **NEVER manipulate prices/yields or tax wealth** (Brian decision A/B; consistent with the deterministic `_seed_economic_opportunities` seeder and the long-standing "events create OPPORTUNITIES, never OBLIGATIONS" principle).
- **SPEND ADVISORY section (decision F):** tells the LLM it MAY return the optional `recommend_fidelity` field (eco/standard/high/max + reason) on high-stakes moments — which `_set_recommend_fidelity` already parses and `@director status`/`@director fidelity` already surface. This makes slice 2's advisory channel functional end-to-end (the LLM now knows the field exists).

### 2026-06-14 — T3.20 migration-framework safety harness + additive-fields concern closed — *drop migration-framework-harness*
First slice of T3.20 state-preservation (`launch_criteria`: every schema change must have a tested, data-preserving path). A GENERAL guard over the migration framework — distinct from the existing per-feature schema tests — plus a HEAD-verification that closes a flagged-but-false launch concern. Test-only; no engine/schema change; collision-free.
- **Static framework integrity (`tests/test_migration_framework_integrity.py`):** the headline guard asserts `SCHEMA_VERSION == max(MIGRATIONS)` — the classic silent bug where a migration is added but the version isn't bumped, so it never runs on a live DB (`current_version` already exceeds the key). Plus: no migration key above `SCHEMA_VERSION` (orphaned/never-runs), every value is a list of real SQL strings (an EMPTY list is allowed — a reserved version the framework skips via `if not stmts`), keys are ints in range.
- **Boot re-entrancy / data preservation (real temp-file `Database`):** a fresh `initialize()` reaches `SCHEMA_VERSION`; and the production reboot path — `initialize()` re-run on an already-current, POPULATED DB (it runs `SCHEMA_SQL` + the version-gated migrations every startup) — preserves a seeded account+character unchanged, leaves the version at 44, and does NOT duplicate the `schema_version` row.
- **Deliberately NOT tested (design nuance):** re-running EVERY migration against a populated DB. The 8 data-backfill statements in `MIGRATIONS` (e.g. the `mail_v33` INSERT) are intentionally once-only behind the `schema_version` gate; re-applying them is a non-scenario that would falsely flag idempotency. The realistic safety property is the reboot no-op (tested above).
- **Closed a false launch concern (HEAD-verified):** the readiness review's "additive persisted fields shipped on schema 43 without a bump (chain `kind`, questline slots, zone `threat_band`, encounter `min_band`/`max_band`) need a save backfill" is **not a bug.** All are config/world-YAML or definition fields read with explicit defaults (`zp.get("threat_band")`, `e.get("min_band", 1)`, `cb.get("kind") or "tutorial"`, `getattr(c, "kind", "tutorial")`), regenerated each load — nothing is persisted per-save, so there is nothing to backfill. Real column additions DO go through sequential `ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN ... DEFAULT` migrations (verified 30->44).
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_migration_framework_integrity.py` (6) + full-suite gate.
- **Files:** `tests/test_migration_framework_integrity.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
### 2026-06-13 — NPC dialogue: era-guard the primary `talk <npc>` LLM path — *drop npc-dialogue-era-guard*
Closes the era hole on the **highest-traffic** LLM→player surface: `ai/npc_brain.py::NPCBrain.dialogue()` returned the local model's output straight to the player with **no era check**, and its system prompt said only "in a Star Wars setting" (no era → Mistral's GCW-saturated default). Every `talk <npc>` exchange could surface the Empire, stormtroopers, TIEs, or canonical figures.
- **Both halves of the guard (same pattern as the idle-queue + ambient drops):** `_build_system_prompt` now leads with the shared `ERA_PROMPT_HINT` (Clone Wars ~20 BBY framing — the positive half) and drops the era-unspecified "in a Star Wars setting" identity phrasing; `dialogue()` runs the generated line through `engine.era_validator.era_violations()` (the negative half) and, on a leak, speaks a canned in-era `fallback_line` instead — and **never persists** the off-era line to `npc_memory`.
- **Bonus correctness fix:** the fallback is now chosen **once** and reused for both the era-guard and the memory-save guard. Previously `dialogue()` called `self._get_fallback()` (a `random.choice`) twice — once as `generate(fallback_text=…)` and again in the `response != self._get_fallback()` memory-save check — so on an AI-down turn the two random picks could mismatch and a fallback line could be saved to memory as if it were real dialogue. One stable `fallback` closes that.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_npc_brain_era_guard.py` (7 — off-era token & canonical-figure responses → fallback; clean response passes through; off-era not persisted / clean persisted via a memory-save spy; system prompt carries "Clone Wars" and drops the GCW phrasing) + `test_npc_dialogue_cleanup` regression green (31 together) + boot import.

### 2026-06-13 — Ambient dynamic pool: era-guard the LLM→player boundary — *drop ambient-dynamic-pool-era-guard*
Closes the **second** live LLM-output-reaches-players-without-an-era-check hole (the first was the Ollama idle queue, closed in `ollama-era-guard`). `engine/ambient_events.py::AmbientEventManager.set_dynamic_pool` ingests the Director's LLM-generated `ambient_pool` lines and serves them to **every player in a room** via the ambient tick. The Director (`director.py:1093-1106`) filters length, game-command keywords, and online-player names — but **not era** — so a Haiku-generated GCW leak ("Imperial patrols increase…") would surface to players unfiltered.
- **Fix (boundary discipline):** `set_dynamic_pool` now drops any line failing the shared `engine.era_validator.era_violations()` guard before it enters the dynamic pool, logging the drop count. The static `data/ambient_events.yaml` pool still covers the zone, so a dropped line just shrinks the dynamic variety — never an empty room. Same guard, same single-source canon as the idle-queue tasks; the length/keyword filters are unchanged.
- **Found + LOGGED (not fixed here): `TD.AMBIENT_INJECT_ONCE_PHANTOM`.** `engine/director.py:1490` calls `get_ambient_manager().inject_once(content)` for `delivery=="ambient"` narrative beats, but `AmbientEventManager` has **no `inject_once` method** — so that branch always raises `AttributeError` and silently falls back to a comlink. The whole Director "ambient delivery" path is dead. Reviving it changes room-wide visibility/zone-targeting semantics that live in `director.py` (a different active lane), so it's logged for a focused, coordinated fix rather than guessed at.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_ambient_era_guard.py` (6 — off-era token lines dropped, canonical-figure line dropped, all-off-era zone absent, clean lines preserved, length filter still applies, empty clears) + ambient regression incl. the static byte-equivalence guard (`test_f6a4_int_byte_equivalence`) and singleton-bindings green (63 passed together) + AST/import validation.

### 2026-06-13 — Director adaptive-spend slice 2: manual `@director fidelity` toggle + `recommend_fidelity` advisory — *drop director-fidelity-slice2*
Completes the adaptive-spend governor (`director_scope_and_adaptive_spend_v1.md` §5; Brian decisions E/F/G) on top of slice 1's auto-governor. Admins can now SEE and OVERRIDE the cadence governor, and the Director can FLAG a high-ROI window for more spend — the "Director recommends its own spend" idea. No schema change; spend stays bounded by the `ClaudeProvider` circuit breaker regardless of the pinned tier. Parser lane verified clear before editing.
- **Manual override (`DirectorAI.set_manual_fidelity`, surfaced via `@director fidelity <tier|auto>`):** pins `_turn_interval` to a `FIDELITY_INTERVALS` tier (`eco`/`standard`/`high`/`max`) — including the manual-only `max` ($40 burst / 15-min) tier the auto-governor never reaches (decision E/G) — or `auto` hands control back to the slice-1 governor. Applied immediately, validated, case-insensitive. In-memory (a restart reverts to AUTO — persistence is a noted follow-up; there is no general director-state kv table and this drop deliberately does not bump the schema).
- **LLM advisory (`DirectorAI._set_recommend_fidelity`, decision F):** `_run_api_turn` now reads an optional `recommend_fidelity` field from the Director's response (a bare tier or `{tier, reason}`), validates it against `FIDELITY_INTERVALS`, and stores it as a momentary admin-facing flag (a turn that doesn't recommend clears the stale advisory). **Advisory ONLY — it never auto-acts on the live cadence** (guarded by `TestSlice2DoesNotAutoAct`).
- **Observability (`@director status` + `@director fidelity`):** both render `governor_state()` — tier / interval / auto-vs-manual / reason — plus any standing `recommend_fidelity` advisory, so an admin can see what the governor is doing and what the Director would spend on.
- **Post-review fixes (2 MAJOR caught by code-reviewer, both now guarded by tests):** (1) the empty-server *skip* path in `_governed_turn` no longer clobbers `_turn_interval` to `eco` when a manual tier is pinned (a skip must not silently demote a pin); (2) `set_manual_fidelity` now normalizes case *before* the clear-path check so `"AUTO"`/`"OFF"` (and surrounding whitespace) correctly clear the pin via the public method, not just the pre-lowercased parser path. Plus a log-accuracy nit (clear vs set).

### 2026-06-13 — Agent Skills: `stat-d6` + `world-yaml` for inline main-session work — *drop claude-skills*
Adds the project's first `.claude/skills/` — the richer **Agent Skills** format (a `SKILL.md` per skill, auto-surfaced by `description` match with progressive disclosure), distinct from the existing agents (isolated, must be spawned) and `/`-commands (manual end-of-drop rituals). Slash commands have been merged into skills upstream, so the four `.claude/commands/*.md` are already legacy-format skills; these two are the first to use the format's net-new capabilities — **auto-invocation** and **on-demand detail** — for the main session's *inline* D6/world work, which the spawn-only agents never reach.
- **`stat-d6`** (`.claude/skills/stat-d6/SKILL.md`) — the canonical WEG R&E D6 statting/authoring procedure surfaced into the main context: provenance re-stat (WotC = lore-only), the WEG40120 sidecar→PDF lookup-and-cite ritual, the three funnel functions verified at HEAD (`adjust_credits`@`db/database.py`, `perform_skill_check`@`engine/skill_checks.py`, `adjust_territory_influence`@`engine/territory.py`), faucet/sink pairing, `force_sensitive`-is-derived (never a `save_character` kwarg — the `_CHARACTER_WRITABLE_COLUMNS` allowlist rejects it), the no-phantom-consumer rule (match `engine/npc_loader.py` / `engine/items.py`), era cleanness B3, and the validate-before-handback step. The `content-author` agent is its bulk/parallel counterpart; the skill is its inline-main-session twin.
- **`world-yaml`** (`.claude/skills/world-yaml/SKILL.md`, `paths`-scoped to `data/worlds/**`) — the safe-edit procedure for world/map YAML: additive-only (zero deleted lines), comment-preserving string-replacement (NEVER a yaml round-trip), don't-move pinned coordinates, match-a-live-consumer, and the right post-edit validator (`tools/check_map_cardinals.py` for exit graphs, `tools/verify_tutorial_chains.py` for chains). Proactive partner to the reactive deletion-blocking `world_yaml_additive_guard.py` hook — teaches the correct technique so the hook never has to fire.
- **Guard test** `tests/test_claude_skills_integrity.py` (new) — validates every `SKILL.md`'s frontmatter (`name` == dir, non-empty `description` ≤ 1536-char cap, `paths` shape) and that every concrete repo file a skill references actually exists at HEAD (the no-phantom-consumer invariant applied to tooling; skips the gitignored `docs/sourcebooks/` tree and glob/illustrative tokens).
- **Discoverability:** `CLAUDE.md` agent-roster section gains a short Skills subsection.
- **Verified:** `tests/test_claude_skills_integrity.py` green (6 tests / 17 subtests); the phantom-reference guard confirms all funnel/loader/validator/doc references resolve. Tooling-only — no engine/runtime surface touched.
- **Files:** `.claude/skills/stat-d6/SKILL.md` (new), `.claude/skills/world-yaml/SKILL.md` (new), `tests/test_claude_skills_integrity.py` (new), `CLAUDE.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`.

### 2026-06-13 — Wilderness encounter spawn counts honor authored ranges (bias low) — *drop encounter-count-range*
Resolves `TD.ENCOUNTER_COUNT_RANGE_IGNORED` (Brian balance ruling: **ship, bias low**). Wilderness encounters author `count` as a `[lo, hi]` range in the region YAMLs, but `engine/creature_library.py::creature_spawn_count` could not parse a list — `int([4, 6])` raised `TypeError`, was swallowed, and **every** ranged encounter silently fell back to the creature `pack_count` minimum (the six-rider Tusken war party fielded 2; `gang_patrol [2,4]` → 2; `maze_ambush [3,5]` → 3). The fix honors the authored spread without a galaxy-wide difficulty spike.
- **Low-biased roll (`engine/creature_library._roll_low_biased`):** `min` of two uniform `randint(lo, hi)` rolls, so the mean sits ~a third up the range (`[4,6]` → ~4.56, vs uniform 5.0, vs the old always-4). It still **frequently spawns the minimum** (so no encounter ever fields *fewer* than before) and caps at the authored `hi` — the difficulty creep is deliberately gentle, per the ruling.
- **`creature_spawn_count` now routes a 2-list `count` through the low-biased roll.** Scalar `count`, no-`count` (pack-min fallback), and solo-default paths are unchanged; a reversed `[hi,lo]` is sorted; a 1-element list is treated as a scalar; a malformed/non-int list falls through to the pack fallback. Chosen so "bias low" is satisfied deterministically with no magic skew constant.
- **Decision provenance:** the count-range quirk was discovered + deliberately deferred by the wilderness-phantom-creatures drop as a conscious balance call (not slipped into a content fix). Brian ruled tonight; recorded in `TODO.json` `design_calls_resolved_recent` → `BALANCE.encounter_spawn_count_range`.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_encounter_count_range.py` (14 — within-bounds over 3k rolls, low-bias mean below the uniform midpoint over 20k rolls, full-range span, the exact "no longer always minimum" bug, reversed/scalar/single-element/malformed/no-count edges, and end-to-end through `spawn_encounter_creatures` honoring `[3,5]`) + `test_lane_a_phase_b_spawner` + `test_wilderness_encounter_template_resolution` regression (34 passed together). Parallel-safe: `engine/creature_library.py` is in neither live session's avoid-set; data/tests otherwise.
- **Files:** `engine/creature_library.py`, `tests/test_encounter_count_range.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — Idle-queue EventRewrite: couple the web broadcast to the DB persist — *drop idle-queue-rewrite-broadcast-guard*
Resolves `TD.IDLE_QUEUE_EVENT_REWRITE_BROADCAST_WITHOUT_PERSIST` — a latent consistency bug in `engine/idle_queue.py::EventRewriteTask.execute` surfaced by the era-guard drop's code-review fan-out. The websocket re-broadcast of a rewritten Director headline was gated only on `self.session_mgr`, a **sibling** of the `if db and self.event_id:` `director_log` UPDATE — so on any path where `db` is falsy or `event_id == 0`, clients would receive the live `news_event` rewrite that was never persisted, then get the **original** headline back on reconnect/reload (contradictory state).
- **Fix (one condition):** the broadcast is now gated on `if self.session_mgr and db and self.event_id:` — the *same* condition as the persist — so a rewrite is broadcast only when it was also written to `director_log` (broadcast implies persist). Production behavior is unchanged (the Director always enqueues with a real `db` + `event_id > 0`); the fix closes the latent path for any future caller.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_idle_queue_event_rewrite.py` (4 — clean path persists *and* broadcasts; `db=None` → no broadcast; `event_id=0` → neither persists nor broadcasts; off-era rewrite → neither, re-confirming the era-guard early-return) + era_validator regression green (19 together).
- **Files:** `engine/idle_queue.py`, `tests/test_idle_queue_event_rewrite.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — Director soft economic NUDGES: act on the economy digest (decision A) — *drop director-economic-nudges*
Step 4 of the Director scope expansion (`director_scope_and_adaptive_spend_v1.md` §4) — the ACTION layer on top of the economy-eyes PERCEPTION that shipped in `director-economy-eyes`. The Director now turns macro economic signals into a SOFT opportunity SEED (Brian decision A): when wealth is piling up or the market is hot, it sends a merchant caravan players can take or ignore. Deterministic + free (no API call), so economic reactivity is always-on, independent of the paid LLM turn. Pure `engine/director.py`; no new seams; zero collision with the parallel content lane.
- **Decision A — seeds, never levers (verified):** the seeder fires exactly ONE event — `merchant_arrival` (`rare_vendor`: a discounted merchant caravan; live consumer `parser/space_commands.py::apply_rare_vendor_discount`) — and is hard-blocked from the price/yield-LEVER events (`trade_boom`/`spice_demand`/`bounty_surge`/`intelligence_thaw`, named in `ECON_FORBIDDEN_LEVER_EVENTS`). It changes no prices/yields/credits directly and adds NO new faucet/sink — it reuses an event already balanced at ship, through the `WorldEventManager.activate_event` seam (whose own cooldown/max-concurrent/no-repeat guards back it). All three opportunity-seed flags (`rare_vendor`/`krayt_bounty`/`hutt_auction`) were grep-verified to have live consumers — no phantom producer.
- **Pure, testable classifier (`DirectorAI._classify_economic_seed`):** maps the economy digest → at most one seed. **wealth_surge** (`total_faucet >= ECON_SURPLUS_RATIO x sink`) and **trade_boom** (`>= ECON_BUSY_TXNS` txns with a commerce-flavored dominant faucet), gated by an `ECON_MIN_FLOW` floor so trivial windows never trigger. Surge beats boom. Thresholds are first-cut/playtest-tunable (lift to config in the T3.19 sweep).
- **Always-on, conservative wiring (`DirectorAI._seed_economic_opportunities`, called from `_governed_turn` after `_safe_faction_turn`):** runs on every executed faction turn, gated on `ECONOMIC_SEED_MIN_PLAYERS` (never seed for an empty server) + a 1h `ECONOMIC_SEED_COOLDOWN_SECONDS`; fail-open (never breaks a turn). A WEM-declined activation does NOT burn the cooldown (retry next window). Logged to `director_log` as `economic_nudge` (a distinct event_type, so it never pollutes the `faction_turn` budget rollup).
- **Noted follow-ups (NOT this drop):** decision-B per-player wealth/power -> content magnet via targeted `pc_hooks` (needs a per-player wealth signal; the macro digest is aggregate); prompt-tuning so the paid LLM turn ALSO leverages `digest["economy"]` (lives in `director_config.yaml`).
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_director_economic_nudges.py` (16 — classifier thresholds, surge>boom, non-commerce/sub-floor None, the decision-A invariant guard, seeder gating/cooldown/fire-on-surge/fire-on-boom/decline-no-burn/fail-open) + 88-test adjacent director-suite regression green (economy-eyes / adaptive-spend / living-galaxy / cw-mapping / bugfixes / rewicker) + full suite 9235 passed (3 pre-existing chain-walkthrough parallel-flakes, all pass solo/serial, unrelated — drop is director.py-only). Post-review hardening: the `log_event` telemetry call is isolated so a log hiccup can't swallow a successful seed (code-reviewer nit).
- **Files:** `engine/director.py`, `tests/test_director_economic_nudges.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — Ollama runtime era-guard: shared `era_validator` + idle-queue output filter — *drop ollama-era-guard*
Closes a live era-cleanness hole in the Ollama idle queue (the GPU-idle content pre-generator wired at `server/game_server.py:381`). Mistral 7B is GCW-saturated and **`HousingDescTask` literally prompted it with "set during the Galactic Civil War era"** in a Clone Wars game, with **no validator between its output and players** — era cleanness was enforced only by tests over *static* strings, which cannot catch text an LLM generates at runtime. This is the runtime era-guard `free_llm_enrichment_roadmap_v1.md` names as STEP 0 / the load-bearing prerequisite.
- **New authority module `engine/era_validator.py` — single source of truth.** Lifts the `_BANNED` GCW-token canon (+ the `_CANONICAL_FIGURES` Q1 list) that previously lived as **two divergent copies** (`tests/test_laneb_era_cleanness.py`, `tools/ingest_lore.py`) into one importable home, exactly as `ingest_lore.py:56`'s own comment requested. Exports `BANNED_ERA_TOKENS`, `CANONICAL_FIGURES`, `era_violations()`/`is_era_clean()` (the runtime drop-gate), and `ERA_PROMPT_HINT` (CW prompt-hardening). Pure stdlib — imports nothing from `engine`, so tools/ + tests import it with no cycle.
- **Both halves of the guard, per the roadmap.** *Positive half:* `ERA_PROMPT_HINT` (Clone Wars ~20 BBY; Republic/CIS; explicit "never the Empire/Imperials/stormtroopers/TIEs; no canonical figures") is prepended to all four idle-queue task prompts so the model generates FROM the era — including the three that were silently era-unspecified (`AmbientBark`/`SceneSummary`/`EventRewrite`), not just the GCW-mislabeled `HousingDesc`. *Negative half:* `era_violations()` filters every generated variant before it caches/serves — barks drop per-line (pool shrinks, static room flavor covers), scene summaries/housing descs/event rewrites drop whole (column stays NULL / cache stays empty / original headline stands). The guard errs toward dropping (case-insensitive substring): a false-drop costs one pool entry, a false-accept leaks off-era text to players.
- **Drift can't reopen:** `test_laneb_era_cleanness.py` and `ingest_lore.py` now `import` the shared tuple; a new `tests/test_era_validator.py` asserts the **identity** (`laneb._BANNED is BANNED_ERA_TOKENS`, same for ingest) so a future private copy fails the suite.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_era_validator.py` (15 — canon membership, drift-identity for both consumers, case-insensitive token + canonical-figure catch, clean-CW-prose passes, and the real fix end-to-end: `AmbientBarkTask`/`HousingDescTask.execute` against a fake AI actually drop off-era output before caching) + migrated `test_laneb_era_cleanness.py` green (22 passed together) + `ingest_lore.py --mock` offline pipeline smoke green + AST/import validation of all touched files. A source regression guard locks "Galactic Civil War" out of `idle_queue.py` for good.
- **Files:** `engine/era_validator.py` (new), `engine/idle_queue.py`, `tools/ingest_lore.py`, `tests/test_laneb_era_cleanness.py`, `tests/test_era_validator.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — Questline graduation infinite re-fire: clear the pending flag from the correct slot — *drop questline-graduation-refire*
Fixes a BLOCKER in the T5 questline graduation path found by an adversarial break-it pass. `engine/chain_graduation.py::execute_pending_teleport` walks both chain slots (onboarding `tutorial_chain` + mid-game `active_questline`) and records `pending_state_key` = the slot the pending-teleport flag was found on. The two early `_clear_pending` calls (bad-data + missing-room bail) correctly pass `pending_state_key`, but the **success-path** call (line 419) omitted it — so `_clear_pending` defaulted to the onboarding slot. For a **questline** graduation the flag lives in `active_questline`, so it was never cleared: `execute_pending_teleport` returned `True` again on every subsequent command, re-firing the "Your training is complete" flavor + a synthetic look **on every command until server restart**.
- **Why onboarding graduation was fine (and the smoke missed it):** an onboarding chain's flag lives in the *default* slot, so the bug only affects questline graduations (the `mastery` / `quest` arc, drops 33-35). The chain-walkthrough smoke only exercises onboarding chains.
- **Fix (engine, parallel-safe, one line):** `engine/chain_graduation.py:419` now passes `pending_state_key` to `_clear_pending` (matching the other two call sites). The flag clears from the slot it was stamped on; `execute_pending_teleport` returns `False` on the next command.
- **Regression test:** `tests/test_f8c2c_chain_graduation.py::TestQuestlinePendingTeleportClearsSlot` — a questline-slot graduation clears `active_questline.pending_drop_room_id`, and a **second** `execute_pending_teleport` call returns `False` with no synthetic look and no re-sent flavor (the exact re-fire the bug caused).
- **Provenance:** break-it adversarial pass (in-process harness) reproduced the re-fire with a three-call confirmation; root-caused to the missing kwarg. The same pass independently re-confirmed `TD.ENCOUNTER_COUNT_RANGE_IGNORED` (left as the logged tech-debt balance decision, not fixed here).
- **Verified:** 83 targeted (graduation + interstep teleport + t5 questline engine/content) green incl. the 2 new tests.
- **Files:** `engine/chain_graduation.py`, `tests/test_f8c2c_chain_graduation.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

Closes an onboarding-chain stranding bug of the same class as the wilderness drop, in the tutorial chains. The `separatist_agent` chain step 4 "Talk past Republic Security" completes primarily on a Con check, with a `combat_won` **fallback** keyed to `enemy_template: republic_security_officer` ("if the bluff fails you'll have to fight," `chains.yaml`). But **no NPC carried `ai_config.chain_enemy_template: republic_security_officer`**, so the combat-won matcher (`engine/chain_events.py::_match_combat_won`) could never fire — a player who failed the bluff and was told to fight was **stranded**. Data + test drop; no engine/parser edits (parallel-safe).

Mirrors the documented `tarko_vinn_petty_smuggler` tag pattern.

It scans the **whole** CW data tree (so it catches tags in the npc manifests AND `tutorial_bounties.yaml`), with an anti-vacuous counter. The existing Class 1–4 (rooms/completion-types/commands/skills) missed this because the dangling reference is a *combat enemy_template*, not a skill or command — the same "partial-coverage test" blind spot the wilderness drop's curated-subset contract had.

### 2026-06-13 — Wilderness encounters: close 4 phantom-producer creature templates + global resolution guard — *drop wilderness-phantom-creatures*
Closes a No-phantom-producers invariant violation in the wilderness encounter → creature spawn bridge: **four `payload.npc_template` refs across two live regions did not resolve in the creature library, so those encounters fired their narrative but spawned nothing** (`engine/wilderness_encounter_runtime.py::spawn_encounter_creatures` returns `[]` on a library miss — a player walked into "Tusken scouts… they have seen you" and then nothing happened, no spawn, no combat). Pure-data + test drop; touches no engine/parser/server code (parallel-safe alongside the Director + parser sessions).
- **Root cause (a misleading dedup comment):** `data/npcs_creatures.yaml` carried a note that R&E-core beasts (dewback, …) needn't be re-stated here "because the core ships them." But the runtime resolves templates ONLY through `engine/creature_library.py::get_creature`, which loads ONLY this file — there is no sourcebook-appendix loader. So a referenced-but-absent creature is a dead encounter. The header note is rewritten to state the spawn-resolution contract plainly so the gap can't be reintroduced.
- **The 4 creatures, authored faithfully (WEG R&E D6):** `dewback` (non_hostile herd → `dune_sea.yaml:dewback_herd`) and `tusken_warrior` (hostile → `tusken_scout_party` + the `tusken_war_party`); `maze_predator` (hostile → `coruscant_underworld.yaml:maze_ambush`) and `underworld_thug` (hostile → `gang_patrol`). Beasts (dewback, maze_predator) keep the KNO/MEC/TEC = 0D convention; the two **sentients** (Tusken Raider, underworld thug) carry real KNO/MEC/TEC and are tagged `intelligent: true`. Provenance cited per entry: dewback calibrated to the statted R&E pack-beast family in WEG40120 (bantha/Ukian-torbull/tauntaun; the dewback's own GG1/COTG block is not on-box); tusken_warrior D6-from-scratch per `secrets_of_tatooine_extraction_v1.md` (the d20 block is discarded); maze_predator anchored to the in-repo anomaly canon (`engine/wilderness_anomalies.py` maze_predator_outbreak/apex) + R&E predator family; underworld_thug from R&E NPC-template conventions (trooper/pirate-sentry).
- **Hardened guard (new file):** `tests/test_wilderness_encounter_template_resolution.py` walks **every** live region via the production entry `load_era_wilderness_regions` (reads `era.yaml content_refs.wilderness`, so new regions are auto-covered) and asserts every hostile/non_hostile encounter template resolves via the runtime resolver `creature_library.get_creature` — **no curated allow-list**. The pre-existing per-biome contracts only checked their own id subset (`if tmpl in TATOOINE_IDS`/`URBAN_IDS`/`CROSSBIOME_IDS`), which is exactly why the 4 slipped through. Also asserts each resolved creature yields a concrete natural-attack damage.
- **Test contract relaxed to match the schema's intent:** `test_lane_a_creatures_tatooine.py::test_non_intelligent_attributes_and_natural_attack` applied the 0D KNO/MEC/TEC rule to *every* creature; it now applies it to non-intelligent creatures only (and asserts an `intelligent`-tagged template actually uses real attributes), so sentient spawn templates are faithful.
- **Discovered, deliberately NOT fixed here (flagged):** `creature_library.creature_spawn_count` cannot parse a `[lo,hi]` range `count` (`int([4,6])` raises → caught → falls back to `pack_count[0]`), so **every** wilderness encounter — the existing 18 too — spawns the pack minimum regardless of its authored range (e.g. the six-rider Tusken war party fields 2). Pre-existing; honoring ranges would shift wilderness difficulty galaxy-wide, so it's logged as `TD.ENCOUNTER_COUNT_RANGE_IGNORED` for a deliberate decision rather than slipped into a content drop. Creature `pack_count` minimums are set to sane spawn counts under the current fallback.
- **Verified:** the 3 lane-a creature contracts + the new resolution guard (27 passed) + spawner/special-attacks/spoils/ey_akh regression (118 passed) + an end-to-end `spawn_encounter_creatures` proof (all 4 now spawn 2/3/3/2; unknown-template still safely returns `[]`); YAML + AST validation of touched files.
- **Files:** `data/npcs_creatures.yaml`, `tests/test_wilderness_encounter_template_resolution.py` (new), `tests/test_lane_a_creatures_tatooine.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
### 2026-06-13 — Director "economy eyes": faucet/sink digest perception — *drop director-economy-eyes*
Gives the LLM Director macro **economic perception** (`director_scope_and_adaptive_spend_v1.md §3`) — step 3 of the Director scope expansion, after multi-zone (§2/§6) and adaptive-spend (§5). Previously the Director's only economic signal was per-org treasury; it ran a war narrative blind to the crafting/trade/bounty economy. Now it sees where credits flow.
- **Pure read, funnel-clean (`engine/director.py::_compile_economy_digest`):** every credit movement already routes through `db.adjust_credits(char_id, delta, source)`, which logs to `credit_log(source, delta, created_at)`. The new method rolls that up over the faction-turn window (30 min) into compact macro signals — `total_faucet`, `total_sink`, `net_flow`, `transactions`, and the top-5 `source` tags each way — and `compile_digest` injects it as `digest["economy"]`. **No new write seam**; it reads the credit funnel, honoring the funnel invariant.
- **Cheap + fail-open:** one indexed `GROUP BY source` query (`idx_credit_log_source`); returns `{}` on an idle window (adds nothing to the digest) or a read failure (e.g. pre-`credit_log` DB), and is skipped entirely when `compile_digest` is called without a `db`. Tiny token cost (per the design's "breadth is nearly free").
- **Perception only (this drop):** the Director can now factor a smuggling boom / deflation / a player getting rich into its narrative + hooks. ACTING on it with soft opportunity nudges (Brian decision A — seeds, never price/yield levers) is the separate next step (§4). Prompt-tuning to explicitly leverage the economy block is a follow-up (the prompt lives in `director_config.yaml`).
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_director_economy_eyes.py` (8 — totals/net, sorted+capped top lists, empty/zero-movement → `{}`, read-failure fail-open, digest integration with/without db) + director-suite regression green (cw-mapping / adaptive-spend / living-galaxy / bugfixes).
- **Files:** `engine/director.py`, `tests/test_director_economy_eyes.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — T3.20 safe character-load: guard attrs parse + force-sensitivity fail-safe — *drop t3-20-safe-load*
Fixes the two T3.20 launch-blockers (`HANDOFF_t3_20_state_preservation`) — a live save that couldn't load right — both in `engine/character.py::from_db_dict`, read-side, no schema change.
- **Blocker 1 — corrupted attribute locked the player out:** the attributes + force-attribute loops called `DicePool.parse()` **unguarded** (the earlier char-load hardening guarded only the skills loop), so one bad value (e.g. `"4X+2"`) raised and aborted the WHOLE character load — that character could not log in. Now each parse is wrapped (mirrors the skills-loop guard): the bad field is skipped with a warning, the rest of the character loads.
- **Blocker 2 — silent Force downgrade (`FORCE.sensitivity_failsafe_to_jedi`, Brian Ruling 5):** `force_sensitive` is DERIVED from `control`/`sense`/`alter` in the attributes JSON, so a corrupt/pre-derivation blob made a path-committed Jedi silently reconstruct as `force_sensitive=False` (losing their Force on that login). The committed path is recorded in the `village_chosen_path` **typed column** (survives blob corruption), so a committed path (`a`/`b`/`c`) with no recovered Force attrs now **fails SAFE to `force_sensitive=True` + a loud warning** (flagging the Force dice for a backfill) instead of a silent downgrade. `force_sensitive` stays derived state — never persisted (the `save_character` allowlist already blocks it), so this re-asserts safely every load; uncommitted chars get no spurious grant.
- **Deferred follow-ups (noted, not in this drop):** the idempotent Force-attribute *backfill runner* (write-side restore of lost control/sense/alter — `HANDOFF_t3_20_state_preservation`'s one net-new build) and the HANDOFF's HIGH/MEDIUM risk items.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_t3_20_safe_load.py` (9 — corrupted-attr-loads, corrupted-force-attr, malformed-JSON+committed fail-safe, valid-but-missing-force+committed, path-c, uncommitted-no-grant, missing-column-no-grant, normal-force-unchanged, corrupt-force-value+committed) + 785-test char/village/chargen/powered regression green.
- **Files:** `engine/character.py`, `tests/test_t3_20_safe_load.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — Director adaptive-spend governor (slice 1): skip-empty-turns + auto cadence — *drop director-adaptive-spend*
First slice of the Adaptive Spend Governor (`director_scope_and_adaptive_spend_v1.md §5`, Brian decisions D/E). Cadence is the only spend dimension that scales API cost (breadth/depth/memory/Ollama texture are always-on constants), so the `SpendGovernor` is a **cadence controller** that moves `self._turn_interval` within a budget ceiling and skips the paid turn on an empty server. All in `engine/director.py` (no parser collision); the manual `@director fidelity` toggle + the LLM `recommend_fidelity` advisory field are slice 2.
- **Skip-empty-turns (decision D):** `tick()` now routes a due faction turn through `_governed_turn`, which calls `_should_skip_turn` — at ≤1 players online the paid API turn is skipped (an empty server shouldn't pay to narrate to nobody), with a **bounded overnight catch-up**: if the world has been stale past `OVERNIGHT_CATCHUP_SECONDS` (6h) AND players were seen within `OVERNIGHT_CATCHUP_LOOKBACK` (24h), one catch-up turn fires so the world visibly moved by morning. Tracked via `_last_executed_turn_time` (real turns) + `_last_populated_time` (last tick with >1 online).
- **Auto cadence governor (decision E):** `_apply_governor` sets `_turn_interval` for subsequent turns from a cheap ROI heuristic — `FIDELITY_INTERVALS` = eco 60m / standard 30m / high 18m / max 15m. ≥4 players or a high-ROI in-window digest → escalate to `high`; ≤1 → `eco`; else `standard`. **Budget-guarded:** never auto-escalates to `high` once month-to-date spend (`get_budget_stats`) hits the `$30` auto ceiling (`GOVERNOR_AUTO_CEILING_USD`); the `ClaudeProvider` circuit breaker (`monthly_budget_cents`) is the hard backstop underneath. `max` (15m/$40) is reserved for the slice-2 manual toggle.
- **Telemetry:** `governor_state()` snapshot (tier / interval / manual flag / reason) + `_last_fidelity_reason` for the slice-2 `@director status` display; the governor `log`s WHY each cadence change happens.
- **No behavior change when busy:** with ≥2 players the turn runs exactly as before (the governor only sets the next interval). Always-on dimensions untouched.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_director_adaptive_spend.py` (count-online, skip-empty/overnight-catch-up edge cases, auto tiers, the budget guard, high-ROI digest escalation, manual pin, governor_state, governed-turn skip-vs-run) + 41-test director regression green.
- **Files:** `engine/director.py`, `tests/test_director_adaptive_spend.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — Director multi-zone "living galaxy": native CW faction axis + 34-zone load — *drop director-living-galaxy*
Clears `DIRECTOR.zonestate_cw_faction_axis` (Brian's one open design call) and the `DIRECTOR.multizone_living_galaxy` build. Brian ruled **Option A — native CW axis rewrite** (the more faithful path; he delegated the alert-semantics mapping to me under decide+build+log). The Director now tracks **all 34 config zones across every planet + space**, each computing a **correct, distinct** alert from real Clone Wars influence — not the 6 stale Mos Eisley keys that didn't even match the CW config and made every zone read the same wrong alert.
- **The blocker (verified at HEAD):** `VALID_ZONES` was 6 hardcoded keys (`spaceport/streets/cantina/shops/jabba/government`) that don't match the CW config keys (`tatooine_mos_eisley`, `senate_district`, …), so every zone seeded to the 30-fallback; and `ZoneState` hardcoded the GCW axis (`imperial/rebel/criminal/independent`) so `set_faction('republic',80)` silently orphaned and `compute_alert()` read a stale `imperial=50` → **every zone HIGH_ALERT**.
- **ZoneState native rewrite (`engine/director.py`):** influence now lives in a faction-agnostic `scores` dict keyed by the era's `VALID_FACTIONS`. `compute_alert()` reads three alert ROLES (authority/warfront/underworld) resolved from the **existing director_config rewicker** (`imperial→republic`, `rebel→cis`, `criminal→hutt_cartel`) via a new module-level `ALERT_AXIS` — so it's correct for CW **and** the emergency GCW fallback with no new config. `VALID_ZONES = frozenset(DEFAULT_INFLUENCE.keys())` (the 34-zone era config).
- **Alert thresholds (mine, first-cut/playtest-tunable):** authority≥70→LOCKDOWN; underworld≥70→UNDERWORLD; warfront≥40→UNREST; authority<30 & warfront<40 & underworld<40→LAX; authority≥50→HIGH_ALERT; else STANDARD. Preserves the GCW ordering it replaces. `jedi_order` + `bhg` are atmospheric overlays, not primary alert drivers in v1. Result: **12 lockdown / 5 unrest / 5 underworld / 7 standard / 4 lax / 1 high_alert** across the galaxy (verified live).
- **Consumers re-keyed to native CW factions:** digest `zone_influence`; `@director` influence table (both display paths in `director_commands.py`); session HUD `alert_faction` (`server/session.py`); `get_all_zone_states`/debug; the local-nudge heuristic `apply_player_action_deltas` (axis-keyed, era-robust zone selection); **`engine/security.py::_apply_director_overlay`** — the LIVE per-room security overlay now reads native influence (it was **dead for CW**, reading `getattr(zs,"imperial")`=0; senate_district republic=90 → martial law → SECURED, verified). `missions._pick_type` spawn bias now triggers on a **dominant-alert ≥40% share** (neutral at the baseline galaxy — no permanent smuggling skew the old "any zone" check would have introduced with 34 zones).
- **Era cleanness (B3):** removed the GCW production strings in `_generate_local_headline` ("Imperial forces…", "Rebel sympathizers…") and the security-shift notices ("weak Imperial presence") → CW flavor (Republic/Cartel/Separatist/authority).
- **Supersedes** the drop-39 "leave ZoneState axis untouched" contract; `test_director_cw_faction_mapping.py` + `test_b1f_rewicker_boundary.py` updated to the native contract.
- **Noted follow-ups (additive, INERT-not-broken for the 34 zones):** the faction-turn overlay zone map (`_DIRECTOR_ZONE_TO_DB_NAME`/`_BASE_SECURITY`) still covers only the legacy 6 keys (the per-turn overlay is a no-op for CW zones; the live per-room overlay works); smuggling/space `get_alert_level("spaceport")` is inert (was already) — zone-wire later.
- **Verified:** new `tests/test_director_living_galaxy.py` (axis resolution, 34-zone load, scores-dict round-trip/clamp, the original-bug repro, native alert semantics, galaxy differentiation, baseline-neutral spawn bias, era-correct deltas) + updated `test_director_cw_faction_mapping` / `test_b1f_rewicker_boundary` + 228-test director/security/era-cleanness regression green + boot smoke (34 zones load; live overlay reads native influence).
- **Files:** `engine/director.py`, `engine/security.py`, `engine/missions.py`, `parser/director_commands.py`, `server/session.py`, `tests/test_director_living_galaxy.py` (new), `tests/test_director_cw_faction_mapping.py`, `tests/test_b1f_rewicker_boundary.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — Director API path works live: SSL fix + 2 verified director.py bugs — *drop 51*
Makes the Director's Claude API path actually reach the API from Brian's box — **verified live end-to-end for the first time** (the real `ClaudeProvider.generate()` returned a completion; previously every live call failed). Three coupled fixes, the prerequisites for the multi-zone "living galaxy" + adaptive-spend build.
- **SSL (the box blocker, root-caused this session):** `ai/claude_provider.py` built a bare `aiohttp.ClientSession()` (certifi default), which fails on Brian's box with `CERTIFICATE_VERIFY_FAILED`. Root cause is **Norton Antivirus** "Web/Mail Shield" doing local TLS interception (NOT a corporate proxy — an earlier note misattributed it) — it re-signs certs with a private root in the Windows store that certifi doesn't read. New `_build_ssl_context()` returns a `truststore.SSLContext` (reads the OS store → Norton's root is trusted there → handshake succeeds), injected via a `TCPConnector`. Fail-safe: `None` → aiohttp's certifi default on any non-intercepting box. (Memory `anthropic-api-box-blockers` corrected.)
- **Bug 1 — the dead influence lever (uncaught crash):** `engine/director.py::_run_api_turn` called `self._apply_influence_delta(...)` which was **never defined** → an uncaught `AttributeError` on every API turn that returned `influence_adjustments` (the influence never applied AND the narrative event after it never ran). Now defined: it mutates the in-memory `ZoneState` (`set_faction` clamps to bounds) and persists via `_set_influence`. Correctly targets the Director's OWN `zone_influence` model (string zone keys), NOT the player-territory `adjust_territory_influence` funnel (org_code + int zone_id) — they're distinct influence systems.
- **Bug 2 — cost telemetry logged $0:** `_run_api_turn` hardcoded `tok_in=tok_out=0`, so `director_log` always recorded zero cost and `estimated_cost_usd` always reported $0 — which the cost circuit-breaker and the upcoming adaptive-spend ceiling depend on. The provider now captures each call's usage (`self._last_usage`) and exposes `last_usage()`; the Director reads it to log REAL token counts. (Confirmed live: 20 in / 7 out on the smoke call.)
- **Verified:** `tests/test_director_bugfixes.py` (9 — the lever defined/async/applies-delta/clamps/zero-noop/unknown-zone-safe, `last_usage` default + copy-safety, the SSL context builds) + a LIVE end-to-end `generate()` smoke (real completion + real usage) + 208-test director/provider/territory/influence regression green.
- **Files:** `ai/claude_provider.py`, `engine/director.py`, `tests/test_director_bugfixes.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — Lore-ingestion toolchain + full sourcebook ingestion (lorebook 74→1,978 entries) — *tooling*
Sourcebook → lorebook pipeline so the WEG D6 corpus can ground both AI layers (Director + NPC dialogue). All tools live in `tools/`, are review-file-only (never edit the live lorebook directly), and share one `_BANNED` era-guard + canonical-figure check. Pairs with `sourcebook_ingestion_pipeline_v1.md` + `sourcebook_grounding_reprioritization_v1.md`.
- **`tools/ingest_lore.py`** — PDF → OCR (PyMuPDF text layer; Tesseract fallback on scanned pages, auto-detected at the Windows install path) → Haiku era-translation to ~20 BBY → era-guard → review yaml with `planet`/`surface_affinity` filter tags. **Hardened this session:** `truststore` injection (the dev box sits behind a Lockheed TLS-inspection proxy that breaks Python's default SSL — certifi can't fix it, the Windows cert store can) + a loud fatal-abort so an auth/credit/SSL failure can't masquerade as a silent 0-entry run (verified: exit 3 with the cause + fix, no file written) + UTF-8 console safety.
- **`tools/harvest_extractions.py`** — $0 harvest of the "Deliverable A" lore dicts already sitting in the 16 `docs/design/*extraction*.md` docs, through the same era-guard. 45 clean entries (13 correctly rejected as genuine GCW leaks, e.g. "General Airen Cracken").
- **`tools/append_lore.py`** (new) — safe additive appender: parses a review yaml's keepers, dedups by title against the live file + within the batch, **comment-preserving text append** (no YAML round-trip, per the map-safety invariant), backs up to `.bak`, then **re-validates the whole file against the loader's hard rules and rolls back on any failure** (a malformed append can never block seeding). Era-rechecks every keeper.
- **`tools/ingest_batch.py`** (new) — one-command runner for the grounding-priority book set (under-grounded planets first: Coruscant/Kuat/Nar Shaddaa), sequential (no OCR thrash), stops on a fatal API error instead of hammering.
- **Step 1 — free harvest:** 33 harvested entries appended (45 minus 12 already-present) → **74 → 107**.
- **Concurrency + robustness (added when the paid run scaled up):** opt-in `--concurrency` runs OCR pages AND API chunks in parallel — thread-safe (pixmaps rendered sequentially since PyMuPDF isn't thread-safe on one Document, then Tesseract run concurrently on the PNG bytes) — with 429 retry-with-backoff + read-timeout retry so parallel load never silently drops a chunk. OCR bumped 200→300 DPI; the extract prompt now tells the model to silently fix obvious OCR artifacts and **omit (not invent)** anything too garbled. Cut Coruscant (162 fully-scanned pages) from a 20-min sequential stall to a clean run.
- **Step 2 — full 12-book ingestion (after the account was funded):** 12 WEG/d20 sourcebooks → **2,023 clean** extracted entries. An LLM **quality-gate** (12-reviewer workflow) then caught **61 subtle drops the static `_BANNED` list can't see** — notably **"New Republic"/"Grand Moff"/"Mon Mothma" era leaks** (those tokens aren't in `_BANNED`), post-war "civil war" phrasing, and OCR-garbled proper nouns ("Grand Moll Bank"). Curated append (exclude the 61, `priority ≥5` floor −81, dedup −10) → **107 → 1,978 entries**, parses clean, lore-loader + era-cleanness tests green. Coverage: Coruscant 111 / Kuat 35 (the two worst gaps, filled) + 1,695 era-neutral "all". Inert until the next server reseed.
- **Follow-up surfaced:** `_BANNED` should gain the post-CW/New-Republic tokens (New Republic, Grand Moff/Moff, Mon Mothma…) so the runtime era-guard + static tests catch what only the LLM gate caught here. (The Director's latent SSL bug this entry originally flagged was independently fixed by drop 51 — `truststore` in `claude_provider.py`.)
- **Decisions recorded:** keep keyword+tag lorebook retrieval (no vector RAG; FTS5 is the next rung if ever needed); quest/scenario expansion ruled POST-LAUNCH-OK with the painless path verified at code level (`quest_expansion_postlaunch_path_v1.md`, TODO T3.24).
- **Files:** `tools/ingest_lore.py`, `tools/harvest_extractions.py`, `tools/append_lore.py` (new), `tools/ingest_batch.py` (new), `data/worlds/clone_wars/lore.yaml` (74→1,978), `.gitignore` (ingest_review/), `docs/design/quest_expansion_postlaunch_path_v1.md` (new), `docs/design/sourcebook_ingestion_pipeline_v1.md`, `docs/design/sourcebook_grounding_reprioritization_v1.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — Character-load skill robustness (adversarial-sweep hardening) — *fixup*
A break-it-tester sweep of drops 44-50 (all confirmed robust) surfaced 2 character-load crash paths — both fixed defensively (no behavior change for valid data):
- **`from_db_dict` skills loop** (`engine/character.py:882`) had no per-entry guard, so a corrupted `skills` column value (a non-D6 string like `"TRAINED"`) raised an uncaught `ValueError`/`AttributeError` that aborted the whole character load AND leaked raw Python error text to the player (`get_char_obj` is on the `attack`/`+sheet`/HUD path). Now skips a malformed entry with a warning, matching the JSON-decode tolerance already on the blob. **Pre-existing** (predates drop 44); reachable only via DB corruption, but it's the only CRASH+LEAK the sweep found.
- **`Character.has_skill_dice`** (drop 50) raised `AttributeError` on a non-`DicePool` skills value (caught upstream today by `get_powersuit_strength_bonus`, but a footgun for any future caller). Now an `isinstance` guard treats junk as untrained.
- **Verified:** `tests/test_powered_suit.py` (18 — +2 robustness pins) + 548-test character/skill/chargen/powered regression green.
- **Files:** `engine/character.py`, `tests/test_powered_suit.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`.

### 2026-06-13 — Powered armor: the Powersuit Operation skill + the first exo-suit — *drop 50*
Closes `CRAFT.powered_suit_design` (the other HOOK long-pole). Brian ruled "register a new powersuit skill"; this lands the skill + the first POWERED armor whose servo-assisted Strength bonus reaches combat, gated by proficiency and hard-capped (conservative charter). Unblocked by drop 47's equipment-instance accessor.
- **New skill** (`data/skills.yaml`): `Powersuit Operation` under **Mechanical** (WEG40120's "Powersuit operation", a reaction-capable *Operation skill, sibling of Ground-Vehicle/Walker/Repulsorlift Operation). The registry is data-driven, so it auto-registers with the right governing attribute — `_skill_to_attr` resolves it to `mechanical` (no hardcoded-map edit, unlike the restraints-escape `lifting` case). Spec-free (no Imperial powersuit models in the Clone Wars era). Skill count 75→76.
- **Powered-armor fields** (`engine/weapons.py`): `strength_bonus` (a D6 code) + `powersuit_skill` (the gate flag) on the Weapon dataclass + loader. Default empty/false → every existing armor row is unchanged.
- **The bonus consumer** (`engine/character.py::get_powersuit_strength_bonus`): reads the worn suit's `strength_bonus`, **hard-caps at +1D** (a hypothetical +5D suit still yields +1D — no power creep), and **halves it (floor) for a wearer with no trained Powersuit Operation dice** (the servos fight an untrained pilot). Gated on the armor's `powersuit_skill` flag (so the flag is consumed, not a phantom field) AND a robust skill-presence check via a new `Character.has_skill_dice` helper (tolerates the 0D-skill-isn't-trained case + the underscore-form NPC key dialect — both caught in review). Folded into the combat **soak roll** (`engine/combat.py`): powered armor makes you tankier. Strength-based melee deferred.
- **The first powered suit** (`data/weapons.yaml` + `data/schematics.yaml`): `labor_exo_frame_pl9` "Loader Exo-Frame (PL-9)" — a Clone Wars industrial cargo-loader exo-frame up-armored for the field (+1D STR, +1D+1/+1D+2 soak, -1D Dex). Craftable (Armor Repair / Sela Tarn / diff 20 / composite+metal+rare q70 / 6000cr) — a clear tier above flex-armor. A 6000cr SINK, no new faucet. Integrated weapon mounts stay deferred (lore).
- **Three review findings fixed pre-handback** (invariant-auditor + code-reviewer): the `powersuit_skill` field was a phantom (stored, never read) → now the gate; the skill check counted `DicePool(0,0)` as trained (DicePool has no `__bool__`) → now `has_skill_dice` with `is_zero()`; the underscore-form key was a dead dual-`.get()` → now a canonical scan. All three pinned by new tests.
- **A stale teach-pin** (Sela Tarn's exact armor-schematic set) drifted +1 with the new exo-frame → loosened from exact-match to subset (the structural intent: "all drop-C armor binds to Sela," robust to new Sela schematics).
- **Verified:** `tests/test_powered_suit.py` (16 — skill registers under mechanical, item loads, bonus trained/untrained/0D-untrained/underscore-trained/flag-gated/capped/ordinary-zero/none-zero, combat-soak integration trained>untrained>unpowered, the schematic) + 1129-test armor/weapon/combat/craft/skill regression green (1 stale pin fixed). Invariant-auditor + code-reviewer (all findings fixed).
- **Files:** `data/skills.yaml`, `engine/weapons.py`, `engine/character.py`, `engine/combat.py`, `data/weapons.yaml`, `data/schematics.yaml`, `tests/test_powered_suit.py` (new), `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_c.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — Restraints/handcuffs — verb layer + gates (closes CRAFT.HOOK.restraints) — *drop 49*
Wires the drop-48 engine core to the player surface, completing one of the two HOOK long-poles. A captor can now cuff a defeated/willing prisoner, who's locked out of move/attack/gear until they break free or are released. Mirrors `parser/demolitions_commands.py` (the engine does the work; the parser is a thin front end). Design: `docs/design/restraints_system_design_v1.md`.
- **The binders item** — a craftable consumable (`data/consumables.yaml` + `data/schematics.yaml`: Security skill, taught by Vek Nurren, difficulty 14, metal + composite components, 120cr). A pure SINK (crafted/bought, consumed on a successful cuff) — no credit faucet. Registered in the parity invariant's `NON_STIM_CONSUMERS` so it can't be an inert token.
- **Async orchestration** (`engine/restraints.py`): `attempt_cuff` (resolve target via `match_in_room` → consent/defeat gate → consume binders → persist), `attempt_uncuff` (captor-or-admin authority), `attempt_escape_action`, `set_consent_action`. The gate runs BEFORE consuming binders — a rejected cuff doesn't waste them (pinned).
- **Verbs** (`parser/restraints_commands.py`, registered in `game_server.py`): `cuff <target>` (aliases restrain/bind), `uncuff <target>` (unbind/release), `escape` (struggle), `allowrestrain on|off` (opt-in consent toggle).
- **Gates** — `is_restrained(char)` blocks at 6 sites: `MoveCommand` (can't walk off), `AttackCommand` declaration (can't wield — mirrors the retreat-refusal gate), and the 4 equip verbs Equip/Unequip/Wear/RemoveArmor (can't change gear). Social verbs, `look`, and `escape` stay available (bound ≠ silenced). The gate is a lazy local import + early return, a no-op for the absent-key case (every existing character unchanged).
- **v1 scope (conservative charter, logged):** cuffs PCs only (NPCs have no `attributes` column for persistent state — a future increment); fixed escape DC 15; one escape attempt per command; no damage from being cuffed; release = captor-or-admin only.
- **A craft-parity invariant caught a real gap:** binders, as a craftable consumable, was flagged as an inert token until registered with its real consumer — fixed (the no-phantom-consumer guard working). An almost-shipped phantom component type (`electronics`, not a canonical RESOURCE_TYPE) was caught + corrected to `composite` pre-commit.
- **Verified:** `tests/test_restraints_verbs.py` (16 — the consent/defeat gate across defeated/healthy/consenting, binders consumed-on-success / kept-on-rejection, self/NPC/not-found rejection, uncuff captor/admin/third-party authority, escape persistence, consent toggle) + `test_restraints_engine` (21) + the updated craft-parity test + 297-test move/equip/combat-command regression green. Invariant-auditor CLEAN; smoke-verifier BOOTS CLEAN (227).
- **Files:** `engine/restraints.py`, `parser/restraints_commands.py` (new), `server/game_server.py`, `parser/builtin_commands.py`, `parser/combat_commands.py`, `data/consumables.yaml`, `data/schematics.yaml`, `tests/test_restraints_verbs.py` (new), `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_a.py`, `docs/design/restraints_system_design_v1.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-13 — Restraints/handcuffs — engine core (state model + consent/defeat gate) — *drop 48*
First slice of `CRAFT.HOOK.restraints` (one of the two HOOK long-poles). Builds the persistent-restraint STATE MODEL + the Brian-decided PvP norm as a self-contained, inert engine module — the verb layer (cuff/uncuff/escape/allow-restrain) + the move/attack/equip gates + the binders item land in the follow-up slice that wires this to the player surface (the riskier half — it touches hot command paths — so it ships separately). Design: `docs/design/restraints_system_design_v1.md`.
- **The norm (Brian):** consent/defeat-gated — a PC may be cuffed only if DEFEATED (`wound_level >= INCAPACITATED`) or CONSENTING (`allow restrain` opt-in); a healthy unwilling PC cannot be cuffed (the grief guard). NPCs need no consent.
- **`engine/restraints.py`** (mirrors `engine/buffs.py`): state lives in `attributes.restraint` JSON (`{applied_by, applied_by_id, item_key, escape_difficulty, applied_at}`) — **no schema migration**, and absent = not restrained so every existing character is unchanged. `get_restraint`/`is_restrained`/`can_be_restrained` (the gate)/`apply_restraint`/`release_restraint`/`can_release` (captor-or-admin authority)/`set_consent`/`restraint_consent`/`attempt_escape`. Persistent (survives logout via `save_character`), distinct from the ephemeral combat grapple (`Combatant.restraint`).
- **Escape = WEG Strength, funnel-routed.** `attempt_escape` rolls `perform_skill_check(char, "lifting", difficulty)` — `lifting` is the Strength-GOVERNED skill, so it's a faithful Strength roll. **A test caught a real bug here**: routing through `"strength"` directly mis-maps (the skill→attr table sends the bare attribute name to the perception default → a 2D roll ignoring the prisoner's real Strength). Fixed to `lifting`. Conservative: fixed DC 15 (Moderate), one attempt per command, no auto-progress (retunable when T3.19 lands).
- **Balance (conservative charter):** no cuffing healthy unwilling PCs, no damage from being cuffed, release = captor-or-admin only (capture stays meaningful), binders are a pure item sink (no credit faucet).
- **Inert:** no callers yet (the verb slice wires it) — the same producer-without-consumer-is-authorized pattern as the ambient Phase 0 scaffolding; the design doc authorizes it.
- **Verified:** `tests/test_restraints_engine.py` (21 — the consent/defeat gate across healthy/defeated/mortally-wounded/wounded-not-incap/consenting/NPC/already-restrained/malformed, apply-read-release round-trip, JSON-string + dict shape preservation = logout survival, release authority, consent toggle, escape uses the stored difficulty + rolls real Strength). AST clean.
- **Files:** `engine/restraints.py` (new), `tests/test_restraints_engine.py` (new), `docs/design/restraints_system_design_v1.md` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
