### 2026-06-12 — Market segmentation (decision a): the buy-verb gate — *same-day drop 10*
`CRAFT.market_segmentation_impl` delivered — and the audit found the violation wasn't where the queue expected. The NPC channels that LOOK like stores were clean: commissary sells faction-issue keys (its `blaster_pistol` is band-25, which decision a explicitly allows at a rank-gated requisition discount), and player-droid shops are the decision's own sanctioned band-2/3 channel (pinned untouched). The violation was **the bare `buy` verb itself**: the BuyCommand fallthrough — originally the ship-weapon shop — resolved the **entire weapon registry** by name with no stock gate, no vendor-presence gate, and no room gate. Every row was credit-purchasable anywhere at book cost + haggle (a generic 3D vendor when nobody's in the room), under the mislabeled `ship_weapon_purchase` tag — and every Gundark drop silently widened that store: **the Drop G contraband band was purchasable for credits, no Gundark required.**
- **The gate:** `vendor_stocked: bool` on WeaponData — **DEFAULT CLOSED**, so every future row ships off-market until deliberately opened. `buy` refuses unstocked rows with the redirect ("Craft it, check player shops — or know the right people"); the `weapons` listing stays a full stats reference but **prices only stocked rows** (the cost column reads "craft" otherwise — the list keeps its reference job without advertising unbuyables).
- **The open market: 11 Avail-1 commons at book cost** — hold-out blaster, blaster pistol, heavy blaster pistol, sporting blaster + sporting rifle, knife, vibroblade, stun baton, and the Gundark Avail-1 trio (vibrosaw, DL-22, DL-6H). **The band-consistency test rejected two of my own first-cut picks before the drop shipped:** vibroaxe and stun_pistol are both band-40 schematic outputs (heavy vibroblade / basic stun pistol) — decision a closes them, and the test that enforces "no band-40+ craft output on the open market" earned its keep twice on day one.
- **Grandfather-vs-withdraw, resolved:** nothing stocked needed withdrawing — the violation was the ungated verb, not stock lists. Items players already bought stay theirs (inventories untouched); the gate closes future purchases only.
- **Noted, not built** (`OBS.buy_verb_followups`): `buy` still lacks a vendor-presence/room gate (open commons purchasable in the desert — a follow-up call); the `ship_weapon_purchase` tag mislabels ground buys (rename during T3.19, ledger-continuity caveat); commissary's tracking_fob advertises "+1D to Search" with no consumer — a one-field Drop-F-seam candidate once its landing shape is verified.
- **Tests:** `tests/test_econ_market_segmentation.py` (9 — exact open-list pin; default-closed on a bare WeaponData; contraband + thermal closed; the band-40+ sweep over every weapon-typed craft output; open rows have real prices; buy-gate and listing source pins; commissary band-line pin with the corrected criterion; player-shop-channel-untouched pin). Sandbox: 9 + 174 adjacent green.
- **Files:** `engine/weapons.py`, `data/weapons.yaml`, `parser/space_commands.py`, `parser/builtin_commands.py`, `tests/test_econ_market_segmentation.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-12 — Gundark Drop G: tuition, contraband, the black market — *same-day drop 9* — **THE LANE IS COMPLETE (A–G)**
The finale, under decisions **CRAFT.schematic_tuition = a** (resolved this session), **3a**, and **(a)=b**. Three systems and three recipes, and the sourcebook lane that started with the P0 remediation closes on its own bookend: Gundark himself, dealing the catalog's worst pages.
- **Tuition (decision a).** `schematic_tuition()` in engine/crafting: **50% of base_cost, floor 50 cr**, charged via the `schematic_tuition` ledger tag — a real credit sink scaling with the recipe. The old behavior (talk grants the trainer's ENTIRE catalog free) is replaced: **talk grants the cheapest recipe free once per character per trainer** ("first lesson's on the house" — tracked in `attributes.trainer_free_lessons`), lists the rest with prices, and the **new `learn <name>` command** buys them one at a time (trainer must be in the room; the free lesson works through `learn` too; insufficient credits refuses cleanly). **PC-to-PC teaching stays free, untouched, pinned.** Verified before building: **no tutorial chain depends on trainer grants** (the KDY chain uses its own `+craft fetch` flow) — the first-free mechanism is kept as diegesis, not necessity. **⚑ WINDOWS WATCH ITEM #5:** trainers no longer hand over whole catalogs on hello; players with established characters keep what they know, but new learning costs credits.
- **Contraband (decision 3a) — the field ships WITH its enforcer.** Schematic `contraband: true` flags the **landed item** in both the weapon and gear branches, and **patrol boardings now sweep carried inventory**: a new branch in `patrol_comply` (between the smuggling-cargo check and the clean path) runs the same Con-15-to-hide flow as cargo — succeed and they pat you down and miss it; fail and the goods are **CONFISCATED** (the band's risk-side sink) with a **Class-4 infraction**, "Restricted goods on person." Fail-open sweep; legacy items and lawful gear untouched.
- **The black-market band** — Avail 4/X, **q70** materials, rubric extrapolating +3/die past 6D with the **Heroic 26 cap**: **Disruptor Pistol** (6D+2, diff 24, 3,000 cr — banned on every world with a functioning court) · **Predator Rifle EXP-7a** (7D prototype, diff 26, 7,000 cr — the book's recoil Strength roll stays notes) · **Anti-Vehicle Grenade** (7D `single_use`, diff 26, 750 cr — the no-scale-reduction rule stays notes). Tuitions: 1,500 / 3,500 / 375 cr.
- **The teacher is Gundark.** The in-fiction compiler of *Gundark's Personal Gear* itself — a Whiphid arms dealer at the **Nar Shaddaa Undercity Market** (WEG original persona, Q1-safe), `trainer: true`, candid that patrols confiscate what they find: *"I teach you to BUILD it so the loss is survivable. That's the whole business model."* Seeded via `npcs_drop_craft_g_gundark.yaml` + an era.yaml load line.
- **Resolved exclusions, pinned:** **thermal detonator stays uncraftable** (resolved by recommendation, vetoable — the X-class icon's scarcity IS its identity, and a craftable 10D would dominate the ordnance economy; Drop D's pin stands) · **Lowickan Firegems** are natural gems, not recipes (the hyperdrive-sabotage plot device stays logged for the cartel lane) · heavy disruptor (book quirk: weaker than the standard at twice the price) · pulse rifle (cone-primary unmodeled) · the plot-artifact-priced X espionage devices.
- **Three prior pins flipped WITH the drop:** drops A, B, and C each carried a "no contraband field yet" guard — Drop G is the yet. All three now pin the field's **scope** (exactly the black-market band, all Gundark-taught, nothing lawful flagged), so a stray `contraband:` on a lawful recipe fails loudly.
- **Tests:** `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_g.py` (19 — tuition math floor; first-talk grants only cheapest + lists prices; second talk grants nothing; learn charges the right tuition with the right tag; insufficient-credits refusal; trainer-must-be-present; learn-as-free-lesson; PC-teach-free pin; landing-flag pins ×2 branches; carried-sweep flagged-only; comply-branch confiscation + Class-4 pin; roster rows/rubric/q70/bindings; band tuitions; resolved-exclusion absences; Gundark seed shape/room/era/binding). Sandbox: **602 green** across the ENTIRE net — craft A–G, P0, crafting state, skill keys, skill checks, combat (incl. the session54 umbrella), economy, patrol era-cleanness, Q1 sweep, era-clean, SRB, hazards, wilderness, encounters, hygiene.
- **Files:** `engine/crafting.py`, `engine/encounter_patrol.py`, `parser/crafting_commands.py`, `data/weapons.yaml`, `data/schematics.yaml`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/npcs_drop_craft_g_gundark.yaml` (new), `data/worlds/clone_wars/era.yaml`, `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_g.py` (new), `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_a.py`, `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_b.py`, `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_c.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-12 — Gundark Drop F: espionage kit + the carried-tool seam — *same-day drop 8*
3 schematics riding ONE new mechanic, per gundark plan §5/§8 Drop F. Pre-flight found §5's dominant pattern — skill-bonus gear (+1D security, +1D first aid, …) — had **no consumer anywhere**: the same gap that deferred macrobinoculars, med-aid, and the gyro-grappler in earlier drops.
- **The seam:** `perform_skill_check` now applies a **carried-tool bonus** — `_best_tool_bonus` scans the character's carried items for `skill_bonus` dicts (`{skill, bonus}`), canonicalizes the skill through the Drop 1 helper (underscore data-form matches space-form checks), and applies the single **best** matching tool. Tools never stack — carrying two medscanners is one medscanner that beeps twice. Placement follows the SRB.3 lead-bonus philosophy verbatim: live at the chokepoint so every out-of-combat caller benefits without knowing the mechanic exists. **Combat is structurally untouched** — engine/combat builds its pools directly and never calls the chokepoint (pinned), so a code slicer can never buff a blaster roll. `SkillCheckResult` gains additive defaulted `tool_pips`/`tool_name` fields for UIs that want to credit the tool. Fail-open throughout; inventory source and shape-tolerance mirror `_has_mitigation`. **Caught en route:** the module lacked a `json` import and the helper's fail-open was silently masking the NameError — smoke-tested end-to-end after the fix (2D base + UniTech Patch → 3D+2).
- **Landing passthrough:** the gear branch copies `skill_bonus` from schematic to the landed dict — gear has no stat registry; the carried dict IS the record.
- **Roster (zero new NPCs — the Vek Nurren lesson, pinned):** **Code Slicer** (Ouwani UniSlice — +1D security, Avail 3 q55, the Old-Republic-era lock-breaker, 2,000 cr) · **UniTech Patch** (+1D+2 security, Avail 2 q40, 5,200 cr — the book's breach-masking/fake-alarm tricks stay notes) · **Medscanner** (Cryoncorp Mediscan 21 — +1D first aid, Avail 2 q40, 3,000 cr, properly answering Drop E's med-aid deferral). All `computer_prog`-crafted, electronic-primary mixes per §4 spy gear. Trainers: **Renna Dox** ×2 (the existing sensor_mask/comm_jammer slicer-tech) and **Heist** (the Cutting Edge medic) — both seeded-trainer-pinned.
- **Out with reasons:** Force Detector (CRAFT.HOOK.force_detector — quest-artifact recast only; the never-a-recipe pin checks **parsed data**, since the file's own comments rightly mention the exclusion) · qualifier-bound bonuses (DataSearch "info search only", geological scanner "survey only" — deferred rather than over-broadly granted; a blanket +search would buff spotting too: the no-rewrite rule) · plasma-cutter-as-weapon (a fixed 7D melee at 150 cr is an economy-breaking book aside; its tool identity waits on breaching mechanics) · electronic blaster sight (+1D blaster is a combat mod — wrong seam by design) · sniffers/autoscan/camo-netting (search-vs-hide and stationary-scanner systems absent) · Master Command Unit, Voice Box, Master Coder Chip, Electronic Lock Breaker, Disruption Bubble (Avail 4/X band → Drop G).
- **Two PRE-EXISTING reds fixed with attribution** (both verified red against the untouched upload, NOT this drop's doing): `test_srb1_medic_stim`'s four-entry catalog pin and `test_srb1_stim_schematics`'s hardcoded four-key selector — both stale since the medpac family (medpac, medpac_advanced, medpac_fastflesh) landed in `_STIM_CATALOG` **with correct consumable schematics**. The count pin now lists the intended seven; the selector follows the live catalog (the test's intent is catalog↔schematic agreement, so the selector must follow the catalog). The medic economic loop was, in fact, closed.
- **Tests:** `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_f.py` (14 — best-single/no-stacking; dialect canonicalization; non-match unaffected; malformed fail-open; full-check application + result surfacing; no-tool defaults; combat-isolation pin; landing-passthrough pin; rubric/bindings/mix ×3; seeded-trainer pins; grant-on-talk superset semantics; force-detector parsed-data pin). Sandbox: **288 core** (craft A–F + P0 + skill-keys + combat batches) + **273 blast-radius** (SRB + hazards + encounters + missions + era-clean) green.
- **Files:** `engine/skill_checks.py`, `parser/crafting_commands.py`, `data/schematics.yaml`, `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_f.py` (new), `tests/test_srb1_medic_stim.py`, `tests/test_srb1_stim_schematics.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-12 — Gundark Drop E: field gear — the outfitter, the sink, the seam — *same-day drop 7*
Three fixes and two consumer-real items, per gundark plan §4/§8 Drop E. The fixes ARE the drop — pre-flight found the survival-gear loop broken at three separate joints:
- **⚑ Vek Nurren was a dangling trainer.** Five existing gear schematics (cooling_unit, breath_mask, radiation_suit, anti_theft_alarm, water_canteen — five different skills) name `trainer_npc: Vek Nurren`, and he was seeded **nowhere**: the entire survival-gear teaching loop was phantom — hazards consumed the items, the craft branch could land them, and no player could ever learn one. (The near-collision with *Venn Kator*, the Docking Bay 94 ship-component trainer, is probably how the dangle survived audits — now pinned distinct.) Seeded: a Sullustan ex-scout field outfitter at **Lup's General Store** (density-directive co-location, the Sela Tarn precedent), `trainer: true`, `train_skills: [survival]`, seven schematics bound (his five plus Drop E's two), granted-on-talk pinned end-to-end.
- **⚑ `uses` never decremented — the sink was missing.** Crafted gear landed with `uses`/`max_uses` and *nothing consumed them*: radiation_suit's 10 uses and anti_theft_alarm's 1 were decorative. Now mitigation gear with `max_uses > 0` **spends a use when it actually averts a hazard** and is removed at zero (with a spent message via the pose-event path). `_find_mitigation_item` mirrors `_has_mitigation`'s source and shape-tolerance exactly (the two must agree or a player could pass the presence check and dodge the consume); `_consume_mitigation_use` mutates **both stores** — the db mirror *and* the live session dict the hazard tick re-reads (stale-sync would have re-mitigated forever). Durable gear (max_uses 0), equipment-slot matches, and legacy string items are untouched by shape. Fail-open throughout. **WINDOWS WATCH ITEM #4:** consumable mitigation gear now depletes.
- **anti_theft_alarm had no consumer** — urban_danger's mitigation list was `[]`. Wired: with the new decrement, the 1-use alarm defeats exactly one pickpocket attempt and falls apart. The schematic finally does something.
- **New items ride consumers that exist:** the **Luma Flare** (Salamini 3287 — a 4D thrown burn on the attack path + Drop D's `single_use`; the 300 m illumination and ≤50 m blind stay notes; demolitions diff 14, Avail 2) and the **Animal Excluder** (Merr-Sonn, extraction's "direct wilderness-encounter hook" — security diff 14, electronic+composite, gear, 350 cr) riding a **new aversion seam in `roll_encounter`**: an additive `carried_keys` kwarg (the async movement caller fetches one inventory read per wilderness move), and a post-pick 50% aversion applied **only to creature-templated hostile/non_hostile picks** (caravans, weather, and templateless flavor pass through). Cooldown still marks — the animal approached and was repelled — and the caller surfaces `reason="averted_by_excluder"` as a flavor line. Book power settings/willpower roll = notes; tunables → T3.19.
- **Deferred with reasons (no consumer):** med-aid/medkit (no skill-modifier or surgery-kit gating — "medkit" in medical_commands is a medpac alias), rope/grapplers/line-throwers (climbing modifiers), rations (no hunger), organic gill (no aquatic hazard), automap/comlinks, conveyance packs (movement systems — the powered-suit design-pass family), restraints (CRAFT.HOOK.restraints, standing).
- **Tests:** `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_e.py` (19 — seed shape/room/era/seven-grant/Venn-vs-Vek distinctness; decrement both-stores ×multi-use/last-use/durable; find-helper dict+legacy shapes; end-to-end consume through `check_hazard_for_character` itself; urban_danger pin; excluder averted/fires-without/aversion-can-fail/non-creature-unaffected under scripted rng + cooldown-marks; caller-wiring pins; flare row + both schematics' rubric/bindings; seam-constant↔output_key match). Uses `asyncio.run` (3.14-safe). Sandbox: **543 green** across craft A–E + P0 + skill-keys + combat + P2P + era-clean + economy + wilderness + encounter + hazard batches (pytest-asyncio added to the sandbox alongside aiosqlite/bcrypt/aiohttp).
- **Files:** `engine/hazards.py`, `engine/wilderness_encounters.py`, `parser/builtin_commands.py`, `data/weapons.yaml`, `data/schematics.yaml`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/npcs_drop_craft_e_outfitter.yaml` (new), `data/worlds/clone_wars/era.yaml`, `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_e.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-11 — Gundark Drop D: ordnance + the single-use consumption mechanic — *same-day drop 6*
3 demolitions schematics (decision b=a) + 2 grenade rows, scoped by two pre-flight findings: **`blast_radius` loads into WeaponData but nothing in combat consumes it** (frag/thermal's single-target behavior is the precedent — blast stays data + notes), and **ammo is wholly unmodeled** — every grenade at HEAD was an infinite-use weapon, so craftable explosives without a sink would be a permanent-weapon printer.
- **The mechanic (faucets and sinks land together):** `single_use: bool` on WeaponData (explicit per-row, never type-derived) + loader; flagged rows are consumed from the equipment slot at attack **declaration** — the throw is committed, and round resolution rolls the action's captured skill/damage strings (never a live equipment re-read), so the early clear is provably safe. Guarded by the same `damage == default_damage` "this attack actually uses the equipped weapon" condition the declare broadcast uses, so an explicit `with <skill> damage <dice>` override never eats the grenade. Canonical per-slot write preserves armor. `_declare_and_broadcast` now returns success (was None-always). **frag_grenade and thermal_detonator retro-flagged** — ⚑ WINDOWS WATCH ITEM #3: grenades stop being infinite; the actor gets an "expended with the throw" line.
- **Roster:** Incendiary Grenade (Avail 1, q25, 4D — Old Republic jump-trooper issue, era-gold) · Frag Grenade schematic over the EXISTING row (Avail 2, q40, 5D) · Merr-Sonn Stun Grenade (Avail 2, 6D stun_only — **book-rechargeable, the sanctioned `single_use: false` exception**, pinned). All demolitions-crafted (registered Technical skill, resolves post drop-1), Kayson-bound per (a)=b — his back-room stock is canon-textual; Drop G re-binds R enforcement. **Thermal detonator stays uncraftable** (X-class icon, pinned; Drop G black-market call at best).
- **Deferred wholesale with reasons:** gas/spore/glop/smoke (effect-primary, no consumer), mines + shaped charges + detonite + thermite (demolition-placement/breaching mechanics — their own pass), electronet (restraint-gated), missiles (launcher/mount-gated), anti-vehicle grenade + **Lowickan Firegems** (contraband band → Drop G; the Firegems hyperdrive-sabotage device is noted for the cartel/espionage plot lane).
- **Tests:** `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_d.py` (17 — rubric recompute; q-bands; chemical-primary mix; demolitions+Kayson binding; skill resolution; new-row stats; retro flags; single_use defaults-false sweep over ordinary weapons; thermal-not-craftable pin; consumption hook presence + default-damage guard + declare-returns-success + armor-slot-preserving write). Sandbox: 256 green (craft A–D + P0 + crafting_state + skill-keys + combat batches incl. the session54 umbrella).
- **Files:** `engine/weapons.py`, `parser/combat_commands.py`, `data/weapons.yaml`, `data/schematics.yaml`, `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_d.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-11 — P2P hard cap removed: tax kept, velocity alert added — *same-day drop 5*
**ECON.p2p_cap_review = a (explicit sign-off; reverses audit v2 §2.4).** Under vendor segmentation (a), crafters are the supply chain and a single quality item legitimately trades above the old 1,500-cr cap — the cap now fought the core loop, and its own design note conceded multi-alt funneling only slows linearly under caps. Volume telemetry replaces volume refusal.
- **Removed:** both S51 enforcement blocks — the offer-time check and the race-safe accept-time recheck — and the `P2P_DAILY_CAP` constant. Nothing in the trade path refuses on volume.
- **Kept:** the 5% transaction tax (`p2p_tax` sink, floor 1 cr), the `p2p_transfer` ledger tag, the alt-account [TRADE BLOCKED] prohibition (both item and credit paths — session44's pins untouched), `get_daily_p2p_outgoing` + the 24h window constant.
- **Added:** `engine.economy_alerts.evaluate_p2p_velocity_alert` — caution at **1,500** (the old cap, repurposed as the alert band) and critical at **7,500**, fail-safe on malformed input; a `format_alert_line` p2p branch; generic severity/direction/net fields so the existing `@economy` readouts render it unchanged; and a **fail-open post-trade hook** (telemetry can never disturb a completed trade — mirrors the faucet throttle's posture). Thresholds are T3.19 tunables.
- **Old-policy pins rewritten WITH the drop, not skipped:** `test_tier2_tuning_batch.TestP2PCap` (now pins the constant's ABSENCE + the alert band), `test_session51_economy_hardening.TestP2PDailyCapConstants` (cap gone, window stays; the DB-harness query tests are policy-neutral and untouched), and the EE8 smoke scenario — renamed `ee8_p2p_large_trade_flows_and_alerts`: a 6,000-cr trade completes end-to-end, the tax shows, and the sender's volume lands in the alert ring buffer.
- **Tests:** `tests/test_econ_p2p_cap_removal.py` (16 — comment-stripped source pins that no volume block remains / tax + tags survive / the hook is fail-open / alt block intact ×2 paths; evaluator bands + fail-safe + readout-shape compatibility + format branch + ring-buffer round trip; reversed-pin guards on all three rewritten sites so a future "fix the test by restoring the cap" fails loudly). Sandbox ran the S51 DB-harness suites for real (aiosqlite/bcrypt/aiohttp installed): economy batch 105 green.
- **Files:** `parser/builtin_commands.py`, `engine/economy_alerts.py`, `tests/test_econ_p2p_cap_removal.py` (new), `tests/test_tier2_tuning_batch.py`, `tests/test_session51_economy_hardening.py`, `tests/smoke/scenarios/economy_extended.py`, `tests/smoke/test_smoke_economy_extended.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-11 — Gundark Drop C: non-powered armor + the armorer trainer + a v22 latent — *same-day drop 4*
10 schematics + 10 `type: armor` rows + the teacher, per gundark plan §3.1/§5/§8 Drop C under decisions (a)=b and 4a, the mechanical-use mandate, and a registry-reality call: **armor rows live in `data/weapons.yaml`** — wear, soak, and sheet all read the weapon registry, so the plan's separate `armor.yaml` was superseded by extend-don't-add (the Drop A branch comment updated to match).
- **Roster** — Avail 1 (q25): Koromondain underlayer vest (+1D+2/+2) · Concussion Vest (+1D phys) · Link Armor (full mesh, +1D/+2, −1D Dex, "Jedi wore it centuries ago" era texture). Avail 2 (q40): Riot Armor (+2D/+1D) · Camo Scout Armor (+1D/+2) · **Blast Vest (ablative)** — the §10 worked-sample item itself (+2/+1D, 3,000 cr). Avail 3 (q55): Castaan Staad (concealable Twi'lek craftwork) · Coynite Battle Armor (+2D/+2D, −1D, the 150-cr book-quirk priced as written per §5.3 — the q55 materials are the real cost; flagged as a price-sanity watch) · Ubese Raider (+2D/+1D, no penalty) · Flex-Armor TY1 (Old Republic full suit, −1D). Sub-systems with no consumer (camo spot bonus, IR alarm, enviro filter/flash-guard, swim mods, layering, armor mods) are notes, never fields. **Curated out:** near-collisions (CT3 helmet vs blast_helmet, Corellian 611 vs Ubese) and identity-is-the-unmodeled-mechanic items (Reflec conditional weave, Smasher servo rig, Stalker/Dura integrated suites, Doubler holo).
- **§3.2 powered/space suits DEFERRED wholesale** (pinned by test): `powersuit operation` is not a registered skill and weapon mounts have no consumer — that family needs its own design pass, not piecemeal rows. §3.3 attachments route to their gates (net gun → CRAFT.HOOK.restraints; launchers → mounts).
- **Trainer:** **Sela Tarn**, original character (Q1), ex-Judicial quartermaster, seeded at **Kayson's Weapon Shop** via `npcs_drop_craft_c_armorer.yaml` + an era.yaml load line — co-located per the 2026-06-02 Tatooine density directive (one storefront, two trades). `trainer: true` + `train_skills: [armor_repair]`; all 10 schematics `trainer_npc: Sela Tarn`, granted on talk (pinned end-to-end through `add_known_schematic`).
- **⚑ v22 LATENT FIX — armor Dexterity penalties have NEVER applied.** Data stores penalties signed per the book (`"-1D"`); `DicePool.parse("-1D")` silently returns (0,0); all three combat consumers therefore subtracted zero — Bounty Hunter Armor's −1D included, since v22. The producer (`get_armor_dex_penalty`) now returns the **magnitude** (consumers subtract via `apply_wound_penalty(pool, pen.dice)`), fixing every signed row old and new at one chokepoint. **WINDOWS WATCH ITEM #2:** combat pools for anyone in penalty armor correctly drop; tests pinning the old free-heavy-armor math will flip.
- **Drop-1 ripple fixed in the trainer surface:** the skill-trainer menu's raw `skills.get(underscore_key)` showed a trained PC's bonus as 0 (and pre-unification, underscore `train_skills` entries were silently OMITTED from menus via the registry miss — Venn's list was incomplete). Canonicalized at the menu key.
- **Logged, not built:** `OBS.quality_and_boosts_not_combat_read` — combat sources damage AND protection from the registry by key, so crafted quality and experiment boosts never reach combat math (quality = condition/value/experiment-base today, convention-consistent; experiment boosts may be display-only). Needs a deliberate quality→combat-stats design pass.
- **Tests:** `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_c.py` (20 — §10-anchored unit helper + recompute ×10; q-bands; composite>metal mix + size totals; rows/protection/dex/cost vs extraction; **soak reads parse every row incl. the pip-only `"+2"` forms this drop introduces**; dex-penalty magnitude + the BH-armor latent pin; full-loop landing-dict→`carried_to_instance`→`find_carried_gear(want_armor=True)` and the not-a-weapon negative; NPC file shape/room-exists/era-loads/binding/teach-grant ×10/skill-resolves; no-contraband; no-powered-suits pin). Sandbox: 220 green (craft A/B/C + P0 + crafting_state + skill-keys + combat batches) + era-clean 12.
- **Files:** `data/weapons.yaml`, `data/schematics.yaml`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/npcs_drop_craft_c_armorer.yaml` (new), `data/worlds/clone_wars/era.yaml`, `engine/character.py`, `parser/npc_commands.py`, `parser/crafting_commands.py`, `tests/test_craft_p2_gundark_drop_c.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-11 — Dead inline-onclick class: tour + every Webify modal close button — *same-day drop 3*
**Found live by Brian on the first minute of onboarding testing:** the UI-7 first-run tour's NEXT and SKIP TOUR buttons did nothing. Root cause is a CLASS, not an instance: `static/client.html`'s entire inline script is a strict-mode IIFE, so its function declarations are closure-scoped — but inline `onclick="..."` attributes resolve in GLOBAL scope at click time. Every handler referenced from markup without a `window.NAME = NAME` export is a silently dead button (console ReferenceError, zero UI effect). The audit found **12 dead handlers spanning the whole Webify wave**, not just the tour: `advanceOnboardTour`/`endOnboardTour`/`showOnboardTour` (UI-7 NEXT/SKIP/the TRAINING-head ? replay) **plus the close-✕ and backdrop-click handlers of every modal the wave added** — inventory (UI-4a), shop (UI-4b), board (UI-5), craft (UI-8), and city. ESC paths worked (bound via addEventListener inside the IIFE), which is exactly why the modals *seemed* fine in testing. 17 of 31 onclick names had followed the file's export convention; the Webify additions consistently skipped the line.
- **Fix (extend-don't-add):** `window.X = X` exports at each definition site, matching the file's existing convention, with a class-explaining comment at the first cluster. Inline script re-parsed clean (`new Function` syntax check).
- **Regression net — the class made unrepresentable:** `tests/spa/test_client_onclick_exports.py` (4) — (1) a whole-file SWEEP: every function invoked from any inline onclick must be window-exported in client.html or globally provided by a loaded external script (parser ignores `.method(` calls so `event.stopPropagation()` can't false-positive); **bite-verified** by removing one export from a scratch copy and watching the sweep name it. (2–3) instance pins for the 12 repaired handlers + a markup-still-references guard so pins retire consciously. (4) a DYNAMIC jsdom test under `runScripts: 'dangerously'` (the only mode that executes attribute handlers) that extracts the LIVE tour JS block and the LIVE action-button markup from client.html at test time, then dispatches REAL clicks: 1/4 → NEXT → 2/4; SKIP hides the overlay and sets `m3_onboard_tour_done`; `maybeShowOnboardTour` is then a no-op while the TRAINING-head ? force-replay still shows — the exact end-to-end path Brian clicked.
- **Why no prior test caught it:** the spa suites exercise the M3 modules' render contracts and the wireup tests do static script-tag checks — nothing ever executed client.html's inline handlers. The new sweep closes that for every current and future onclick.
- **Sandbox:** new suite 4 green · wireup 42a/b/c + m3_onboard 36 green · modal-family spa (craft/board/inventory/shop) 14 green.
- **Files:** `static/client.html`, `tests/spa/test_client_onclick_exports.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-11 — Skill-key resolution unification: crafter training NEVER counted — *same-day drop 1*
**P0-class, found during Drop B pre-flight and reproduced live before any claim was made.** The repo carried two key dialects for the SAME skills with no translation between them: space-form (SkillRegistry keys, chargen templates, train/CP writes, MISSION_SKILL_MAP, combat literals) vs underscore-form (every `schematics.yaml skill_required`; most NPC yaml skill blocks — 46× `melee_combat:`, 43× `first_aid:`). Cross-dialect lookups silently resolved UNTRAINED, and in `_skill_to_attr`, to the **wrong governing attribute** (the `"perception"` miss-default).
- **Reproduction (the headline):** a PC with Blaster Repair **3D** + Technical **3D** crafting a blaster rolled **2D raw Perception** — `pool_str: "2D"`. Nine of twelve `skill_required` values mis-resolved on BOTH axes. P0.1 made craft roll the right *name*; the name never *resolved*. Net: crafter build investment was disconnected from craft quality for every PC since crafting shipped.
- **Two more live instances of the class:** (1) `MISSION_SKILL_MAP`'s technical mission rolls plural `"space transports repair"` while chargen stores the registry-canonical singular — Space Transport Repair training never counted on missions. (2) Combat queries `Character.get_skill_pool("melee combat")` space-form against underscore NPC dicts — **every melee_combat-keyed NPC attacked and parried at raw attribute** (paper-tiger brawlers, 46+ NPCs).
- **Fix — one translation point, both resolution surfaces (extend-don't-add):** `engine.character.canonical_skill_key()` (lower/strip/underscores→spaces + a SMALL sanctioned alias map: `computer_prog`→computer programming/repair, plural-transport→singular, `pickpocket`→pick pocket), routed through `SkillRegistry.get`, `Character.get_skill_pool` (+ a miss-path canonical scan over stored keys for the NPC dicts), `Character.advance_skill` (write convergence), `perform_skill_check` ingress, `_get_skill_pool` (+ the same miss-path scan), `_skill_to_attr` (+ sanctioned `craft lightsaber`→technical fallback for the T5 schematic), and the `train` command's ingress (so `train blaster_repair` — which the registry now ACCEPTS — cannot create a split-key skills dict).
- **Regression net:** `tests/test_skill_key_resolution.py` (22) — helper basics/aliases/idempotence; registry both-dialects; the governing-attribute table for ALL schematic skill_required values + a whole-catalog "perception default unreachable" sweep; the four `_get_skill_pool` lookup quadrants incl. the plural-transport mission quadrant; end-to-end `perform_skill_check` trained-pool pin (6D, not 2D); `Character.get_skill_pool` underscore-NPC quadrants; **whole-catalog structural gate** (every `skill_required` must canonicalize to a registered skill or the sanctioned set — future data-side spellings fail at data-entry time, which is what makes Drop B+'s rubric mass-application safe); MISSION_SKILL_MAP resolution; write-site source pins ×3.
- **⚑ WINDOWS WATCH ITEM (deliberate behavior change):** melee/multi-word-skill NPC pools correctly JUMP (untrained→trained); craft and technical-mission rolls now include training. Any test pinning the old untrained rolls will flip — those pins were pinning the bug. Sandbox: 125 green across combat/skill batches (test_combat_mechanics, test_skill_checks_unit, test_drop_h_combat_npcs) + the 22 new.
- **Files:** `engine/character.py`, `engine/skill_checks.py`, `parser/cp_commands.py`, `tests/test_skill_key_resolution.py` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

The P0 output-type parity test learned the tuple-membership branch form.

### 2026-06-10 — CRAFT.P1: persistence no-op class FIXED (E7's first catch) — *same-day drop 7*
Brian's suite run on the drops 3–6 rollup: **2 failed / 8,039 passed** — both failures mine, both fixed.
- **⚑ The headline: `db.save_character(id)` with NO kwargs is a silent no-op** (`if not fields: return`, db/database.py:1813). Seven sites believed they were saving; nothing was. **E7 caught it on its very first Windows run** — craft reported success, `consumables.medpac=0` on re-fetch — which is precisely the invariant that smoke was built to hold. The same audit then mapped the full class:
  - **`_save_char`** (the helper every crafting verb trusts) — now persists `attributes=char["attributes"]`, with a docstring pinning why it is DELIBERATELY attributes-only: `db.add_to_inventory` does its own DB read-modify-write, so a blanket dict-inventory write after a delivery would clobber the landed item (F2 evaporation reborn as a stale-dict overwrite).
  - **Craft component consumption never persisted** — `resolve_craft` consumes dict-side; with `_save_char` a no-op that meant **infinite materials across reload, for every output type**. Fixed with an ordering-critical save: `inventory=char["inventory"]` immediately after `resolve_craft`, BEFORE `_deliver_item`'s DB RMW (saving after would clobber the delivered item; a source-order pin enforces this).
  - **Survey** — add_resource (inventory) + cooldown (attributes), neither persisted. Now an explicit both-column save; survey also joined the `crafting_state` push set (the panel stages `survey` — without a refresh the MATERIALS section went silently stale; ledger §1.9 updated).
  - **Teach target** — PC-taught schematics never persisted across reload. Explicit `attributes=` kwarg.
  - **Space salvage credits** — dict mutation + no-op save: never persisted AND bypassed the `adjust_credits` ledger chokepoint. Rerouted through `adjust_credits(char_id, amt, "space_salvage")` with the dict synced from its return — the economy invariant restored.
  - **Space salvage resources** — never persisted. Explicit `inventory=` kwarg.
  - **`encounter_anomaly._award_resources`** — doubly broken: `add_resource(dict(char), …)` mutated a THROWAWAY COPY, then no-op saved. Anomaly resource rewards never landed. Now mutates a working dict and persists its inventory.
- **Regression net (the class, not the instances):** `TestPersistenceNoOpClass` in `tests/test_craft_p0_remediation.py` (+7 → 35) — an **AST-walk sweep** over all of `parser/` + `engine/` asserting no `save_character` call exists with positional args and zero keywords (AST, not regex, so docstrings describing the old bug and kwarg/`**splat` calls can't false-positive — the first regex draft flagged 4, of which 3 were false positives and 1 was my own docstring); the `_save_char` attributes-only pin; the consumption-before-delivery ordering pin; survey both-columns + push pin; teach kwarg pin; the salvage→`adjust_credits` ledger pin; the anomaly real-dict pin.
- **TODO hygiene:** `last_updated` restored to bare ISO (`2026-06-10`); the prose moved to a new `last_updated_note` field. The repo's own hygiene suite (9 tests) green in sandbox.
- **Clobber-safety audit:** `check_spacer_quest` operates on the same session dict the craft flow mutates, so the terminal attributes save carries both the consumable and any quest update — no cross-write. `BuyResourcesCommand` verified already correct (adjust_credits + explicit inventory save).
- **Sandbox verification:** AST ×3 on touched modules; core batch **116 green** (P0/P1 35 + crafting_state 8 + hygiene 9 + syn6c 40 + untangle 15 + stragglers 9).
- **Files:** `parser/crafting_commands.py`, `parser/space_commands.py`, `engine/encounter_anomaly.py`, `web_client_vision_and_protocol_v1_4.md`, `tests/test_craft_p0_remediation.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-10 — CRAFT.P0 IMPLEMENTED: crafting remediation + inventory-aware gear verbs — *same-day drop 5*
Implements `crafting_integration_design_pass_v1.md` §2 in full, under Brian's eight design decisions (all option-a + rubric sign-off + ABI acceptance) and the new **mechanical-use mandate** (§3.2a: every craftable item must have a defined gameplay use; restraints + Force detector tiered long-pole as `CRAFT.HOOK.*`).
- **P0.1 — phantom re-delivery (T2.DEF.t5_discoverability, all five bugs):** `craft` passes the real `SkillCheckResult` (except-branch builds an auto-success `SimpleNamespace`) and rolls **`skill_required`**; `schematics` reads `components`+`skill_required` with a `[*]` craftable flag + per-component min-quality; `resources` reads `quantity` (the `r['amount']` KeyError crash); `check_resources` distinguishes **quantity-blocked** ("need 3x metal — you have 1x") from **quality-blocked** ("have 5x but only 0x at q75+, best grade q72 — refine or survey higher-grade"), type still named (syn6c-compatible).
- **P0.2–P0.4 — every craft landing → `db.add_to_inventory`** (fires the F.8.c.2.b₂ `item_acquired` hook the old paths bypassed): weapon (was: appended to nonexistent `session.items` → **evaporated**), component + survival_gear (was: bare-list column writes that **destroyed resource stacks** under dict format), and a **NEW `equipment` branch** (6 schematics previously consumed components and produced nothing) + an unhandled-output_type guard that logs and tells the player instead of silently eating components. The two mis-typed t5 ship parts re-typed `equipment`→`component` with `stat_target/stat_boost/cargo_weight` (surge converter: hyperdrive +3 — −0.25 multiplier per effective pip, 0.5 floor; engine core: speed +2 = one-slot cap reach, the T5 value proposition).
- **P0.5 —** `hazards._has_mitigation` reads dict-format inventory (`items`) and the canonical equipment slots via `equipment_keys` — survival gear **never mitigated** under dict format and the equipped/worn checks read nonexistent row columns.
- **P0.6 — `electronic` formalized** (decision 1a) in `RESOURCE_TYPES` + `HARVESTABLE_RESOURCE_TYPES` + city survey yields (chemical/energy/**electronic**). Closes two latent bugs: sensor_mask/comm_jammer permanently uncraftable, and **`buyresources electronic` charging credits then failing the add** (the vendor priced it at 25 cr all along). syn6c constant pins updated (11→12, harvestable+electronic) with provenance.
- **P0.7 — dangling weapon keys statted** (decision 6a): `stun_pistol` (2D stun-only, 3-10/30/60, 300 cr) + `blaster_carbine` (StarSlasher, 5D, 3-25/50/250, 900 cr) re-statted to WEG D6 from the Gundark extraction. **`stun_only` is wired, not decorative** (mechanical-use mandate): new `WeaponData.stun_only` + loader + the attack declaration **forces stun mode** ("only fires stun bolts") — the v22 stun-capability gate's mirror.
- **⚑ P0.9 — NEW finding, fixed: the gear-verb surface leaked in three directions.** `equip <name>`/`wear <name>` **MINTED free pristine vendor instances from the registry** — no ownership check, no credit cost, an unlogged faucet that also made crafted/modified instances unequippable (UI-4a's panel stages `equip <item>` *expecting* inventory-aware behavior; the economy audit's prized decay loop and the experiment system were both nullified). `unequip`/`remove` **DESTROYED** the slotted instance. `buy` **destroyed the displaced weapon**. Now: equip/wear pull the carried instance from inventory (helpful refusals distinguish "doesn't exist" / "is armor, use wear" / "you don't own one — buy, craft, or loot"); displaced gear and unequipped/removed gear return to inventory; buy returns the displaced weapon. New `engine/items.py` helpers `find_carried_gear`/`instance_to_carried`/`carried_to_instance` (one matching+conversion surface). Acquisition is now exclusively buy/craft/loot/trade. No tutorial chain or chargen path relied on the mint (verified — chains teach no `equip`; chargen grants credits, not gear).
- **P0.8 — tests:** `tests/test_craft_p0_remediation.py` (28 — check_resources diagnostics ×4; electronic ×4 incl. a whole-catalog undeclared-component-type pin; output_type-coverage ×3 incl. catalog-vs-branch parity; weapon-output resolution ×2 incl. whole-catalog dangling pin; hazard shapes ×4; carried-gear helpers ×3; comment-stripped source pins ×8). **E7/E8 smoke scenarios UN-DEFERRED** via direct DB state seeding (schematic grant + component stacks + canonical equipment write — no cooldown/node harness extensions needed): E7 runs learn→list→craft and asserts a reported success has actually landed (the scenario that would have caught F1.D and F2); E8 equips a crafted-pattern instance and runs one real experiment (would have caught the "no weapon equipped" reader regression). RNG-tolerant: legitimate failed rolls don't flake; crashes and success-without-item always fail.
- **Sandbox verification:** AST ×11, YAML ×2; 92 green in the core batch (P0 28 + syn6c 40 + untangle 15 + stragglers 9) + session56 umbrellas + npc_buyback + syn6a green; economy_validation/session51 import-skip (pytest/aiosqlite absent — environment, not regression). **Windows full suite is the gate for E7/E8 and the verb-level behavior.**
- **Files:** `engine/crafting.py`, `engine/hazards.py`, `engine/weapons.py`, `engine/items.py`, `parser/crafting_commands.py`, `parser/builtin_commands.py`, `parser/combat_commands.py`, `parser/space_commands.py`, `data/schematics.yaml`, `data/weapons.yaml`, `tests/test_craft_p0_remediation.py` (new), `tests/test_syn6c_t5_crafting_and_harvest_nodes.py`, `tests/smoke/scenarios/economy_progression.py`, `tests/smoke/test_smoke_economy_progression.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-10 — Suite triage: `+sheet` NameError FIX + equipment-reader straggler sweep (13 sites) + Lane-D manifest count — *same-day drop 3*
Brian's 2026-06-10 full-suite run: **6 failed / 7,988 passed**. Two root causes, one of which unspooled into a full reader-migration audit.
- **Root cause 1 — `engine/sheet_renderer.py::render_game_sheet` NameError (5 of 6 failures: H7, CW4, GCW4, G3, T4).** The equipment untangle migrated the weapon block to `equipment_keys()` but the worn-armor block still referenced the deleted `equip_data` local → every `+sheet` crashed. Fixed by hoisting one `equipment_keys()` call for both slots.
- **The crash prompted a symbol-level audit of EVERY remaining raw `equipment` reader/writer** (grep HEAD, per the phantom-delivery invariant). The untangle handoff claimed "all readers/writers migrated"; HEAD disagreed — **12 more un-migrated sites**, all silently misbehaving under canonical per-slot storage:
  - `parser/combat_commands.py::_resolve_equipped_weapon` — read legacy shape-2 `"key"` → **`attack` ignored the equipped weapon** and fell back to default blaster 4D. → `equipment_keys`.
  - `parser/combat_commands.py::_apply_combat_wear` — `parse_equipment_json` → None → **weapon wear never applied post-combat**; the `serialize_equipment` persist clobbered armor. → `read_equipment`/`write_equipment`, armor preserved.
  - `parser/builtin_commands.py` ×4 — look-at "Wielding" + room-contents "wielding a" (raw `eq["weapon"]` is now an instance dict → line silently vanished); **sell-equipped** (`parse_equipment_json` → "Nothing equipped to sell" always; `serialize_equipment(None)` wiped armor on sale); `+weapons` equipped footer; `+armor` "Wearing" footer (instance dict passed as registry key). → `equipment_keys`/`read_equipment`/`write_equipment`.
  - `parser/crafting_commands.py` — `_prep_weapon_and_schematic` (**`experiment` always said "no weapon equipped"**); `_handle_fumble` all four outcomes (exploded/broken wrote `"{}"`, jammed/quality_loss wrote shape 2 — **every fumble wiped worn armor**). → canonical, armor read once and preserved across all outcomes.
  - `parser/shop_commands.py::_find_in_inventory` — **equipped weapon could never be stocked on a vendor droid**. → `read_equipment`.
  - `engine/vendor_droids.py::stock_droid` — equipment-source stocking wrote `equipment="{}"`, **wiping the armor slot**. → weapon-slot-only clear.
  - `parser/force_commands.py::_apply_disarm` (PC branch) — raw `pop("weapon")` worked on canonical but left a residual legacy shape-2 weapon equipped. → normalize via `read_equipment`/`write_equipment`.
- **`parse_equipment_json`/`serialize_equipment` docstrings now carry LEGACY warnings** (shape-2 only / armor-clobbering); zero live engine/parser callers remain (one test fixture intentionally exercises shape-2 read tolerance and stays).
- **Root cause 2 — `tests/test_world_writer.py::test_manifest_room_count`** golden count stale at 280; Lane D (2026-06-07) added 7 Geonosis rooms (Gladiator Barracks interior + E'Y-Akh anchors) and missed this pin. → 287, with provenance comment.
- **Tests:** `tests/test_equipment_reader_stragglers.py` (NEW, 9 — exact `+sheet` crash repro on canonical-both-slots + all-shapes render tolerance + `equip_data` symbol gone; slot-preserving round-trips; **source pins**: zero live `parse_equipment_json`/`serialize_equipment` callers, zero bare `equipment="{}"` wipe-writes outside chargen). Sandbox: AST green on all 10 touched modules; `test_equipment_untangle` (15) + new suite (9) green. **Windows full suite is the acceptance gate for the 5 smoke failures** — they exercise the live server stack.
- **⚑ Phantom recurrence caught:** `web_onboarding_design_v1.md` and `web_client_vision_and_protocol_v1_4.md` were listed in the UI-5/6/7 rollup's Files but are **absent from Brian's 2026-06-10 11:35 HEAD upload** (the upload script excludes no `.md`) — the v1_4 ledger was thus phantomed TWICE (06-07 rollup, then again in the 06-10 reconstruction's packaging). ### 2026-06-10 — Webify UI-7 (web onboarding: training panel + coach pulses + first-run tour) DESIGNED + IMPLEMENTED — *same-session drop 2*
Brian's mandate: onboarding is a major retention feature — handle it well and thoroughly. UI-7 had **no accepted design** (the Webify pack deferred it by design until the loop shipped), so this drop ships the design AND the implementation: **`web_onboarding_design_v1.md`** (repo root) is the contract; this entry is the ledger.
- **The load-bearing finding (HEAD audit, design §1):** UI-7 is NOT a tutorial system — the tutorial system is BUILT and live. Nine CW chains in `chains.yaml` (authored NPC briefings, per-step `teaches` command lists, objectives, completion contracts, graduation rooms); **web chargen already starts the chain** (`server/api.py` writes `attributes.tutorial_chain` at creation — a new web player logs in standing in their chain's starting room on step 1); the 11 F.8.c.2.b completion hooks fire live; graduation teleports work; `chain status`/`chain attempt` are the Telnet parity surface. `chain_events.get_active_step_info`'s docstring even said *"Used by web HUD"* — **which nothing in the web path did**. UI-7 fills that aspirational seam: the accepted concept sentence from the implementation handoff ("coach-mark layer over the existing client, `onboarding_state`, the F.8.c.2.b hooks"), expanded and built.
- **Layer A — training panel.** New `onboarding_state` push → a right-column `.side-panel` (FIRST in the stack — the new player's primary surface): chain name + STEP n/M, a **step rail** (done/current/ahead dots), step title, NPC line, the authored **briefing** (`npc_intro` — re-display of dialogue the NPC already streamed), the **objective** (mirrors the UI-6 line), and **teaches chips** — one per corpus `teaches` token, click → stage `token + ' '` (never auto-sent). **The panel cannot invent a verb: it renders only what chains.yaml teaches.** `completion_type == 'skill_check_passed'` adds an **ATTEMPT** chip staging the real `chain attempt`. **Step-advance flash** (`STEP COMPLETE` band + rail-dot pop) on pushed-step increase — credits rewards already toast via the UI-6 `credit_event` riders, zero new reward plumbing. **Graduation card** (`CHAIN COMPLETE — <name>`, DISMISS hides the panel) on the active→graduated transition.
  - **Producer (extend, not add):** `engine/chain_events.py::build_onboarding_state(char)` layered on `get_active_step_info`, which gains ADDITIVE fields (`chain_total_steps`, `teaches`, `npc_role`, `npc_intro`, `completed_steps` — list copies, corpus can't be mutated; `chain status`/`chain attempt`/tests unaffected). Graduated payload resolves `chain_name` from the corpus with an id fallback. Never raises (malformed attrs → None).
  - **Push:** `server/session.py::_hud_sidebar_onboarding(char)` in the sidebar section of `send_hud_update` (needs only `char` — placed before the db-gated sidebar block). **Graduation memo** (`_last_chain_step`, the `_last_sent_credits` precedent): active → push every tick (idempotent render); graduated → push ONCE, only when the chain was active this session; **a reconnect after graduation pushes nothing**.
- **Layer B — quick-action coach pulses.** Teach tokens with EXISTING anchors pulse that button on step render: `look`→LOOK, `say`/`talk`→SAY, `+bounties`→JOBS. Finite CSS animation (~6 beats, then still — no nag, no JS cleanup). **No new anchors invented**; unmapped tokens (`+sheet`, `attack`, …) stay chip-only.
- **Layer C — first-run client tour.** Four sequential coach marks over the chrome (input bar → quick-action row → objective line → training panel): dim via the spotlight ring's spread shadow, caption card clamped to the viewport, NEXT/SKIP. Shown **once per browser** (`localStorage['m3_onboard_tour_done']`, try-wrapped per the `fk_clean_mode` convention — cosmetic browser state, never game state) and **only while a chain is active** (veterans/skippers never see it); steps with missing/hidden anchors are skipped, not spotlit blind. Replayable via the panel-head `?`.
- **Honesty rails (design §4):** no invented verbs; nothing web-exclusive (`chain status` + the streamed NPC dialogue are the text path); no producer-less fields — `in_step_location` ("wrong room" hint) was considered and **deferred to Phase 2** rather than half-built (needs a room-id↔slug resolve per tick); **tutorial_v2 core/electives are out of scope** (parallel elective system; logged, not silently absorbed). Phase 2 candidates logged in design §5 + the protocol ledger.
- **Tests:** `tests/test_onboarding_state.py` (8 — active shape/passthrough incl. completed_steps+total, skill-check exposure, graduated payload + unknown-chain fallback, no-chain None, malformed-attrs tolerance, **legacy `get_active_step_info` keys survive**, list-copy corpus isolation) + `tests/spa/test_m3_onboard.py` (4 jsdom — rail states + **exact `token + ' '` staging** + invented-verb-never guard + pulse-anchors-only [JOBS/LOOK/SAY, INV untouched]; ATTEMPT only for skill checks staging exact `chain attempt`; **first render never flashes / advance flashes once / same-step re-render quiet** + dot pop; graduation card + DISMISS callback + stages-nothing). `m3_onboard.js` added to the wireup load order. Chain-consumer regression sweep green (197 passed: f8c2b events/phase2/attempt/prereq+skill, chains yaml, plus the morning's UI-5/6 suites).
- **Files:** `web_onboarding_design_v1.md` (new), `engine/chain_events.py`, `server/session.py`, `static/client.html`, `static/spa/m3_onboard.js` (new), `tests/test_onboarding_state.py` (new), `tests/spa/test_m3_onboard.py` (new), `tests/spa/test_client_wireup_42a.py`, `web_client_vision_and_protocol_v1_4.md` (§1.8 + reserved), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-10 — Webify UI-5 (bounty board) + UI-6 (objective line + juice) IMPLEMENTED · `_hud_active_jobs` bounty-branch FIX · protocol-ledger v1_4 phantom CAUGHT + reconstructed
Continues the Webify package per `HANDOFF_webify_UI1_thru_UI4b_2026-06-07.md` §6 build order. **Delta-on-existing; token-only; real verbs only; Telnet untouched.**
- **UI-5 — Bounty board (NEW modal).** The `bounties` verb now also pushes a structured `board_state` to WebSocket clients (Telnet keeps `format_bounty_board` unchanged).
  - **Producer (extend, not add):** `engine/bounty_board.py::build_board_state(posted, claimed, now=None)` — pure/sync assembler: each contract is `BountyContract.to_dict()` **plus a server-derived `expires_in_secs`** (remaining seconds, clamped ≥0, `None` when no expiry — the client never trusts its own clock against the `expires_at` epoch); the viewer's CLAIMED contract is prepended and sets `claimed_id` (deduped if also in the posted list); malformed contracts are skipped, never raised.
  - **Push (parser):** `BountiesCommand` reuses the **same chain-visibility-filtered list** the Telnet text path renders (`filter_visible_bounties`), so tutorial-tagged contracts never leak to the web surface either; WS-gated via the established `Protocol.WEBSOCKET` pattern.
  - **Client:** `static/spa/m3_board.js` (`window.M3Board`) — tier filter row with the PAY_RANGES legend, contract cards (tier stud, target line, crime, reward + `+N alive`, **live 1s countdown** going `--warn` under 30 min, expandable DETAILS = posting org / contract id / tip, **CHAIN tag** on `chain_bounty_id`), **claimed card pinned first** (then reward desc) with a CLAIMED badge. **Real verbs only:** ACCEPT stages `bountyclaim <id>` (suppressed everywhere while the viewer holds a claim — one at a time), TRACK TARGET stages `bountytrack`; **no abandon verb exists at HEAD so none is offered**; staged, never auto-sent. `M3Board.stop()` drains the countdown interval; the modal close path calls it (M3Region convention). **Tier hue ramp is token-only** (extra `--text-dim` → average `--text` → novice `--accent` → veteran `--accent-bright` → superior `--warn` — mirrors the Telnet ANSI escalation inside the pad palette). `client.html`: board modal (shares `.inv-modal` chrome), `handleBoardState`/open/close/backdrop, `stageFromBoard`, dispatch case, script tag, **JOBS quick-action button** (sends the real `bounties` verb — room-independent, unlike a shop trigger), token-only `m3b-*` CSS. **Scope honesty:** `board_state` carries the NPC contract board only — Dark-Side Notoriety (prestige, no credits) is a different surface on the PC bounty board and is not folded in.
  - **Tests:** `tests/test_board_state.py` (7 — shape, derived/clamped `expires_in_secs`, claimed-first + `claimed_id`, dedup, empty/None, malformed-skip, chain passthrough) + `tests/spa/test_m3_board.py` (4 jsdom — reward-desc sort + **exact `bountyclaim <id>` verb** + abandon/breakfree-never guard; claimed-pinned + CLAIMED badge + **ACCEPT-suppressed-while-claimed** + exact `bountytrack`; tier filter + details expansion stage nothing; urgent-countdown class + null-expiry renders no countdown + empty state). `m3_board.js` added to `test_client_wireup_42a.py`'s pinned load order (stale "11 expected" docstring made count-agnostic — no count assertion existed).
- **UI-6 — Objective line + juice (BUFF on existing surfaces).**
  - **`hud_update.objective` (server):** `_hud_active_jobs` now derives a single orientation string via a new module-level `_objective_line(jobs)` (pure, sandbox-testable): first job wins; formats — tutorial → step objective, bounty → `Hunt <target> — <reward:,> cr bounty` (the design's shell format), mission → `label — objective`, smuggle → `label — reward cr`, quest → objective; 96-char ellipsis truncation; `""` = hide.
  - **Tutorial-chain job (extend the producer):** `_hud_active_jobs` now puts the **active tutorial-chain step first** (`{type:'tutorial', label: step.title, objective: step.objective}`) — corpus via `engine.chain_events._get_corpus` (the chain subsystem's cached loader; the HUD tick never re-reads chains.yaml). A player in the tutorial is the player who most needs the line.
  - **REAL BUG FIX — the bounty branch never fired:** `_hud_active_jobs` checked `accepted_by`/status `"accepted"`, but `BountyContract`'s fields are **`claimed_by`** and status **`"claimed"`** (`BountyStatus.CLAIMED`) — so the active-bounty HUD job has matched **no contract ever** since it shipped. Fixed to the real fields (direct str-enum equality, not `str()`-wrapping, which renders the member name on some Python versions).
  - **Client:** boxed `#g-objective` line atop the vitals card (between char-meta and VITALS; literal `▮▮` house glyphs preserved byte-identically on the untouched label), shown/hidden by `handleHudUpdate`. **Juice on the real `credit_event`:** a ~700ms cubic-ease **count-up** on `#g-credits` animating from `credits − delta` → `credits` (derived start → order-independent of the `hud_update` render; rAF-guarded with a direct-set fallback) and a 2.6s top-center **reward toast** (`+N cr` / `−N cr`, `--self`/`--warn` toned, `aria-live`). The pre-existing delta chip behavior is preserved verbatim; the producer is unchanged (no `reason` field invented — plumbing ledger tags through is a separate change, noted in the protocol ledger).
  - **Tests:** `tests/test_hud_objective.py` (12) — `_objective_line` per-type formats/priority/truncation/malformed-tolerance (pure), plus **functional `_hud_active_jobs` runs against the real board singleton** (reset in fixture teardown — singleton-isolation discipline): the bounty-branch fix proves the claimed contract now surfaces (and drives `objective`), other characters' claims don't, an active chain step (stub corpus through the `_get_corpus` seam) outranks a claimed bounty, and an inactive chain adds nothing.
- **⚑ PHANTOM-DELIVERY CAUGHT — `web_client_vision_and_protocol_v1_4.md`.** The 2026-06-07 rollup's CHANGELOG Files list names the protocol ledger as a delivered new file, but it is **absent from Brian's HEAD** (upload script excludes no `.md`; older root docs round-trip fine) — the zip never carried it. **Reconstructed this drop** from the handoff §5 pinned shapes, with a provenance note, and extended with the newly shipped `board_state` + `hud_update.objective` + `credit_event` riders, the reserved entries (`buffs[]`, `shop_state mode:'vendor'`), and the message conventions. The standing grep-HEAD-on-pickup discipline is what caught it.
- **Sandbox verification:** AST-clean on all touched Python; JS parse-clean on `m3_board.js`; 19 new python tests + 4 new jsdom tests green; full prior-Webify SPA sweep green (wireup 9, shop 3, inventory 3, region 5, chips 4, scroll 3); touched-module regression sweep green (`test_bounty_board_unit`, `test_session55_jobs_umbrellas`, `test_equipment_untangle`, `test_inventory_state` — 108 passed). DB/server-integration tests not runnable in-sandbox (aiohttp/aiosqlite absent) — run the full suite on the Windows box.
- **Files:** `engine/bounty_board.py`, `parser/bounty_commands.py`, `server/session.py`, `static/client.html`, `static/spa/m3_board.js` (new), `tests/test_board_state.py` (new), `tests/test_hud_objective.py` (new), `tests/spa/test_m3_board.py` (new), `tests/spa/test_client_wireup_42a.py`, `web_client_vision_and_protocol_v1_4.md` (new — reconstructed), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.

### 2026-06-07 — Webify UI-1 (scroll-on-move) + UI-2 (Region panel) + UI-3 (combat condition chips) + equipment-instance untangle + UI-4a (inventory panel) + UI-4b (shop card) IMPLEMENTED — *session rollup*
First three implementation drops of the Webify package (per `HANDOFF_webify_ui_implementation_2026-06-07.md`). **Delta on the existing m3 client — no map/tier/composition rework; token-only; real symbols only.**
- **UI-1 — scroll-on-move fix (client-only).** `renderEventToActiveLog` now special-cases `room-enter`: a room change is explicit navigation, so it **re-anchors the stream to the new-room banner regardless of scroll position** (the clunk — while scrolled up in history a move silently bumped the unread pill and you never "landed"). New `anchorRoomEnterRow()` pins via the existing `scrollTop` idiom + a rAF re-pin once desc/exits lay out; a **one-beat highlight sweep** (`@keyframes m3-room-sweep`, glows the existing `--accent` border — no new colour, mode-aware) draws the eye. **Telnet untouched** (render-only). Test `tests/spa/test_m3_scroll_on_move.py` extracts the *real* shipped functions (can't drift).
- **UI-2 — Region-control panel (NEW side panel).** `static/spa/m3_region.js` (`window.M3Region`) renders the `region_state` push: region name + security badge, ownership, a **0–150 influence ladder** with **50 (foothold) / 100 (dominant)** threshold ticks and the **viewer's row boxed `◂ you`**, weekly **resource chips** (>1.05 green / <0.95 red / best glows), and an **active-contest tug-of-war** + live countdown. Right-column **`.side-panel` sibling** of the room panel, collapsible like the rest.
  - **Server push (add-beside):** `server/session.py::_hud_sidebar_region` emits `region_state` only when `room["wilderness_region_id"]` is set (viewer org from `char["faction_id"]`); city/ship/interior rooms emit nothing. Client **hides the panel on every room change** (`handleHudUpdate`) and the push that follows **re-shows it** iff still in a region, so leaving a region to a city clears it cleanly. Telnet silently drops the structured message (region prose still flows via the stream / `region` command).
  - **Producer extended additively:** `engine/territory_display.py::get_region_data_block` gains a keyword-only `viewer_org_code`, per-influence `org_name` + `is_viewer`, and a top-level `viewer_org`. The 6 existing `TestRegionDataBlock` cases stay green.
  - **Don't-invent rails honoured:** only `secured/contested/lawless`; only `foothold/dominant/no_presence`; **unaligned PCs see contest/outlook disabled, not hidden**. **B3/Q1-clean** (org *names* come from the server-resolved `org_name`; codes are only humanized — no Imperial/Rebel literal can leak). **Token-only** (the prototype's per-org rainbow is dropped for the `:root` accent/self/warn tokens).
  - **Tests:** `tests/spa/test_m3_region.py` (jsdom render contract — highlight, ladder %, ticks, chips, contest tug + countdown, spectating state — plus static wire-up + server-push guards).
  - **Deferred:** `GET /api/region/{slug}` (the on-enter push covers the live case; noted in TODO).
- **UI-3 — Combat condition chips (BUFF on the built combat HUD).** Surfaces the just-shipped Lane-A creature conditions that were invisible in the HUD. `engine/combat.py::to_hud_dict` now puts **normalized `poison_stacks` + `restraint`** on each combatant in the existing `combat_state` push (engine keys `onset_left`/`rounds_left` → push `onset`/`ticks_left`). New `m3_combat_inspector.js::buildConditionChips(c, isYou)` appends a `.combatant-chips` rail to each pip: **POISON** chip (green, `×N`, `onset N` or `<dmg>·<ticks>t`, **pulses while biting** at onset 0) and **RESTRAINT** chip (red, **GRAPPLED/CONSTRICTED/CHOKED** by `kind` + `hold_damage`, **pulses**). Returns `null` for non-creature fights → **zero DOM** in ordinary combat. Token-only CSS (`@keyframes m3-chip-pulse`, glow via `currentColor`).
  - **TWEAK/Q5 — restraint chip is DISPLAY-ONLY (no `breakfree` button).** Confirmed at HEAD: a held actor can't flee and the break-free roll runs automatically at round end (`_resolve_flee`); there is **no ground `breakfree` verb** (space-boarding only). The chip shows the hold + a `can't flee — auto break-free at round end` note (for the held viewer) and **stages no command**.
  - **Buff chip DEFERRED (no producer at HEAD).** Buffs aren't wired into combat (no `Combatant.buffs`; the combat `Character` isn't dict-like for `get_active_buffs`), so the amber buff chip is **not** shipped rather than rendered with no real producer — gated on a buff↔combat-push integration (TODO). *(Design fork, not assumed: a manual ground break-free action would be a small `combat.py` add — flagged, not built.)*
  - **Tests:** `tests/spa/test_m3_combat_chips.py` (jsdom render contract — biting vs pre-onset poison, restraint kinds + hold damage, the held-viewer note, **`buttons == 0` display-only guard**, null-for-nothing — plus producer/wiring/CSS static guards). The 27 existing field-kit `to_hud_dict` tests stay green (additive serialization).
- **Equipment-instance untangle (UI-4a prerequisite; Brian: "B, go").** The character `equipment` column had **three mutually-corrupting on-disk shapes** — flat key strings `{"weapon":"key"}`, a top-level single instance `{"key":…}` (weapon-only), and per-slot `ItemInstance` `{"weapon":{…},"armor":{…}}` — so `equip` clobbered worn armor, `unequip` wiped it, and the sheet read only the single-instance shape. **Canonicalized on per-slot ItemInstance** with one tolerant reader + one writer in `engine/items.py`: `read_equipment(raw)` → `{"weapon":ItemInstance|None,"armor":ItemInstance|None}` (accepts all three shapes + empty/list/None, exception-tolerant), `equipment_keys(raw)` (key-only drop-in for display sites), `write_equipment(weapon,armor)` (canonical, omits empty slots, round-trips through `read_equipment`). `parse_equipment_json`/`serialize_equipment` kept for back-compat.
  - **Readers unified (tolerant of every shape):** `engine/character.py::from_db_dict` (**fixes the reload bug** — the single-instance shape previously dropped the equipped weapon on reload), `engine/sheet_renderer.py` (×3), `engine/locks.py` (also fixes a latent `.lower()` crash on a per-slot dict), `server/session.py::_hud_equipped_weapon` (now resolves the display **name from the registry** — the old code read a `name` field `ItemInstance` never serialized, so the HUD weapon name was effectively always blank), `parser/builtin_commands.py::InventoryCommand`.
  - **Writers canonicalized + slot-preserving:** `equip` / `unequip` / `wear` / `remove armor` / `repair` (`builtin_commands.py`), weapon-experiment success + failure (`crafting_commands.py`), and the ship-vendor weapon buy (`space_commands.py`) all write the per-slot shape and **preserve the other slot** (equip no longer wipes armor; unequip keeps armor; wear keeps the weapon; etc.). **Fixed a pre-existing `new_credits` NameError** in `RepairCommand`'s success line (would crash every successful repair).
  - **Scope / known limitation (flagged, deferred):** the `Character` object still holds `equipped_weapon`/`worn_armor` as **bare key strings**, so `Character.to_dict()` can't carry instance condition/quality — but `to_dict()` is **not** an equipment-persistence path (every durable write goes through `save_character(equipment=…)`), so the DB JSON written by the commands remains the source of truth for instance data. A Character-object-holds-instances refactor (ripples through combat/sheet) is a **separate larger pass** — noted in TODO tech_debt.
  - **Tests:** `tests/test_equipment_untangle.py` (15) — cross-shape read normalization, key-only view, `write→read` round-trip + idempotence, slot preservation (incl. the unequip-keeps-armor pattern), and a **`Character.from_db_dict` reload round-trip** guarding the single-instance reload bug across all shapes.
- **UI-4a — Inventory panel (NEW modal; Brian's #1, built on the untangle).** A centered modal rendering a new `inventory_state` push: **equipped slots** (weapon/armor cards) on the left, **carried list** on the right, and a footer that **previews the stat delta** of equipping the selected carried item. Opened by the `inventory`/`inv`/`i` command (incl. a new **INV** quick-action button); WS-only push, Telnet keeps the text dump.
  - **Producer (extend, not add):** `engine/items.py::build_inventory_state(equipment_raw, carried, registry)` — equipped read via the untangle's `read_equipment`; **name/slot/value/stats resolved from the weapon registry by key** (`WeaponData.cost`→value, `damage`/`ranges`→weapon stats, `protection_*`/`dexterity_penalty`→armor stats, `weapon_type`→slot); condition/quality/crafter/experiment_count/quantity from the `ItemInstance` (equipped) or carried dict. `InventoryCommand` pushes it beside its text (mirrors the `sheet_data` pattern). Pure + registry-injectable → unit-testable.
  - **Client:** `static/spa/m3_inventory.js` (`window.M3Inventory`) — quality→5-pip gauge (50≈3), condition→3px green/amber/red bar, `[Modified ×N]`, crafter byline, stat chips; **delta footer** compares the selected carried item vs the equipped same-slot item by **D6 pips** (1D=3, mirroring `engine/dice.total_pips`) computed client-side from the dice strings (a relative base like `STR+1D` yields **no arrow**, never a misleading one). `client.html`: modal markup, `handleInventoryState`/open/close/backdrop, `stageFromInventory`, dispatch case, script tag, INV qa-btn, token-only `inv-*` CSS.
  - **Real verbs only / never auto-send:** staged commands branch by slot — weapon `equip <name>` / `unequip`; armor `wear <name>` / `remove armor`; any item `look <name>`. **`drop`/`give` do not exist at HEAD and are never offered** (the design's placeholder verbs were dropped). State-changing actions are **staged into the input**, not auto-sent.
  - **Honest omission:** **no container/weight bar** — there is no encumbrance model at HEAD, so the field isn't emitted rather than faked.
  - **Tests:** `tests/test_inventory_state.py` (6 — registry resolution, empty slots, carried quantity (`qty`→`quantity`), unknown-key fallback to dict name + `misc` slot, **no `container` key**, legacy-shape tolerance) and `tests/spa/test_m3_inventory.py` (3 jsdom — structure, the **exact real-verb command set with a `drop`/`give`-never guard**, pip-delta ▲ + non-comparable-range-no-arrow, `pipsOf` relative-base handling). `m3_inventory.js` added to `test_client_wireup_42a.py`'s expected load order.
- **UI-4b — Shop card (NEW modal; renders an EXISTING push — client-only).** `parser/shop_commands.py` already emits a `shop_state` message (modes `browse` + `dashboard`) for vendor-droid browsing/management, but the web `handleShopState` was an empty stub — so web players saw **nothing** when browsing/managing shops. UI-4b fills it with no engine change.
  - **Client:** `static/spa/m3_shop.js` (`window.M3Shop`) renders both modes into the shared `.inv-modal` chrome. **browse** = the room's vendor droids (a picker when >1, focus follows the server `focused_id` or client tap) → the focused droid's stock rows (slot/name/×qty/price/quality pips/crafter), each with a **BUY** action staging the real `buy <slot> from <shop name>` (the `buy` command routes `… from …` to `_handle_buy_from_droid`); staged, never auto-sent. **dashboard** = owner view: total escrow, per-droid escrow/placed/stock + recent sales (ts/item/+net/buyer) — **display-only** (stock/price/escrow management stays in the text `+shop` flow). `client.html`: `handleShopState` filled, shop modal markup (shares `.inv-modal`), open/close/backdrop, `stageFromShop`, script tag, token-only `shop-*` CSS. Haggling stays text.
  - **Flagged fork (NOT built):** the handoff sketched one `vendor_kind`-keyed shape folding in the **commissary**, but the commissary is a separate system (faction requisition, rank-gated stock, `+commissary buy <key>`, no in-room vendor — `engine/commissary.py`) with a different trigger/model than in-room player vendor droids. Merging needs a trigger + requisition-vs-marketplace reconciliation decision, so it's **flagged for Brian, not guessed** (logged in TODO; a future `mode:'vendor'` slots into the same `shop_state`, where `npc_refuses_buyback` + rank/rep gating would render).
  - **Tests:** `tests/spa/test_m3_shop.py` (3 jsdom — browse stock + focus switch + **the exact real `buy <slot> from <shop>` command with a drop/give-never guard**; dashboard escrow + sales display-only with **zero buy buttons**; empty-room note). `m3_shop.js` added to `test_client_wireup_42a.py`'s expected load order.
- **Protocol:** `web_client_vision_and_protocol_v1_4.md` pins `region_state`, the `combat_state` per-combatant condition fields, `inventory_state`, **and `shop_state`** (browse/dashboard) as public ABIs (buff field + `board_state`/`hud_update.objective` listed reserved; the commissary `vendor_kind` merge flagged as a deferred fork), with the running ledger for the remaining Webify messages.
- **Sandbox verification:** targeted `python3 -m pytest` on the changed modules + AST-validation of touched Python; jsdom available locally so the SPA harness runs rather than skips. (Brian runs the full ~7,700-test pytest on Windows — ground truth.)
- **Files:** `static/client.html`, `static/spa/m3_region.js` (new), `static/spa/m3_inventory.js` (new), `static/spa/m3_shop.js` (new), `static/spa/m3_combat_inspector.js`, `engine/territory_display.py`, `engine/combat.py`, `server/session.py`, `engine/items.py`, `engine/character.py`, `engine/sheet_renderer.py`, `engine/locks.py`, `parser/builtin_commands.py`, `parser/crafting_commands.py`, `parser/space_commands.py`, `tests/spa/test_m3_scroll_on_move.py` (new), `tests/spa/test_m3_region.py` (new), `tests/spa/test_m3_combat_chips.py` (new), `tests/spa/test_m3_inventory.py` (new), `tests/spa/test_m3_shop.py` (new), `tests/test_equipment_untangle.py` (new), `tests/test_inventory_state.py` (new), `tests/spa/test_client_wireup_42a.py`, `web_client_vision_and_protocol_v1_4.md` (new), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
