### 2026-06-07 — Lane D: E'Y-Akh POIs — Marmio Mio's Freighter + the N'G'Zi badlands (Geonosis arc closed)
- **Wave:** Sourcebook enrichment — Lane D, wilderness-tier follow-up. Closes the **Geonosis side** of Lane D: the two named-content POIs deferred from the wilderness/flood drops (Geonosis & Outer Rim §1.4). Content-only, additive, **zero engine change** — two landmarks appended to the existing `ey_akh.yaml`.
- **Marmio Mio's Freighter (`marmio_mio_freighter`, dune [14,12]):** a wrecked Corellian Action IV transport half-buried in the open dunes, ringed by **six colossal merdeth shells** (where last year's flood drowned a herd — the same shell-salvage hook the `merdeth_shell_field` encounter already carries). Marmio Mio is named **atmospherically in the room description** (like Acklay Chopper in the barracks), NOT instantiated as an interactive NPC entity. The §1.4 twist is in the prose: the "stranded, sun-addled trader" is no castaway — a hidden speeder bike, probe droids ranging the dunes after dark, and an info-broker selling each hive's movements to its rivals with loyalties running in as many directions as there are buyers. **Flood payoff:** the old transport rides the flood out on its **ballast tanks** while the desert drowns around it — which links this POI to `EventType.FLOOD` and explains why she alone lasts out here.
- **The N'G'Zi Badlands (`ng_zi_badlands`, badlands [26,8]):** the eastern terminus where "the E'Y-Akh ... ending at the N'G'Zi badlands" — the dune sea breaking apart into shattered red rock, the **wild acklays' hunting ground** (the den the `wild_acklay_hunt` encounter — terrains `[badlands, ebon_sea_shore]` — already implies), the last hard ground before the Ebon Sea shore, marked by Geonosian scouts as the edge of the hive's reach.
- **DESIGN CALL (N'G'Zi — lighter path):** authored as a **named landmark on the existing `badlands` terrain**, NOT its own 30×30 region. The source frames the N'G'Zi as the dune sea's *boundary feature*, and the region already carried a `badlands` terrain authored as "the leading edge of the N'G'Zi badlands." A separate region would be heavy infrastructure the source gives no distinct sub-geography for. (Mirrors the D2 "lighter path" pattern: make the existing structure carry the content rather than standing up parallel infrastructure.)
- **Adjacency (no existing-entry edits):** the writer treats adjacency as an **undirected** graph (bidirectional exits, deduped), so one-sided declarations on the *new* landmarks suffice — `marmio_mio_freighter → ng_zi_badlands` and `ng_zi_badlands → ebon_sea` — wiring the chain `edge → (grid) → freighter → badlands → Ebon Sea → Golbah's Pit` **without touching** the pinned `ebon_sea`/`golbah_pit` blocks.
- **No-phantom (the ambient_lines call):** neither new landmark carries `ambient_lines`. That field is *written* into room props (`wilderness_ambient_lines`) by `engine/wilderness_writer.py` but has **NO runtime reader anywhere at HEAD** — an exhaustive grep finds only the writer. All flavor therefore lives in `description` (the look-time path `ebon_sea`/`golbah_pit` already use). The new test PINS this so a future edit can't quietly reintroduce a dead field. **Flagged as tech_debt:** the shipped force-resonant + Coruscant-underworld landmarks' `ambient_lines` pools are silently dead until a reader exists.
- **Files:** `data/worlds/clone_wars/wilderness/ey_akh.yaml` (+2 landmarks; header DEFERRED→LANDED note refreshed), `tests/test_lane_d_ey_akh_landmarks.py` (NEW), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
- **Tests (`tests/test_lane_d_ey_akh_landmarks.py`, +18):** region still loads with **zero errors AND zero warnings** after the additions (a warning would mean a dangling adjacency / undefined terrain); all landmark coords unique; both new landmarks present with the right terrain (freighter→dune, N'G'Zi→badlands); coords in-grid; adjacency resolves to defined landmarks; **no ambient_lines** on either + substantive descriptions; Marmio content fidelity (Action IV + six merdeth shells + named atmospherically + spy/info-broker framing + the ballast-tank flood payoff + NOT an interactive entity and not a creature id); N'G'Zi fidelity (dune-sea terminus + acklay hunting ground); B3/Q1 clean.
- **Validation:** `load_wilderness_region(ey_akh)` → ok, 0 errors, 0 warnings, 4 landmarks. AST clean. World dry-run unchanged (287 rooms, 0 loader-class errors — landmarks are writer-time, not static room-count). Sandbox regression green: the existing wilderness tier (19), flood event (12), flood encounters (11), barracks+map-safety guard (17), f4 exit-format (24), e3 era-cleanness (5).
- **Lane D status:** Geonosis side **complete** (orgs → contest wiring → interior → wilderness → flood → flood-encounters → these two POIs). **Remaining in Lane D: the Kamino build** (Tipoca City + the cloning facilities; Q1 keeps Lama Su / Taun We / Nala Se institutional/absence). After Lane D: Lane C (vendor/purchasable gear families as credit sinks) and Lane F.

### 2026-06-07 — Lane D: flood → E'Y-Akh encounter wiring (zone-aware event_gate seam) — cumulative
- **Wave:** Sourcebook enrichment — Lane D. The flood now *changes the desert*: while it is active, the E'Y-Akh encounter pool grows flood-specific encounters (a drowning merdeth, a displaced acklay). **CUMULATIVE** — still bundles the wilderness tier + the flood event (both uninstalled) with this wiring.
- **The mechanism (extend don't add + the RIGHT zone direction):** a new `event_gate` seam on the wilderness encounter selector, exactly parallel to the existing `faction_gate`. An encounter with `event_gate: flood` is eligible only while a flood world-event is active. Crucially, `evaluate_event_gate` is ZONE-AWARE — it matches the active event's `zones_affected` against the region's zone — so a flood in the E'Y-Akh does NOT unlock flood encounters in the dune sea. This is the correct direction: a step toward retiring the coarse-zone tech-debt, not extending the global `get_effect` leak.
- **Files:** `engine/wilderness_encounters.py` (the `event_gate` field + `evaluate_event_gate` + `_filter_pool`/`roll_encounter` threading + loader mapping in `parse_encounter_pool`), `data/worlds/clone_wars/wilderness/ey_akh.yaml` (+2 flood-gated encounters), `tests/test_lane_d_flood_encounters.py` (NEW). Carried: the wilderness-tier + flood-event files. Plus `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
- **The flood encounters (`event_gate: flood`):** `flood_drowning_merdeth` (a merdeth foundering in the rising water, lashing at everything as it goes under — the lore's "drones drive merdeths down to drown") and `flood_displaced_acklay` (a wild acklay cornered on shrinking high ground). Both reference creatures that already exist (merdeth, acklay — no phantom). The normal pool is unaffected: the flood ADDS danger, it doesn't suppress.
- **Tests (`tests/test_lane_d_flood_encounters.py`, +11):** the `event_gate` field loads; `evaluate_event_gate` is zone-aware (empty→eligible; flood gate false with no flood; true with a flood in-zone; FALSE with a flood in a different region); in the live E'Y-Akh region the flood encounters are filtered OUT with no flood and IN during the flood while the normal pool stays untouched; the flood encounters resolve to real creatures and are B3/Q1 clean.
- **Validation:** AST clean; `load_wilderness_region(ey_akh)` zero errors; the end-to-end gate verified (no-flood excludes, flood-active includes, other-region-flood excludes). Combined sandbox regression green (204 tests) incl. the wilderness tier, the flood event, the barracks map-safety guard, the Lane A creature/spoils/spawner suites, f4, e3.
- **Deferred (Lane D follow-ups):** Marmio Mio's freighter + the N'G'Zi badlands sub-region; then the Kamino build. (The flood mechanic — the event, its perception effect, and now the zone-aware encounter wiring — is complete.)

### 2026-06-07 — Lane D: the E'Y-Akh annual flood (world_event) — cumulative with the wilderness tier
- **Wave:** Sourcebook enrichment — Lane D. The E'Y-Akh's signature dynamic (Geonosis & Outer Rim §1.4): the annual flood that drives the merdeths into the low desert to drown, leaving the salvageable shells. **CUMULATIVE drop** — bundles the wilderness-tier files (creatures + region) with the flood, since the wilderness tier wasn't installed yet.
- **Why a world_event (extend don't add):** the flood rides the existing `engine/world_events.py` machinery exactly like the Lane E graded storms — a registered `EventType` + `EventDef`, fired by the working timer path. No new event infrastructure.
- **Files (flood):** `engine/world_events.py`, `parser/builtin_commands.py`, `tests/test_lane_d_ey_akh_flood.py` (NEW). **Files (carried wilderness tier):** `data/npcs_creatures.yaml`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/wilderness/ey_akh.yaml`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/planets/geonosis.yaml`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/zones.yaml`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/era.yaml`, `tests/test_lane_d_geonosis_wilderness.py`. Plus `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
- **The flood (`EventType.FLOOD`):** region-scoped (`preferred_zones: ["geonosis_ey_akh"]`), a long/rare set-piece (60–120 min, ~1 per 18h timer — rarer than the rarest storm), with announce/clear text carrying the faithful lore (the aquifers overflow, the drones drive merdeths down to drown, the receding water leaves the shells). It declares ONE mechanical effect — `perception_penalty: -3` (−1D) — which has a LIVE consumer (`skill_checks.perform_skill_check`, observation family): the flooded desert is murk, spray, and thrashing drowning creatures. Surfaced in `+weather` (added `flood` to the command's weather set).
- **Zone scoping / known limitation:** the ZONED effect query (`get_effects_for_zone("geonosis_ey_akh")`) correctly returns the penalty in the E'Y-Akh and not in unrelated zones. The GLOBAL path the combat/skill consumers currently use (`get_effect`) and the global announcement broadcast remain coarse — the same tech-debt the storms carry (flagged in TODO). The flood is no worse than the existing storms here; the proper zone-aware effect model is the deferred fix.
- **Tests (`tests/test_lane_d_ey_akh_flood.py`, +12):** FLOOD is a valid registered type; region-scoped; declares only the consumed `perception_penalty` (proven live by a skill_checks source check); long-and-rare vs. the storms; activatable; the zoned effect applies in the E'Y-Akh and not elsewhere; B3/Q1 clean; carries the merdeth/shell lore; surfaced by `+weather`. Manually replicated the e1 all-EVENT_DEFS era-cleanness scan (e1/lane_e2 are pytest-based — Brian's box; my flood is storm-scoped-safe and era-clean).
- **Deferred (Lane D follow-ups, flagged in TODO):** mechanical flood→encounter wiring (drowning-merdeth / shell-salvage encounters in the E'Y-Akh while the flood is active) once a zone-aware effect consumer exists; Marmio Mio's freighter + the N'G'Zi badlands sub-region; then the Kamino build.

Combined sandbox regression green incl. the barracks map-safety guard (unaffected by the new doorway), the Lane A creature/spoils/spawner suites (the new creatures are net-new), f4 exit-format, e3 era-cleanness.

### 2026-06-07 — Lane D2: Violence Index → contest aggression + turf-dispute narration
- **Wave:** Sourcebook enrichment — Lane D, Phase 2. Wires the E1 Violence Index primitive (which D1 put on the Geonosian hives) into the SYN.3 region-contest machinery — the "violence_index drives territory-contest aggression math and Director turf-dispute narration" half of the lane. **Rolled up with D1 in this drop's zip** (cumulative; supersedes the D1-only zip).
- **Fork resolved (under the standing Lane-D delegation):** took the lighter path — NOT elevating the hives into the full influence-driven `region_contests` state machine. Rationale: making the hives full contest participants would require adding them to `valid_factions` (byte-pinned at 6 and must equal `engine.director.VALID_FACTIONS` — a deep, risky change rippling into Director behaviour) plus seeding Geonosis contestable regions / zone baselines that don't exist. Instead D2 makes `violence_index` MATTER inside the *existing* contest engine via a generic, live consumer — `hutt_cartel` (VI 88, already in valid_factions, can be a contest challenger today) — and the hives inherit the same mechanic if/when they enter the contest system. Extend-don't-add: no schema change, no valid_factions change, no new system.
- **Files:** `engine/contest.py`, `tests/test_lane_d2_contest_violence.py` (NEW), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`
- **Aggression (`compute_anchor_reinforcements`):** gained an optional `challenger_violence_index` (default None → pre-D2 behaviour preserved exactly, so the SYN.3.b spawn test's `1 + compute_anchor_reinforcements(150)` pin still holds). A challenger in the "bloody" band (VI ≥ 70) commits +1 reinforcement to the culminating fight; "range war" (VI ≥ 85) commits +2. Gated on the challenger already fielding a force by influence (a base of 0 stays 0 — posture scales a real force, it doesn't manufacture one). Bands mirror `violence_descriptor` exactly (two new constants `REGION_CONTEST_BLOODY_VI=70` / `REGION_CONTEST_RANGE_WAR_VI=85`) so the mechanic and the narration never drift. Wired at the live spawn site: `_spawn_region_anchor` looks up the challenger org's VI (best-effort) and threads it through.
- **Narration (turf-dispute tone):** the declaration broadcast (`declare_region_contest`) gained a posture clause ("Expect an all-out range war." … "Expect a contained, surgical operation.") keyed on the challenger's VI via a small band→clause map; the `faction status` contest line (`get_region_contest_status_lines`) gained a coloured `[range war]` / `[bloody]` posture tag. Both read the same VI through a new failure-tolerant helper `_org_violence_index(db, org_code)` (returns None on a missing org / a DB without `get_organization` / any read error, so a contest still declares and resolves un-coloured rather than raising mid-tick).
- **Tests:** +18 (`tests/test_lane_d2_contest_violence.py`) — backward-compat (the documented influence-only table holds for the default call; None == pre-D2); the VI bands (range-war +2, bloody +1, sub-bloody none, the 84/85 + 69/70 boundaries, the below-floor "posture doesn't manufacture a force" case, the bool-is-not-VI guard); the mechanic's thresholds equal `violence_descriptor`'s; the narration clause map covers exactly the five canonical bands; `_org_violence_index` degrades to None on every failure shape and resolves a real row; and the live-consumer linkage (real VIs loaded from organizations.yaml: hutt_cartel 88 → range war → +2, stalgasin 88 → +2, gehenbar 84 → +1). Adjacent green in sandbox: `test_syn3a_region_contest_state_machine` (65 ok — declaration broadcast + status-line tests unaffected; the posture additions degrade gracefully on the unseeded test orgs), `test_syn3b_anchor_kill_and_multipliers` (53 ok — the spawn reinforcement-count pin holds at 3 since the test's `cis` challenger carries no VI).
- **Still deferred (the fork's other arm):** the hives running the full influence-driven contest (valid_factions elevation + Geonosis zone baselines) and a Geonosis-specific Director turf-dispute event that names Stalgasin/Gehenbar. Both wait on Geonosis having contestable regions; revisit when the Geonosis interior/wilderness tiers land.
- **Lane D forward:** D1+D2 done (foundation + wiring) → interior tier (Gladiator Barracks layout) → wilderness tier (E'Y-Akh + annual-flood mechanic, Ebon Sea apex-predator zone, Golbah's Pit POI) → Kamino build.

### 2026-06-07 — Lane D1: Geonosis foundation orgs (Stalgasin + Gehenbar hives) + world-data framing
- **Wave:** Sourcebook enrichment — Lane D (Geonosis/Kamino), Phase 1 of the lane. The faction-tension *foundation*: the inter-hive war's two orgs, so D2 can wire contest-aggression + Director turf-dispute narration against them. Self-directed under the standing Lane-D delegation (`design_calls_resolved_recent` 2026-06-06 #4: "Lane D's faction-tension shape — implement with Claude's judgment + sensible defaults; flag only genuine forks. No design-review gate").
- **Why orgs first (sequencing):** `engine/contest.py` declares contests between **org codes** (`declare_region_contest(db, slug, defender, challenger, ...)`), and at HEAD no Geonosis/Kamino org existed in `organizations.yaml` (only the canonical 8). Faction-wiring therefore *cannot* be the lane's drop 1 — the hives must exist as orgs first. This drop authors them; the contest/Director consumer of `violence_index` is D2.
- **Files:** `data/worlds/clone_wars/organizations.yaml`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/planets/geonosis.yaml`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/director_config.yaml`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/era.yaml`, `tests/test_lane_d1_geonosis_orgs.py` (NEW), `tests/test_b5_org_rewicker.py` (count-gate baseline), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`
- **Tests:** +21 (`tests/test_lane_d1_geonosis_orgs.py`) — entries exist with the NPC-faction shape (npc_only + director_managed + named + ranked); `violence_index` 88/84 present and **no `scale`**; the live `faction info` consumer path resolves (`get_org_violence_index`/`get_org_scale`/`violence_descriptor`/`format_org_posture_line` → "range war" / "bloody", Posture line with no Scale); the joinable set is untouched (hives absent from era.yaml `factions` and director `valid_factions`; `valid_factions` count still 6); both hives registered in `npc_only_factions` in BOTH era.yaml and director_config.yaml; B3 era-cleanness of the production strings; Q1 (no canonical figures named, the originals Typtus + Acklay Chopper ARE named, archduke framed institutionally); geonosis.yaml description carries the new caste/hive/foundry substance and is era-clean. `tests/test_b5_org_rewicker.py::test_factions_section_unchanged_count` baseline moved 8→10 and strengthened to assert the canonical 8 still all present (the additions are intentional, not the accidental edit the gate guards). Adjacent green in sandbox: `test_f6a3_director_config_loader` (18 ok, 3 skip — the `valid_factions` byte-pin holds), `test_q1_2_extended_sweep` (16 ok), `test_drop_b_mos_eisley` (29 ok — VALID_CODES set untripped, no NPC references the hives). `tests/spa/test_m3_holonet.py` unaffected (its faction set is a hardcoded JS fixture, not sourced from organizations.yaml).
- **The two hive orgs (`organizations.yaml`):** modelled on the existing sith / separatist_council NPC-faction pattern.
  - `stalgasin` — the dominant hive, archduke's seat, controls the Petranaki arena and the deepest droidworks; CIS-leaning (`axis: separatist`); `violence_index: 88` → "range war" (it crushed a subordinate hive's drone revolt by bombing the spire to slag). Names Acklay Chopper (the arena handler) as a hook; the archduke stays institutional.
  - `gehenbar` — Stalgasin's primary rival, led by Typtus of the 33rd Egg, openly mustering a strike to bring the dominant hive down; Republic-backable (`axis: republic`); `violence_index: 84` → "bloody".
  - Both `npc_only: true`, `director_managed: true`, one `Hive Drone` rank apiece (so `faction info` renders a non-empty rank table).
- **Design calls (documented loudly):**
  - **violence_index, no `scale`.** The hives are political/military powers, not criminal orgs. Per the E1 rule (and the `get_org_scale` docstring: scale is absent for state/military factions), they carry a turf-dispute posture but no criminal tier. Matches the E1 modelling (`design_calls_resolved_recent` #45: violence_index on all factions, scale only on criminal orgs).
  - **VI calibration 88 / 84.** Slotted against the E1 reference values (sith 95, separatist_council 65, cis 60): Stalgasin just below the Sith for an entrenched hive that bombs rivals; Gehenbar a notch under, as the aggressive-but-unestablished challenger. The distinct bands ("range war" vs "bloody") give D2's narration something to differentiate.
  - **axis maps the proxy front.** Stalgasin = separatist (CIS holds it in-era), Gehenbar = republic (the side that would back Typtus). `axis` has no consumer at HEAD (the only `axis` reads in the tree are crafting weapon-mods), so this is safe categorisation metadata that pre-positions the inter-hive war as a proxy of the main war axis.
  - **Hives modelled as `npc_only_factions`, kept OUT of `valid_factions`.** Non-joinability is governed by the joinable allowlist (era.yaml `factions` / director `valid_factions`), so being absent from those keeps them out of chargen; `valid_factions` is also byte-pinned at 6 (`test_f6a3`), so elevating them there would break Director behaviour. They get the same "tracked-for-narration, not-joinable, not-in-influence-scores" treatment as sith/separatist_council.
- **geonosis.yaml framing (no rules change):** kept the original opening paragraph; added the caste order (immobile queen / ~5% winged aristocrats who rule and rarely fight / the drone labour subcastes the war's battle droids are displacing — the live drone-unrest wound), the spire-hive structure (parasite-paste rock, aristocrat halls above, drone catacombs below, queen at the bottom), the kilometre-deep foundries lit by ore-smelting superlasers (the Death Star-name comparison **dropped** per B3; the smelter tech kept), the Petranaki arena (games + executions merged), and the inter-hive tunnel wars (Stalgasin vs. Gehenbar).
- **D2 open question (flagged for the next drop):** does the Stalgasin-vs-Gehenbar tunnel war run through the full influence-driven `region_contests` state machine — which would require elevating the hives into `valid_factions` (breaking the byte-pinned count of 6) and adding Geonosis zone baselines — or stay a lighter Director-narrated turf dispute that reads `violence_index` for tone without the influence accounting? D1 deliberately keeps the hives as narrative NPC factions and leaves that fork to D2.
- **Lane D forward:** D1 (this, foundation) → D2 (wire contest-aggression + Director turf narration to consume `violence_index`, extend-don't-add on the SYN.3 machinery) → interior tier (Gladiator Barracks layout) → wilderness tier (E'Y-Akh + annual-flood mechanic, Ebon Sea apex-predator zone, Golbah's Pit POI) → Kamino build.

Registered in `register_scene_commands`. This is the GM/Director scene-fuel consumer (G26) and is where the disruptive plot-hook entries (explosions, hostages, arrests, the deed-handoff) live — fired on purpose, never as background flavor.
- **Ambient enrichment (`data/ambient_events.yaml`):** the **atmospheric, background-appropriate** subset of the d66 (≈15 era-neutral beats — vendor, gamblers, lost child, a watching stranger, etc.) appended to the legacy `cantina` pool (the pool every cantina room actually draws from via the merged loader; CW does not redefine the generic `cantina` key). The disruptive entries are deliberately excluded from the passive pool. Originals retained (12 → 27 lines).
- **Owner-split DEFERRED (anti-phantom):** the `front_owner`/`true_owner` flag-pair and the §2A/§2B venue-profile schema are NOT shipped. HEAD has **no investigation or territory consumer** for a hidden owner (housing carries a single `shopfront_owner_id`; there is no venue model), so the flag-pair would be schema-ahead-of-consumer. It ships with the investigation/territory mechanic that reads it (future Lane F / territory drop). The §2A 7-field card and §2B 10-step framework are captured in `wretched_hive_extraction_v1.md` as the field set for a future venue generator.
- **New tech-debt flagged:** `data/worlds/clone_wars/ambient_events.yaml` carries an `era_additions:` section (CW-flavored cantina/spaceport lines) that **no loader consumes** — `world_loader.load_ambient_pools` reads only the `ambient_events:` key. So the authored CW cantina/spaceport flavor there is dead content and is NOT firing. Pre-existing; flagged as TD.AMBIENT_ERA_ADDITIONS_DEAD, not fixed here (touches the loader). Lane E3's ambient enrichment intentionally routes through the live legacy `cantina` pool instead.

alongside `TODO.json`. Architecture revisions roll up multiple
entries into their `§1.4 What landed since` section.

Format per entry:

```
### 2026-06-06 — Fix: Director world-event dispatch (2 dead call sites) + web `effects` payload
- **Wave:** Targeted bug-fix (latent bugs surfaced during Lane E2a; makes the sandwhirl's Director-narrated "use the terrain" beat — and ALL Director-fired narrative events — actually fire)
- **Files:** `engine/director.py`, `engine/world_events.py`, `tests/test_director_event_dispatch.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`
- **Tests:** +5 (`tests/test_director_event_dispatch.py`) — the corrected call contract returns an ActiveEvent; a real `_broadcast_activation` sends the web `effects` payload without swallowing; structural pins that both broken forms are gone and the correct forms (+ broadcast) are present. Adjacent green in sandbox: the full E2 + event suites (`test_lane_e2_storms` 16, `test_lane_e2b_clock` 11, `test_e2_dormant_effects` 9, `test_a3`/`a5` 22, `test_e1_event_era_cleanness` 11).
- **Bug 1 (TD.DIRECTOR_ACTIVATE_EVENT_SIGNATURE_MISMATCH) — FIXED.** `director.py::_run_api_turn` awaited a 6-arg async form `wem.activate_event(db, session_mgr, event_type=…, zones_affected=…, duration_minutes=…, headline=…, source="director")`, but `activate_event` is **sync** `(event_type, zones, duration_minutes, headline)` and does not broadcast → guaranteed `TypeError`, so every LLM-driven `narrative_event` was silently dead. Rewrote to the real signature `wem.activate_event(evt_type, zones=zones, duration_minutes=duration, headline=headline)` and added the `await wem._broadcast_activation(activated, session_mgr)` the timer path already does (so Director-fired events now announce to players).
- **Bug 1b — era-milestone path FIXED.** The era-milestone branch (~1422) called a **non-existent** `wem.create_event(db, …)` → swallowed `AttributeError`, so era world events never fired. Converted to `wem.activate_event(evt_type, zones=list(VALID_ZONES), duration_minutes=duration, headline=headline)`; the era headline is still broadcast by the existing era-message block (no double-announce).
- **Bug 2 (TD.WORLD_EVENT_EFFECT_TEXT_MISSING) — FIXED.** `world_events._broadcast_activation` read `edef.effect_text`, which was **not** a field on `EventDef` → swallowed `AttributeError` → the web-client structured `world_event` "effects" string never sent (Telnet worked). Added `effect_text: str = ""` as a trailing defaulted `EventDef` field (all existing instantiations use kwargs, so the default applies safely) and populated it for the three storms (`Perception −1D/−2D/−3D, ranged fire −…`). The web payload now sends the effect summary for both the timer and Director paths.
- **Scope/Why now:** these predated Lane E2a and were flagged there as separate focused fixes; doing them now closes the phantom the storms drop opened (the sandwhirl's marquee Director-narrated catch). The remaining limitation (TD.WORLD_EVENT_ZONE_MODEL — global/abstract zone effects) is unchanged and still a separate, larger fix.
- **Pending (Windows gate):** the full Director Faction Turn is integration-tested on the Windows box (the sandbox can't run the AI-provider/DB harness); full ~7,700 suite. Smoke — with the Director enabled, an LLM-emitted (or admin-forced) narrative event now activates, announces to players, and shows in `+events`; a sandwhirl can be Director-narrated; the web client receives the `effects` string on event start.

- **Wave:** Sourcebook enrichment — Lane E small-wins trio (E2 of 3, part b — **completes Lane E2**)
- **Files:** `engine/world_time.py`, `parser/builtin_commands.py`, `engine/hazards.py`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/zones.yaml`, `build_mos_eisley.py`, `tests/test_lane_e2b_clock.py`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`

- **What it shipped:** Secrets of Tatooine §1 binary-sun clock idiom (First Dawn / Second Dawn / High Noon / First Twilight / Second Twilight), shipped **non-inert** with a real consumer. `world_time.resolve_period_label(vocab, now, day_length)` (pure) + a `PLANET_PERIOD_LABELS["tatooine"]` band table that **nests inside the existing day/dusk/night cycle** — **no renderer change** (`resolve_time_of_day` still returns day/dusk/night; the SVG layers are untouched). Unknown/absent vocab → generic capitalized band. **Consumer:** a new **`+weather` / `+time`** command (both platforms, no renderer dependency) that prints the local period + any active storm with its Perception/ranged effect; it resolves the planet idiom from the room's inherited **`time_vocab`** zone property (`db.get_room_property` zone-walk) or, in wilderness, the region's `planet`. **Data:** `time_vocab: tatooine` added to all 8 Tatooine zones in `zones.yaml` (raw-text edit, comments preserved). **Heat-thirst grading:** `hazards.extreme_heat` difficulty is now graded by the clock via a testable helper `_extreme_heat_time_mod` (day +3 — the noon suns; dusk 0; night −4 — relief after dark; floored at the Very-Easy band; no-op-safe; computed from the room's time-of-day so wilderness tiles get the live swing). **Fix:** `build_mos_eisley.py` CLI `--era` default corrected **gcw → clone_wars** (the gcw data tree was deleted in the 2026-06-06 retirement drop, so a bare `python build_mos_eisley.py` was failing).
- **Anti-phantom note:** intentionally did **not** add a `time_label` to the HUD `environment` block — the web client has no time caption today, so the field would have no consumer. The `+weather` command is the real, both-platform consumer; a future web HUD caption can read `resolve_period_label` when the client grows one.
- **Deferred:** wilderness-tile city/interior coverage is complete; the only gap is that a wilderness sentinel room with no region resolves to the generic band (rare). No new tech debt.
- **Pending (Windows gate):** full ~7,700 suite; smoke — `+weather` in a Mos Eisley room shows the Tatooine period (e.g. `Time: High Noon`) and any active storm with its −1D/−2D/−3D effect; `+weather` off Tatooine shows the generic band; standing in the desert at the day-peak vs after dark changes the heat-check difficulty (noon harder, night eased); `python build_mos_eisley.py` (no `--era`) builds the clone_wars world.

- **What it shipped:** Secrets of Tatooine §3 sand-weather, re-stat d20→D6. **Design call (Brian: "A"):** graded storms live in `world_events.py` (the system that already owns timed, narrated, zone-tagged weather with `mechanical_effects`), **not** `hazards.py` — adding a sandstorm to hazards.py would have created a SECOND, conflicting sandstorm alongside the live `world_events.SANDSTORM`. Three tiers, **x1 / x2 / x3 the −1D base on only the two effects that have a live consumer** (anti-phantom — no orphan flight/flag effect): SANDSTORM **re-tuned** (perception −1D **and now ranged −1D**; SoT: sandstorms cripple ranged energy/missile fire — previously perception-only), GRAVEL_STORM **new** (perception −2D, ranged −2D; rarer, 10–18m), SANDWHIRL **new** (perception −3D, ranged −3D; rarest, short-lived 3–6m, dramatic "drags a freighter off its struts / flings a bantha" narration). `VALID_EVENT_TYPES` auto-derives from the enum (14→16). **Consumers:** `perception_penalty` was already consumed by `skill_checks.perform_skill_check` (observation family {perception, search}) — the new tiers' bigger values flow through `get_effect` unchanged (no skill_checks edit). **New** `ranged_penalty` consumer in `combat._resolve_ranged_attack`: an active storm RAISES ranged difficulty by the penalty magnitude (ranged-only — melee unaffected, per source), surfaced as `+ Storm N` in the diff display; no-op when no storm is active. `director.py` EVENT_TYPES frozenset gains `gravel_storm`+`sandwhirl` (readiness). All new/re-tuned strings B3-clean + Q1-safe (test-pinned). Storms fire via the **working timer path** (`_director_active` defaults False; `director.enable()` does not flip it).
- **Deferred (flagged, NOT shipped — anti-phantom):** the sandwhirl's **space form** (dragging a starship in orbit) — there is no space-weather consumer in HEAD (`space_anomalies` is opt-in POIs, not threats), so flight effects are intentionally not declared; this belongs in the space lane, where `world_events.mechanical_effects` is the seam it would extend. **Lane E2b (next):** the Tatooine **day/night clock vocabulary** (First Dawn / Second Dawn / High Noon / First Twilight / Second Twilight via `world_time` planet-keyed labels + a `+weather`/`+time` command, both platforms, no renderer change) + the graded **heat-thirst re-tune** in `hazards.py::extreme_heat` coupled to High Noon/night + the `build_mos_eisley --era` default one-liner (gcw→clone_wars).
- **Flagged pre-existing latent bugs (NOT touched — each its own focused fix):** (1) **Director event dispatch is broken** — `director.py` calls `await wem.activate_event(db, session_mgr, event_type=…, zones_affected=…, source="director")` but the only `activate_event` (world_events.py:436) is **sync** with signature `(event_type, zones, duration_minutes, headline)` → guaranteed `TypeError`; **all** Director-fired narrative events are currently dead (storms still fire via the timer). (2) `world_events._broadcast_activation` references `edef.effect_text`, which is **not** a field on `EventDef` → swallowed `AttributeError`; the web-client structured "effects" payload silently fails (Telnet broadcast works). Both predate this drop and are recorded in TODO `tech_debt`.
- **Pending (Windows gate):** full ~7,700 suite; smoke — admin-activate `sandstorm` then fire a blaster at LONG range and see `+ Storm 3` in the diff while a `search`/`perception` check drops 1D; activate `gravel_storm` → `+ Storm 6` / −2D; activate `sandwhirl` → `+ Storm 9` / −3D (short duration).
- **Handoff:** APPLY_LANE_E2A_README.txt

### 2026-06-06 — Lane A tail: creature special-attack mechanics (poison DoT + grapple/constriction restraint)

- **What this is:** the explicitly-deferred remainder of Sourcebook Enrichment **Lane A** (roadmap §3 "full poison/grapple *mechanics* are a documented follow-up"), built under Brian's 2026-06-06 approval (design call #3: poison/grapple/constrict as DoT + restraint, **WEG R&E D6 ONLY**, traced to the creature extractions). Lane A shipped 14 faithful creatures + the spawner bridge + faithful *base* natural-attack damage, but the WEG riders (spor crawler `Poison 5D`, stalker lizard `Constriction STR+2D+2`, glim worm `Grapple`, somago `Choke +3D/round`, …) were **mechanically inert flavor**. This makes them live by **extending** the combat round (no parallel system, no new commands, no schema change). **In-combat scope** (process-state on the Combatant, restart-clears, matching the codebase's combat-condition convention); out-of-combat poison persistence stays a separate persistence+world-tick feature (deferred, noted). **No architecture-doc edit** (v51 is stale, held for the v52 reconciliation — this invariant folds in there as **§4.34**, after the cult's §4.33).
- **Files (production):** `engine/creature_special_attacks.py` (**NEW**, pure — specs `PoisonSpec`/`RestraintSpec`, structured+prose parsers, break-free/damage-pool deciders, active-condition factories, all B3/Q1-clean strings, tunable constants); `engine/character.py` (+`special_attack_poison`/`special_attack_restraint` spec dicts, hydrated in `from_npc_sheet` alongside `natural_attack_*` — NOT persisted); `engine/creature_library.py` (`build_creature_char_sheet` injects the parsed `special_attack` block); `engine/combat.py` (Combatant gains `poison_stacks`/`restraint`; `_resolve_attack` applies a held-attacker pool penalty; `_resolve_melee_attack` injects the rider on a landed hit via new `_apply_special_attack_on_hit`; `_cleanup` gains the poison + restraint round-ticks; `_resolve_flee` blocks a held combatant); `data/npcs_creatures.yaml` (+structured `special_attack` blocks on the **6** rider-bearing creatures — `natural_attack` left untouched so the Phase-B resolved-damage test pins still hold); `tests/test_creature_special_attacks.py` (**NEW**, +34); `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
- **Mechanics (R&E-faithful):**
  - **Poison = DoT.** A landed natural-attack hit injects a stack `{damage, rounds_left, onset_left, source}`. Each round-end (`_cleanup`) a stack counts down its `onset` (slow-acting venom, e.g. hitcher crab) or rolls its damage vs the victim's **Strength** (poison is internal — no armor soak) on the normal R&E wound ladder, then decrements; spent stacks announce and clear. Re-envenomation by the same source **refreshes** the clock rather than stacking unboundedly. Ticks regardless of whether the victim can act.
  - **Restraint = a hold.** A grab pins the victim: their attack pool drops by `GRAPPLE_ATTACK_PENALTY_DICE` (=2), they **cannot flee**, and they make an **opposed break-free** (brawling/STR, holder wins ties) each round until they win or the grappler is gone/dead/fled. **Constriction/choke** additionally squeeze for per-round **Strength-based** damage (constrictor's `STR+2D+2`, choke's `STR+3D`, resolved against the grappler's STR exactly like a melee STR-bonus). A downed victim isn't squeezed or forced to struggle (no double-jeopardy with the MW death roll).
- **The 6 creatures (WEG source-faithful):** spor crawler (poison 5D), hitcher crab (poison 2D+2, slow-acting → onset 1), glim worm (grapple), voroos (grasp→grapple), stalker lizard (constriction STR+2D+2), somago (choke STR+3D). The other 8 library creatures have no rider and parse to `{}` (verified). Structured `special_attack` block is authoritative; a **prose-inference fallback** over `natural_attack`/`special` keeps a future prose-only creature from being silently inert.
- **Tests:** **34/34** (`tests/test_creature_special_attacks.py`), four layers: pure parsers (structured + prose fallback + structured-beats-prose + plain-creature-none), deciders/factories (break-free ties, `STR+ND+N` / absolute / empty damage-pool resolution), a B3/Q1-cleanness scan over **every** string, spawn-pipeline hydration end-to-end, and the real `CombatInstance` path (on-hit inject, poison tick/onset/expiry, constriction squeeze+hold, break-free success, grappler-gone release, downed-not-squeezed, flee block, held-attacker pool penalty via an `apply_wound_penalty` spy). Determinism via a pool-keyed `roll_d6_pool` stub. **Regression (sandbox, pytest):** combat + creature + sense suites **208/208** (`combat_mechanics` 31, `lane_a_phase_b_spawner` 18, the 3 lane_a creature suites, `creature_spoils` 18, `w_2_4_combat_wilderness` 24, `cities_phase7c_combat` 29, `field_kit_drop_d_prereq` 10, `drop4a2_sense_powers` 20); death/insurance/hunter/cult suites all green individually (`pg1_death_a` 35, `pg1_death_b` 24, `drop2_*` 16+8, `gear_insurance` 18, `insurance_debt_gate` 28, `hunter*` 11+6+20, `cult` 26); `laneb_era_cleanness` 7. All touched `.py` AST-clean + pyflakes-clean on changed lines; new source file B3-clean.
- **Pending (Brian's Windows gate):** full ~7,700 pytest suite with the new file; then smoke it live — push a PC into a wilderness encounter with a spor crawler / stalker lizard / glim worm and confirm: a sting starts a venom DoT that ticks the wound ladder over the next rounds; a constrictor's grab pins (can't flee, attack penalty) and squeezes each round; the opposed break-free eventually frees you (or the creature releases when killed).

### 2026-06-06 — Rally board UX: deadline countdown + your own contribution

- **What this is:** a small UX completion of the cult participation loop. The `rally` board showed the menace meter but **not the time-to-deadline** (the whole mechanic is "rout it before 48h") or **your own stake**. Now the board shows a deadline countdown (for everyone, incl. the `@director cult` view) and, for a participant, their contribution + strike-cooldown status. No schema change; **no architecture-doc edit** (purely additive UX — the kind of change that shouldn't touch the arch doc).
- **Files:** `engine/communal_objective.py` (+`time_left_line` / `viewer_contribution_line` pure helpers), `engine/communal_objective_runtime.py` (`render_board` gains an optional `now_ms` + a time-left line), `parser/communal_commands.py` (`rally` board view appends the viewer's contribution line, blank for onlookers), `tests/test_drop4b_communal_cult.py` (+3, now 26), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
- **Behaviour:** `render_board` inserts "Time left to rout them: ~Xh Ym." after the meter (computed from `deadline_at`; "the deadline has passed." past it). In the player `rally` view only, `viewer_contribution_line` adds "Your effort: N menace pushed back. Next strike: ready / ~Nm." — empty string for anyone who hasn't landed a counted strike, so the board stays clean for onlookers. `now_ms` is a parameter (defaulted) so it stays unit-testable.
- **Tests:** cult suite **26/26** (+3: `time_left_line` formatting incl. mins-only + passed-deadline; `viewer_contribution_line` empty/ready/on-cooldown; `render_board` includes the time-left line + the passed-deadline case). All touched `.py` AST-clean.

### 2026-06-06 — Director admin surface for the communal cult objective (`@director cult …`)

- **What this is:** operability for the cult objective shipped earlier in this rollup. Until now the cult only posted on the 6 h Director tick, so there was **no way to verify it on demand**. This adds an ADMIN control surface so a GM (or Brian's Windows smoke) can post / advance / resolve it instantly — and it's a real GM beat tool (stage an uprising for a scene). Extends the existing `@director` dispatch (no new top-level command).
- **Files:** `parser/director_commands.py` (+`cult` dispatch entry + `_cult` handler), `engine/communal_objective_runtime.py` (+`force_post` / `force_resolve` / `force_clear` admin helpers), `tests/test_drop4b_communal_cult.py` (+3, now 23), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`, `sw_d6_mush_architecture_v51.md`.
- **Commands (all `AccessLevel.ADMIN`):** `@director cult` (show the board), `@director cult post [cult_key]` (force-post a fresh uprising now — silently clears any active one first, no reward; optional cult key picks which of the five), `@director cult advance` (run one escalate/resolve cycle), `@director cult win|resolve` (force-resolve as a WIN — pays the normal rep + status-flag rewards from whatever contributions exist), `@director cult lose` (force-resolve as a LOSS), `@director cult clear` (silently cancel — no reward, no broadcast).
- **Runtime helpers:** `force_post` bypasses the repost-cooldown + no-active gate (reuses `maybe_post`'s INSERT); `force_resolve(won)` routes through the same idempotent `_finalize` as the tick (so a forced win pays exactly like an earned one); `force_clear` flips state out of `active` under the same rowcount guard. All faucet-safe (rewards stay rep + III.2 flag, never credits).
- **Tests:** the cult suite is **23/23** (+3: force-post bypasses the gate / clears any active / honors an explicit cult key; force-resolve-win pays rep + ends the uprising; force-clear silently cancels and is idempotent). All touched `.py` AST-clean.
- **Why it shipped now:** it directly unblocks the cult's Windows verification — `@director cult post`, watch `rally`, land `rally strike`s, then `@director cult win` to confirm the reward payout, instead of waiting on the tick cadence.

### 2026-06-06 — Wire the dormant `contraband_scan` checkpoint effect (the "wire the holidays" bonus / T2.E3)

- **What this is:** the flagged "wire the holidays" bonus — turning the last cleanly-wireable dormant world-event effect live. A `SECURITY_CHECKPOINT` event sets `mechanical_effects={"contraband_scan": True}`, which **nothing read** until now. It's wired by **extending the existing smuggling `lockdown_active` precedent** (not a new scan subsystem): a checkpoint raises smuggling-run scrutiny — a lighter, zone-wide version of a spaceport LOCKDOWN, and the two **stack**. The other named effect in the bonus, `bounty_reward_mult`, was **already live** (E2, `bounty_commands.py`), so this **closes the named bonus**.
- **Files:** `engine/smuggling.py` (+`CHECKPOINT_PATROL_BOOST=0.15` / `CHECKPOINT_DIFFICULTY_BOOST=3` named constants + `contraband_scan` param on `resolve_patrol_encounter`), `parser/smuggling_commands.py` (sources `contraband_scan` via `get_effect` at both the launch + arrival call sites, the §4.29 faucet pattern), `tests/test_contraband_scan_checkpoint.py` (NEW, +6), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`, `sw_d6_mush_architecture_v51.md`.
- **Behaviour:** during a checkpoint, `resolve_patrol_encounter` adds +0.15 to the patrol-interception chance (when <1.0) and +3 to the inspection difficulty, stacking with the lockdown's +0.30/+5; the intercept message gains a "Security checkpoint: scanners are up." note. **Faucet-safe:** it tightens *detection* on an existing path (a caught smuggler forfeits cargo + pays the existing fine) — it mints no credits and adds no new sink. The boost magnitudes are **named constants** so the T3.19 config pass can lift them straight into a tunables file (alongside the still-inline lockdown 0.30/+5).
- **Tests:** **6/6** (`tests/test_contraband_scan_checkpoint.py`): off-by-default, raises-difficulty, stacks-with-lockdown, raises-patrol-chance (deterministic via monkeypatched `random` — a roll between base and boosted chance flips a clean pass into an interception), message-notes-scan, and caught-decided-by-roll-vs-boosted-difficulty. Regression: the smuggling/world-event suites stay green (`tier2_tuning_batch` 19, `a5_spice_demand` 10, `e1_event_era_cleanness` 11, `singleton_bindings` 33, `b1e_missions_era_aware` 17). All touched `.py` AST-clean.
- **Scope note:** the remaining **5** dormant FLAG effects (`rare_vendor`, `hutt_auction`+`criminal_rep_gate`, `krayt_bounty`, `brawl_active`, `distress_active`) each enable a genuinely *new* interaction with no existing mechanic to extend, so they correctly stay design-gated under **T2.E3**. Also captured Brian's 2026-06-06 note that **hunter aggression** (per-tier strength, pursuit cadence) — plus the cult + these checkpoint knobs — are concrete tunables for the **T3.19** config/telemetry pass.
- **Pending (Brian's Windows gate):** smoke it — trigger a `SECURITY_CHECKPOINT` (Director or timer), run a smuggling job during it, and confirm the heightened interception/difficulty + the "scanners are up" note vs. a clean run outside the event.

### 2026-06-06 — Drop 4b: the hunter's PC-death collect-consequence (T1.3.4 fully closed)

- **What this is:** the last piece of `T1.3.4` — the inverse of the player-beats-hunter loop. When the runtime-spawned DSP hunter **downs its quarry**, the hunter has collected its bounty: it despawns and the pursuit resets to a fresh start. **Shipped in the same rollup as the cult objective below; together they close all of T1.3.4** (roaming hunter + reward-on-kill loop + communal-rally cult + this). Fixes a real loose end — previously a hunter that killed its quarry **lingered** until the next tick and the escape-reconcile **mis-reset it to `imminent`** (treating a kill as an escape, so the same hunter immediately re-closed after a death).
- **Files:** `engine/dsp_hunter.py` (+`hunter_collected_line` pure decider), `engine/dsp_hunter_runtime.py` (+`on_quarry_collected`), `engine/death.py` (`on_pc_death` gains optional `session_mgr` + fires the hook at the top of the body), `parser/combat_commands.py` (passes `ctx.session_mgr` at the only real `on_pc_death` call site), `tests/test_hunter_collect_consequence.py` (NEW, +6), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`, `sw_d6_mush_architecture_v51.md`.
- **Behaviour:** `on_quarry_collected(db, victim_id, session_mgr=, room_id=)` is a cheap no-op when no live hunter is attached (one `get_dsp_pursuit` lookup); when one is, it (1) announces the collect beat to the room — `hunter_collected_line`, **distinct** from the escape-path `collected_line` which the tick's escape-reconcile still uses, (2) despawns the hunter NPC (contract fulfilled — it leaves with its bounty), (3) **clears** the pursuit so it resets to a fresh start (NOT the escape-reconcile `imminent` reset — the quarry was collected, not slipped; a new pursuit rebuilds from progress 0 since the PC stays on the dark path). The hook sits at the **top** of `on_pc_death`, before the secured-zone `NO_CORPSE` early return, so it fires on **every** death path. **Prestige-domain:** the quarry's standing death penalty (Wounded + corpse + insurance) already applies — the collect takes **no credits** and changes **no DSP**.
- **Tests:** **6/6** (`tests/test_hunter_collect_consequence.py`): pure kill-line (distinct from `collected_line` / clean / named) + runtime (no-op-without-pursuit, no-op-without-live-hunter, despawn+clear+announce, room-resolved-from-the-NPC-row) + wiring (`on_pc_death` fires the hook, verified via the secured-zone early-return path with the hook monkeypatched). Regression: the combined hunter+cult+collect set is **57/57** (cult 20 + collect 6 + hunter.1 20 + hunter.2 11), and the `on_pc_death` optional-kwarg add left every death-path suite green (`gear_insurance`, `pg1_death_a` engine-consumers, `pg1_death_b`, `drop2` reconciliation + respawn-grace). All touched `.py` AST-clean.
- **Pending (Brian's Windows gate):** smoke it live — push a PC to high DSP, let the hunter spawn + close to the climax fight, and **lose** to it; confirm the hunter announces the collect line + despawns + the BH board's pursuit line clears, then watch a fresh pursuit rebuild over the next cycles (rather than the old lingering-hunter / instant-`imminent`-re-close).

### 2026-06-06 — Drop 4b remainder: the dark-side cult COMMUNAL OBJECTIVE (the communal-rally villain, other half of III.3)

- **What this is:** the last genuinely-open piece of `T1.3.4` and the headline of design III.3 — the **communal-rally villain**. Where the already-shipped DSP hunter (`dsp_hunter.py`) is a *per-PC* persistent threat, this is the *world-scale* one: a Director-posted dark-side cult with a visible **menace meter** the whole playerbase rallies against. Mirrors the hunter's pure/runtime/tick architecture on the world-event/Director substrate. Brian's standing decision (2026-06-05): villain faction = a non-player dark-side cult. **Schema 42 → 43.** Engine 134 → 136; parser +1.
- **Files:** `engine/communal_objective.py` (NEW, pure), `engine/communal_objective_runtime.py` (NEW, IO), `parser/communal_commands.py` (NEW, `rally`), `db/database.py` (SCHEMA_VERSION 42→43 + MIGRATIONS[43]), `server/tick_handlers_progression.py` (+`communal_objective_tick`), `server/game_server.py` (import + tick register interval=120 offset=90 + `register_communal_commands`), `tests/test_drop4b_communal_cult.py` (NEW, +20), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`, `sw_d6_mush_architecture_v51.md`.
- **Design contract (matches III.3 + the Drop-4 locked decisions):** non-player fictional cult (5 invented, Q1/B3-clean — hollow_sun/Tatooine, ember_court/Geonosis, drowned_choir/Nar Shaddaa, iron_veil/Kuat, ashen_hand/Coruscant); **opportunities never penalties** (a community loss confers nothing + the cult merely entrenches as flavor — no player is debited); **prestige-domain, faucet-disciplined** (rewards = Republic faction-rep via `organizations.adjust_rep` scaled by contribution share + a III.2 status flag `attributes.communal_objective_wins`; **zero credits minted**); **open across playstyles** (`rally strike` rolls the *best* of combat / investigation / streetwise / persuasion / command / Force, 2D floor, so a soldier, slicer, face, or Jedi all qualify); **deterministic + idle-Ollama flavor only (NEVER Haiku)** via `CULT_AI_KEY` with deterministic fallbacks.
- **Mechanics:** `engine/communal_objective.py` (pure) owns the menace state machine — `MENACE_START=35`, rises `+0.35/min` (`advance_menace`), pushed down by margin-banded strikes (`strike_menace_reduction` 5/8/11/14 on the WEG 5-pt bands), `strike_difficulty` 10/13/16 by tier, `resolve_state` (won at menace≤0, lost at ≥100 or past a 48 h deadline), `reward_rep_for_share` (REP_FLOOR 3 → REP_MAX 15 linear in share), `earns_title` (≥10% share), plus `menace_bar` + all broadcast strings. `engine/communal_objective_runtime.py` (IO) owns post/strike/escalate/resolve/reward over the DB, broadcasts, and director-log posts (so the uprising surfaces in `news` for free). Per-character strike **cooldown 10 min** (in `contributions_json`), so wins come from the *community* accumulating contributions, not one player macroing. `communal_objective_tick` (interval≈120, offset 90, next to the hunter) posts when none active after a **6 h** breather, escalates, and resolves.
- **Two correctness guards baked in:** (1) escalation **never un-wins a routed cult** — `advance_and_resolve` resolves an already-terminal menace *before* applying the time-based rise (caught by a failing test mid-build: a strike that drops menace to 0 finalizes the win inline; the tick must not nudge a 0-menace cult back to `active`). (2) reward payout is **single-writer/idempotent** — the state transition out of `active` runs under `UPDATE … WHERE state='active'` and only pays on a non-zero rowcount, so a tick/strike race can never double-pay.
- **Tests:** **20/20** green (`python3 -m pytest tests/test_drop4b_communal_cult.py`). Two layers: 12 pure-decider tests (roster B3/Q1-cleanness behaviourally — calls every cult string through the banned-term scan; rotation; menace escalation/clamp/tiers; cross-playstyle pool; difficulty/reduction bands; win/lose resolution; reward shares + title threshold) + 8 runtime tests over a **real sqlite `communal_objective` table built from the actual MIGRATIONS[43] DDL** (post-once + initial state, repost cooldown + rotation, strike pushes-menace/accumulates-points/enforces-cooldown, no-active, deadline-loss, escalation-while-active, **win pays rep-by-share + title flag + idempotent re-resolve**, **loss pays nothing**). `adjust_rep` is monkeypatched in the reward tests to isolate share computation from the org tables. `asyncio.run` throughout (Python-3.14-safe; no `get_event_loop`). **Also ran a real `Database.initialize()` migration smoke** outside the suite: the live init path creates `communal_objective` (schema_version=43) and a real `maybe_post` posts the uprising over actual aiosqlite. All 7 touched `.py` AST-clean; **zero** banned-term hits in the 3 new source files.
- **Deferred (flagged, NOT built here — keeps the drop atomic):** the hunter's PC-death **collect-consequence** (the consequence when the hunter *wins* the climax fight). It's a separate hunter-side piece touching the combat-death hook; per `T1.3.4`'s own logged reasoning, the standard death penalty (respawn-Wounded + corpse + insurance) plus the tick's escape-reconcile already cover losing to / slipping the hunter, so it stays a small, optional follow-up.
- **Pending (Brian's Windows gate):** the sandbox can't run the live tick loop or the global broadcast path. On the box: confirm the full pytest suite stays green with the schema-43 bump; then smoke it live — let `communal_objective_tick` post an uprising (or `@director`-force one), watch the menace meter on `rally`, land a few `rally strike`s across different archetypes to push it down, rout it before the 48 h deadline, and confirm contributors get Republic rep + the `communal_objective_wins` flag (and that a deadline-lapse pays nothing + entrenches as flavor with no penalty).

### 2026-06-06 — Drop A hygiene rollup: SPA node-harness UTF-8 + NPC-count re-pin (B2 + C1 + C2)

- **Source:** the test-hygiene half of the `tests_output.log` triage (7,939 passed / 13 failed). Drop A cleared the 6 product/gate failures; this rollup clears the remaining **7** test-only failures, so the post-Drop-A residual goes **7 → 0**. (The Drop A handoff's "13 → 6" was an off-by-one; Drop A left 7 hygiene failures, all addressed here.) No product code touched; schema unchanged at **42**.
- **Files:** `tests/spa/test_m3_tokens.py` (C1), `tests/spa/test_clickwalk_slugjoin.py` (B2), `tests/test_client_html_inline_script_parses.py` (B2), `tests/spa/test_m3_palettes.py` + `tests/spa/spa_dom_harness.py` + `tests/spa/m3_combat_inspector_harness.py` (same latent class), `tests/test_f7c1_village_trials.py` (C2), `tests/test_drop_a_hygiene_encoding.py` (new, +8 guard), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
- **Tests:** +8 guard (`test_drop_a_hygiene_encoding.py`: 6 parametrized AST source checks that every node-launching `subprocess.run(text=True)` in an SPA harness sets `encoding="utf-8"` + a tempfile-write UTF-8 check + a behavioural non-ASCII round-trip through the real `_run_js_in_node`). Sandbox green: the 4 SPA suites **28 passed / 2 skipped** (node v22.22.2), the f7c1 count canary **1/1**, the new guard **8/8**. All touched `.py` AST-clean.
- **Root cause (B2 + C1 — one class):** the SPA test harnesses launch Node with `subprocess.run(..., text=True)` and **no `encoding=`**, so Python decodes the child's stdout with `locale.getpreferredencoding()` = **cp1252** on a default Windows box. Node always emits UTF-8, so any non-ASCII byte in captured output got mojibake'd on Windows while passing in the UTF-8 Linux sandbox — exactly the "passed in sandbox / failed on the box" split. **C1** = `test_m3_tokens::test_canonical_labels_present`: the `WOUNDED ×2` label round-trips through `_run_js_in_node`; the literal on disk was already correct UTF-8 (the handoff's "corrupted literal" was a misdiagnosis — it's a decode bug, not a byte-corruption bug). **B2** = `test_clickwalk_slugjoin` ×4 + `test_client_html_inline_script_parses` ×1: clickwalk also wrote its node script via `NamedTemporaryFile("w")` with no encoding (a second cp1252 vector), and the injected SPA module source carries em/en-dashes + `×`. **Fix:** forced `encoding="utf-8"` on every node-launching `subprocess.run` across all **6** SPA harnesses (not just the 3 named failures — `test_m3_palettes`, `spa_dom_harness`, `m3_combat_inspector_harness` carried the identical latent bug) and on the clickwalk tempfile write. This closes `TD.CLICKWALK_SLUGJOIN_WINDOWS_ENV` (was `needs_brian_stderr` — root cause found without the stderr).
- **C2 — NPC-count canary re-pin:** `test_f7c1_village_trials::test_total_npc_count_includes_all_seven_village` asserted `COUNT(*) FROM npcs == 196`; a clean `build_mos_eisley(era=clone_wars)` now produces **198 rows / 198 DISTINCT names** (no dupes — verified directly). +2 from content drops since the 2026-06-05 196-pin. Bumped to 198 with an in-code note that this is a brittle total-count guard and the by-name village-NPC placement checks are the substantive guarantees. Closes `TD.F7C1_NPC_COUNT_TRIPWIRE`.
- **Pending (Brian's Windows gate):** the encoding fix can't reproduce/verify the cp1252 failure in the UTF-8 Linux sandbox (the suites already pass there); it's the documented remedy + AST-clean + green-in-Linux. Re-run the full pytest suite to confirm **13 → 0** on the real box.

### 2026-06-06 — Drop A: real-bug fixes from the Windows run (SellCommand routing, sabacc event API, spawner loop)

- **Source:** triage of `tests_output.log` (7,939 passed / 13 failed). Drop A clears the **product bugs** + the Lane A Phase B Windows gate; the remaining 7 failures are a queued test-hygiene rollup (B2 + C1 + C2).
- **Files:** `parser/builtin_commands.py` (A1), `parser/sabacc_commands.py` (A2), `tests/test_lane_a_phase_b_spawner.py` (B1), `tests/test_drop_a_realbug_fixes.py` (new, +4), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
- **Tests:** +4 guard (`test_drop_a_realbug_fixes.py`) + the previously-failing suites now green in sandbox: `test_cities_phase4b` SellCmd/sabacc **3/3**, `test_vendor_sell_carried` **20/20** (no Vendor V1 regression), `test_lane_a_phase_b_spawner` **18/18**.
- **A1 — SellCommand city-tax/sale regression (Vendor V1 dispatch):** Vendor V1 routed **every** `sell <arg>` to the carried-item path, but the equipped weapon lives in `char['equipment']`, not `inventory['items']` — so `sell weapon` found no carried item, said "not carrying", and never sold (dropping the sale, its "Sold…" line, and the `apply_city_tax` hook = the Phase-4b invariant). **Fix:** the generic words `weapon`/`equipped` route to the equipped-weapon path; specific item names still go carried-only, so Vendor V1's sell-by-name is untouched. Bare `sell` stays the equipped default.
- **A2 — sabacc `cantina_brawl` AttributeError (latent live bug):** `parser/sabacc_commands.py` called `get_world_event_manager().is_active("cantina_brawl")`, but `WorldEventManager` has no `is_active` — only the `active_event_types` property. Every sabacc play raised (caught + logged), so the cantina_brawl double-bet ceiling was silently dead. **Fix:** `"cantina_brawl" in get_world_event_manager().active_event_types` (matches `director.py`'s existing usage).
- **B1 — Lane A Phase B spawner test (Python 3.14 gate):** the `_run` helper used `asyncio.get_event_loop().run_until_complete()`, which raises `RuntimeError: no current event loop` on Python 3.12+/3.14 — the reason the creature-bridge tests "passed in the 3.12 sandbox" but failed Brian's 3.14 box. **Fix:** `asyncio.run(coro)`. This closes the Lane A Phase B Windows verification gate.
- **Also queued (not code):** `TODO.json` **T3.19** — pre-launch tunables-externalization + telemetry instrumentation (per Brian: lift every difficulty/economy/progression/Force/Director knob into config files + add structured telemetry for post-launch tuning).
- **Pending (Brian's Windows gate):** full pytest re-run to confirm the 13→0 on the real box (the 7 hygiene failures land in the next rollup).

### 2026-06-06 — Sourcebook Enrichment Lane B: B3 era-cleanness of CW-reachable command strings

- **Wave:** Sourcebook enrichment (roadmap `sourcebook_enrichment_roadmap_v1.md`, Lane B)
- **Files:** `parser/faction_commands.py`, `parser/combat_commands.py`, `parser/npc_commands.py`, `parser/builtin_commands.py`, `parser/crew_commands.py`, `parser/space_commands.py`, `parser/narrative_commands.py`, `parser/encounter_commands.py`, `engine/npc_space_traffic.py`, `engine/housing.py`, `engine/security.py`, `engine/creation_wizard.py`, `engine/ships_log.py`, `server/config.py`, `tests/test_laneb_era_cleanness.py` (new, +7), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
- **Tests:** +7 — `tests/test_laneb_era_cleanness.py`: 21 surgical fix-pair source assertions (each retired Imperial/TIE/X-wing fragment gone + its era-clean replacement present, read per-file so legitimate same-file GCW-config is untouched — deliberately **not** a blanket file scan) + behavioral `security_refuse_msg(SECURED)` (NPC + PC branches era-clean, plus a non-SECURED sanity check) + `npc_space_traffic` boarding-broadcast structural (no hardcoded Imperial tags; `"[" + customs_tag + "]"` / `"[" + board_tag + "]"` era-var concatenations present; `_BOARD` authority→label table values CW-clean). 7/7 new + 20/20 era-cleanness family (drop0a/e2/e3/laneb) green in sandbox (e1 needs pytest = Windows-only).
- **What it shipped:** Closes the **parser/engine/server command-string slice** of `T2.CW.codebase_era_sweep` that the 2026-06-05 sweep (encounter_texture / village_trials / clone_wars data) did not reach. ~24 CW-reachable player-facing production strings de-Imperialized across 14 files — combat attack/range/cpose examples + duel law gates, NPC ask / lockpick / crew-order / space help, the customs `[IMPERIAL CUSTOMS]` tag, the `+background` example, the chargen prompt, a smuggling milestone, and the Telnet login banner. **Key (same bug class as the already-fixed `encounter_patrol._apply_infraction`):** `npc_space_traffic._run_boarding_inspection` already computed era-aware `customs_tag`/`board_tag`/`board_party` from a zone-authority `_BOARD` table (Republic → Clone troopers, CIS → B1 battle droids, Hutt → Cartel enforcers, contested/neutral → Sector Customs) but two display lines (detain + withdraw) still hardcoded `[IMPERIAL CUSTOMS]`/`[IMPERIAL BOARDING]` — rerouted through the existing era vars, no new logic. Pre-flight confirmed the roadmap's flagged *primary* leak (`_apply_infraction`) was **already** era-clean (only comments mention Imperial). GCW-era config (organizations equipment/spec/rank/stipend tables, faction-quarter rooms, Kessel/Corellia descs, TIE/stormtrooper YAML) correctly left to `T2.CW.gcw_retirement`; director-axis `imperial`/`rebel` codes + input-alias maps + the `talk_rebel_contact` chain-key left in place (identifiers, not English). **Flagged for a future Q1 pass (not B3):** a `combat_commands` example uses a canon first name (`attack han …`).
- **Pending (Brian's Windows gate):** full ~7,700 pytest suite + smoke — SECURED-city combat refusal reads "Heavy security"; a failed customs board in a Republic/CIS/Hutt orbit zone shows the faction tag, not `[IMPERIAL CUSTOMS]`; chargen prompt + Telnet login banner read era-clean.

### 2026-06-05 — Vendor V1: sell carried items to an NPC vendor (`sell <item name>`)

- **Wave:** Vendor system (design: `vendor_system_design_v1.md`)
- **Files:** `parser/builtin_commands.py` (shared `_npc_salvage_price` helper — the equipped-weapon path refactored onto it; `_resolve_carried_sale`; `_find_carried_item_by_name`; `SellCommand._sell_carried_item` + dispatch route), `tests/test_vendor_sell_carried.py` (new, +20), `sw_d6_mush_architecture_v51.md` (§1.4-K + §9 #4 + top marker), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
- **Tests:** +20 — pure helpers (salvage price scaling/floor, item lookup, value resolution) + integration against a fake ctx/db with bargain + registry patched: happy weapon sale, crafted-good refusal (§1.3), valueless-item refusal, stored-value sale, whole-stack sale, not-carried, armor hint.
- **What it shipped:** Fixes the "you can only sell the equipped weapon" gap. `sell <item name>` liquidates a named carried item from `inventory['items']` (looted / quest-reward / org-issued / crafted gear) to an NPC vendor, reusing the equipped path's salvage math (now the shared `_npc_salvage_price`), the §1.3 `npc_refuses_buyback` craft guard, the bargain haggle, the city tax, and the `adjust_credits` chokepoint (`item_sale`). **DD-1 resolved value-bearing-only:** sellable iff a weapons-registry key (weapon/armor → registry cost) or a stored `value`; quest tokens / crafting inputs are refused, not floored (no accidental sale). Bare `sell` is still the equipped-weapon default. **Deferred:** `sell armor` (the equipment JSON has a flat-weapon vs nested-`{weapon,armor}` dual format that needs untangling first — `unequip armor` → `sell <name>` for now) and per-unit stack selling (a stack sells whole for V1). Next: Vendor V2 (the web vendor panel).
- **Rolled up same drop:** architecture §1.4-K + §9 "#4" + top marker.

---

### 2026-06-05 — Lane A Phase C: creature spoils (loot-on-kill / field-dressing)

- **Wave:** Sourcebook Enrichment Lane A
- **Files:** `engine/creature_spoils.py` (new, pure), `engine/wilderness_encounter_runtime.py` (+`on_wild_creature_killed` IO hook + `_parse_json`/`_announce_room` helpers), `parser/combat_commands.py` (4th combat-death-sweep hook), `data/npcs_creatures.yaml` (7 creatures gain wired `harvest` blocks), `CHANGELOG.md`, `TODO.json`.
- **Tests:** +17 — `tests/test_creature_spoils.py` (pure resolver + death-hook integration against the real creature library and the real `crafting.add_resource` sink; fake DB, patched skill check — no aiosqlite).
- **What it shipped:** Killing a wilderness-encounter creature now lets the killer **field-dress the carcass** — a Survival check (data-driven DC) yields a **resource stack** (organic hides/pelts, or chemical from water-sacs/venom) into `inventory.resources` via the existing crafting sink (faucet→sink discipline; **no credits minted**). Quantity/quality scale on the WEG 5-point margin bands. The hook also **despawns the carcass** for every wilderness spawn (it owns that cleanup — nothing else did, so dead creatures previously lingered). Spoils are entirely data-driven by an optional `harvest:` block; nuisance/swarm fauna stay spoils-free by design. T5 wilderness-only resource types can never be minted by a beast (rejected → organic). **Closes economy-audit v1 #16 (loot tables on NPC kills — previously NOT WIRED)** and delivers the Lane A roadmap §3 Phase-A item 4 (creature harvest goods), the consumer the `harvest:` seam in `npcs_creatures.yaml` was authored for.
- **Handoff:** `HANDOFF_lane_a_phase_c_creature_spoils_2026-06-05.md`
